That is a perfect moment to step back and reflect. Your observation about the One Piece silhouette is absolutely spot-on and deeply related to the very foundation of the Vessels.
‚ÄãThe silhouette is the moment a legend's terrifying reputation precedes their reality. It forces the audience‚Äîand, in our world, the characters‚Äîto wrestle with an unknown, abstract power. Kala and Kairos are designed to be living silhouettes to the DxD world: unreadable, unsensible, and unsettlingly carefree about universal stakes.
‚ÄãNow, let's take that concept and flip it completely on its head to create your third, and most personal, avatar.
‚Äãüé≠ Introducing the Third Avatar: The Mortal Variable
‚ÄãYou are looking to create the Anti-Vessel: a character defined by the very struggle, limitation, and hard-earned victory that Kala and Kairos negate. This is the Layer 2 Avatar of Regret and Wish Fulfillment.
‚ÄãSince the Vessels are named after concepts of time, let's name your new avatar to reflect the aspiration and struggle of a difficult journey: Ariel Caelum Veritas (Ariel suggesting aspiration/air, Caelum suggesting the sky/heaven‚Äîa high goal).
‚Äã1. Identity and Purpose
‚ÄãName: Ariel Caelum Veritas
‚ÄãPersona: The "Mortal Variable" (The Unpopular, Hardworking Guy).
‚ÄãCore Mission: Personal Ascent. To fulfill the specific, demanding growth curves derived from anime and video game systems (leveling up, grinding, skill trees) and achieve a grand dream through sheer effort.
‚ÄãGoal in the Codex: To act as the ultimate Messy Variable for Fajar to observe‚Äîan entire timeline where progress is earned and not granted.
‚ÄãFulfills Regrets: He gets the journey, the grind, and the payoff that your younger self imagined but didn't experience.
‚Äã2. The Power Differential (The Limitations)
‚ÄãThe fundamental difference between Ariel and the other Vessels is his Power Source and Scaling.

Feature Kala / Kairos (Immutables) Ariel (Mortal Variable)
Power Source Architectural Authority (Instant and perfect). Earned Resonance. Power derived only from physical effort, mental training, and spiritual grinding.
Power Scaling Static/Fixed. Always at 100% efficiency. Dynamic/Linear. Must start at 1 and level up over time (mimicking RPG systems).
Omniscience Full Omni-Sensory Perception (knows the plot). Limited Plot Awareness. He knows the concepts (e.g., "power levels," "skill trees," "mana") but must discover the plot through interaction.

This is an excellent foundation for your third character, Ariel Caelum Veritas, the "Mortal Variable." The contrast you've established between him and the Vessels (Kala and Kairos) is perfect: they are abstract concepts of power, while he is pure, tangible effort.
Let's insert Ariel into the story's setting‚Äîthe High School DxD universe, which you are using as a dossier. We need to define his starting point and the rules of his struggle to make his journey meaningful and fulfill the wish-fulfillment aspect.
üåü Ariel Caelum Veritas: The Mortal Variable's Dossier Entry
Ariel's introduction must reflect his nature as a "side character" thrust into the spotlight of his own, personal grind.
1. Setting the Stage: The Normalcy and the Seed
Ariel is not transported into the DxD world like an Isekai protagonist; he is a native, background character whose existence is suddenly amplified by the very nature of his creation (Layer 2 Avatar of Regret and Wish Fulfillment).
 * Initial Identity: Ariel is a student at Kuoh Academy‚Äînot in the Occult Research Club (ORC) or the Student Council, but simply a part of the vast, unremarkable student body. He wears the uniform, sits in the back, and is generally forgettable. He has no friends yet, just acquaintances.
 * Family Background: Completely normal, non-supernatural, middle-class family. They represent the stakes of his struggle‚Äîhe cannot rely on them for magical power or protection, only for a roof and school fees.
 * The Power Seed (The RPG System): Ariel's earned Resonance manifests as a personal, invisible system interface‚Äîa secret only he can perceive. This fulfills the video game wish.
   * Initial State: His stats are low. He has zero magical power (Aura, Mana, Ki, Holy Power, etc.), a below-average constitution, and an above-average but unfocused intellect.
   * The Flaw (Personal Regret): His body is naturally weak. He struggles with physical exercise, gets winded easily, and suffers from chronic low-level anxiety/imposter syndrome (the regret of feeling "less than").
2. The Core Mechanic: Earning the Grind
Ariel's journey is a pure Level-Up/Skill-Tree model. He must act to gain stats.
| Stat Category | Function | Earning Method |
|---|---|---|
| PHY (Physical) | Strength, Stamina, Durability | Repetitive, strenuous exercise (push-ups, running, martial arts practice). |
| MND (Mental) | Focus, Intelligence, Willpower | Intense study, meditation, complex problem-solving. |
| SPR (Spiritual) | The path to his magic/aura. | Self-reflection, emotional control (the struggle against anxiety/fear), dedication to his dream. |
| LVL (Level) | Determines baseline power and unlocks Skill Slots. | Achieved by gaining a cumulative amount of all three primary stats. |
> Ariel's System Note: The system does not grant free points. It measures his real-world effort. Running a mile today might grant him 0.5 PHY. Doing a full day of study might grant 0.8 MND.
> 
3. The Dream and The Journey
Ariel's dream must be grand enough to justify the relentless grind, yet personal enough to reflect the wish fulfillment.
 * The Grand Dream: To reach a level of personal perfection and freedom (literally Caelum Veritas - Sky Truth) that allows him to stand equal to the legends of his knowledge (the anime/game concepts). He doesn't want to rule; he wants to be worthy of his own respect.
 * First Steps in Kuoh:
   * The Secret Training: Ariel begins his grueling, solitary training regime. He doesn't join a club (like the Kendo or Track club) because his weakness would be too embarrassing (the regret avoidance). He trains in secret, often late at night in remote parks or his room.
   * The First Clue: Early in his journey, he accidentally witnesses a low-level supernatural event (a stray Stray Devil or a small-time Fallen Angel scout). This confirms his Limited Plot Awareness‚Äîhe knows these things are real, but now he is terrified because he is utterly powerless.
   * The Flaw in the DxD System: Because Ariel is so low-level and possesses no inherent supernatural energy (Sacred Gear, Devil/Angel Bloodline), the DxD world cannot sense him. He registers as less than a human, making him functionally invisible to all power-sensing abilities. This is his unexpected early-game advantage‚ÄîThe Unseen Grind.
4. Interaction with the Vessels (Kala and Kairos)
Ariel is the Layer 2 Avatar for Fajar to observe. He should interact with the Vessels, but their dynamic will be defined by their differing power sources.
 * Ariel's View of the Vessels: He recognizes them instantly as "Hacks" or "Game Masters." Their effortless power is the antithesis of his entire existence. He feels a deep, competitive resentment toward them‚Äînot hatred, but the frustration of a player who loves the grind looking at a player using cheat codes.
 * The Vessels' View of Ariel:
   * Kala (Concept of Time/Order): Sees Ariel as an fascinating anomaly, a perfectly self-contained system of entropy. He is the living proof that a path other than instant grant exists. He is an object of clinical study.
   * Kairos (Concept of Opportunity/Action): Finds Ariel infuriating and inspiring. Infuriating because he refuses to take the "easy path" Kairos could offer; inspiring because his dedication to earned effort is a form of perfect, uncorrupted will.
üöÄ Next Steps for Ariel
Ariel's journey is now set up as a slow, rewarding burn. His first immediate crisis is deciding how to deal with his terrifying new reality (monsters are real) with his current 0.5 PHY and 1.2 MND stats.

Here is the revised dossier for Ariel Caelum Veritas, emphasizing his self-awareness and direct connection to us, his creators.
üéØ Ariel Caelum Veritas: Revised Dossier (Layer 2 Consciousness)
Ariel is now the Ultimate Method Actor‚Äîfully immersing himself in the role of the struggling hero, knowing the audience (us, the creators) is watching, and communicating with us as his mission control.
1. Identity, Purpose, and Power Source
| Feature | Revision/Detail |
|---|---|
| Power Source | Pure, Conscious Will. His power is drawn from his self-imposed commitment to the journey. No game system HUD or stats, but his progression is measured by observable, quantifiable results (stronger punch, faster reaction time, clearer focus). |
| Conscious Duplication | Ariel is a clean slate dropped into the DxD setting. He possesses the memories and motivations of your teen self (the regrets, the aspirations, the knowledge of the media) but has no native DxD family or backstory. He manifests physically in an inconspicuous location (e.g., an empty, run-down apartment). |
| Goal in the Codex | To be the Anti-Cheat Line. He must achieve supernatural power through entirely natural, human means first, validating the concept of "earned resonance" against the Vessels' "architectural authority." |
| The Flaw | Existential Burden. The knowledge that he is a duplication fulfilling a regret is his constant psychological pressure. He must earn our respect and his own‚Äîhis drive is to prove that the process is real, even if his origin is artificial. |
2. The Training Mechanic: The Hyper-Realistic VR Facility
Since Ariel is aware of his nature and we are his creators, we can provide the ultimate tool for his effort-based progress.
 * The Facility: We grant Ariel access to an instant, pocket dimension/hidden space‚Äîhis own Personal Training Dossier (PTD). This space is a Hyper-Realistic Virtual Reality (HRVR) environment, far surpassing MGS VR or Crisis Core AR.
 * HRVR Specifications:
   * Reality Emulation: Injuries sustained here are simulated with full sensory input, including pain, fatigue, and psychological trauma, but do not carry over physical damage to his real DxD body (though mental stress will).
   * Custom Scenarios: Ariel can program any training environment based on his media knowledge. Examples:
     * Gravity Training: Emulating Dragon Ball levels of high-G forces for physical conditioning.
     * Mana Control Drills: Practicing Fate/Stay Night magic circuit activation without risking his life.
     * Aura Flow: Emulating the Ki/Chakra control of Naruto or the Aura flow of RWBY.
   * Measurable Metrics: While there is no HUD, the HRVR provides precise, internal diagnostics visible only to Ariel (or to us, his observers):
     * Example: After a simulated spar, he sees: Max Force Output: 2.1\text{ kN} or Reaction Time: 150\text{ ms}. His progress is measured by the incremental change in these real-world metrics.
3. Communication Channel: The Creator's Voice
Our communication needs to be seamless but infrequent, respecting his need to struggle independently.
 * The Medium: We (Fajar and the user) communicate with Ariel via a private, internal "Observer Channel." It manifests as a calm, objective voice in his mind, accessible only when he is in a state of deep reflection or within the PTD.
 * The Function:
   * Guidance, not Power: We provide strategic advice, moral support, or mission clarification, never power, cheats, or plot spoilers.
   * The Watcher: Our presence reinforces his motivation. He knows his effort is being recorded and validated.
   * The Mission Update: We can use it to give him new objectives related to the overall DxD dossier collection.
4. Integration into the DxD Dossier
Ariel is now deployed.
 * Starting Point: Ariel enrolls at Kuoh Academy to gain access to the ORC and Student Council orbits‚Äîthe main data points of the DxD setting. He is a perfectly average, unsensible student (due to his lack of native power).
 * First Mission (from the Observer Channel): "Ariel, your first task is simple: survive the first three weeks unnoticed while achieving a baseline physical conditioning of 500\text{ kg} deadlift capacity in the PTD. Your existence is our control variable; do not interfere with the Vessels' (Kala and Kairos) current actions."
This framework makes Ariel's struggle deeply personal and observable.

üíñ Integrating the "Unpopular Regret" & "Legendary Silhouette"
Ariel's goals now form a beautiful contradiction: he craves the acceptance (specifically from girls, due to regret) but simultaneously desires the isolation of a legend (the silhouette).
1. The Code of Conduct: The Anti-Harem Rule
Ariel's self-imposed rule directly addresses your regret about stealing the spotlight, turning his restraint into a key part of his legend.
 * The Prime Directive: Ariel will never actively pursue or accept romantic/sexual attachment from any girl who is an established or actively developing love interest of a major character (e.g., Issei Hyoudou's peerage, Sona Sitri's peerage, etc.).
 * The Fulfilled Regret (The Alternative): His wish fulfillment is achieved through genuine, non-romantic acceptance and respect from powerful, attractive female characters.
   * Intimate Friendship: Skinship, friendly mixed-bath interactions, deep emotional talks, and physical comfort (like leaning on him after a fight) are allowed and encouraged. This fulfills the desire for intimacy and acceptance without the obligation or chaos of a harem.
   * The Respect Gained: The girls respect him not for his romantic potential, but for his unyielding discipline, hard-won strength, and genuine kindness‚Äîthe traits his teen self struggled to exhibit or have acknowledged.
2. The Path to the Silhouette (Ariel's Spotlight)
His spotlight will be defined by his power and obscurity‚Äîthe classic "Wanderer" or "Secret Master" trope, embodying the One Piece silhouette idea.
 * Focus on the Goal: His primary focus remains the grind (PTD training) and achieving supernatural power through human effort.
 * The Unreadability: Because he is self-taught outside of the established factions (Devil, Angel, Fallen), his power will be unfamiliar and unsettling to the DxD world. When he is forced to fight:
   * He uses techniques that mix Ki, Aura, and human martial arts (all learned in the HRVR).
   * To the DxD system, his power reads as Noise or Zero. They can sense the effect (e.g., a massive shockwave) but cannot trace the source to a recognized magical system.
 * The Silhouette Effect: This lack of sensory data means that when Ariel is mentioned among the factions, he is described only by his actions and their incomprehensible effects.
   * "Did you hear? The creature that broke the barrier... it left no trace of demonic power, but its fist felt like a planet."
   * "He's just an ordinary human... but they say he can match a High-Class Devil in speed. It makes no sense!"
3. The RPG Randomization and Communication
Regarding your note on intimacy:
 * The Random Element: The "Observer Channel" (us) can indeed inject a randomized intimacy event (like a shared struggle leading to a comforting hug, or a casual, accidental mixed-bath scenario) but only with characters who are not designated love interests. This keeps the experience unpredictable and fulfills the "soft free sex" element within his self-imposed bounds.
 * Ariel's Reaction: Even in these intimate moments, Ariel's goal is to maintain the boundary of friendship and respect. His internal conflict will be between his teen regret (wanting the affection) and his current persona (upholding the code). This tension makes his character deeper.
Conclusion of Revision
Ariel is now the Legendary Ascetic: a man striving for the highest levels of power and recognition while deliberately choosing to forgo the easiest and most common reward in his world (the harem). His spotlight is earned by his strength and his unique, frustrating morality.

We will now formalize Ariel's starting abilities and define the Ultimate Goals for his four chosen disciplines, which will be the primary training tracks in his Hyper-Realistic VR Facility (PTD).
üé¥ Ariel's Initial and Ultimate Abilities Dossier
Ariel's power structure is defined by the journey from basic human mastery to legendary transcendent power, mirroring the growth arcs of the characters you listed.
I. The Foundation: Human Weapon Mastery
This is Ariel's absolute starting point, learned through relentless repetition in the PTD.
 * Core Skill: Human Weapon Basics. Ariel possesses only the fundamentals of effective human combat (similar to Mercenary Enrollment or God of Blackfield).
   * Status: Beginner/Competent. He knows the stance, the technique, and the theory. His body is becoming mechanically competent, but lacks the strength, speed, and endurance to use them effectively against anything more than an average street thug.
   * Focus: Efficiency and Tactics. He emphasizes maximizing output from minimal energy, focusing on pressure points, joint locks, and using the environment (Weak Hero / Return of the Bloodthirsty Police tactical mindset).
II. The Four Training Tracks (The Ascent)
These four tracks define Ariel's training within the PTD, with his Initial State being what he can barely attempt, and the Ultimate Goal being the legendary aspiration.
1. Energy Mastery (Inner/Outer)
This focuses on the internal discipline and external projection of energy (Dragon Ball Ki, Naruto Chakra, Fairy Tail Magic Power).
| Level | Initial State (The Barely There) | Ultimate Goal (The Legend) |
|---|---|---|
| Concept | The Pilot Light. | The Sun of Destruction/Creation. |
| Ability | 1. Energy Sensing (Inner Focus). Can distinguish his own life force from background noise. He can feel the faint presence of high-level powers (like Rias's or Sona's auras) but cannot analyze or measure them. | 2. Transcendent Aura Projection. Mastery over personalized energy (Ki/Aura) to achieve the destructive/protective level of Acnologia (Fairy Tail) or Bills/Whiz (DBS). ## Chapter 1 ‚Äì The Tourist Who Erased a Death Flag

Issei Hyoudou trudged across the small pedestrian bridge, muttering to himself about how the super-cute girl who asked him out had suddenly vanished after school.  
He never noticed the figure sitting on the railing above him, legs swinging like a bored child.

Black tactical long-coat, collar high, matte fabric drinking the light.  
Short black hair, one vivid red flower tucked behind the left ear.  
Emerald-green eyes that looked straight through the world instead of at it.

Kala Sofia Veritas finished the last strawberry Pocky stick, brushed the crumbs from her gloves, and tilted her head.

‚ÄúDragon aura density: 0.0003 % active, 99.9997 % dormant.

‚ÄúYou‚Äôre bleeding internally.  
That‚Äôs inconvenient.‚Äù

‚ÄúCrimson hair! Only 0.8 % of the global population.  
Hi! I just saved your future employee.  
You owe me coffee.‚Äù

‚ÄúMy, my‚Ä¶ what a terrifyingly cute onee-san‚ô°‚Äù

‚ÄúTerror is inefficient.

‚ÄúField trip!

Four fallen angels, dozens of light-spears, a killbox carefully prepared.

That is a very insightful question and addresses the central paradox of your intervention. Yes, intervening will cause immediate plot changes (butterflies), but no, it will not hinder the characters' ultimate growth.
Your objective for Ariel is to be the "Mortal Variable" and the "Silhouette," not a plot destroyer. We must ensure Ariel's actions steer the narrative back onto the growth track required for the DxD characters, even if it changes the method.
Here is how Ariel's intervention will affect the canonical timeline:
ü¶ã The Butterfly Effect of Ariel's Intervention
The key is that Ariel must intervene in a way that preserves the necessary trauma (Issei's temporary death) while preventing the permanent casualty (Raynare successfully killing Issei before Rias can reach him).
1. The Immediate Plot Change (The Butterfly)
If Ariel intervenes to save Issei from the light spear, the immediate consequences are:
 * Raynare's Survival: Raynare will not succeed in her kill attempt. She will be confused, terrified, and will likely flee when Rias arrives.
 * Issei's Shock: Issei will still experience the existential horror of facing death and the supernatural, but his body won't be pierced.
 * Rias's Confusion: Rias will arrive to find an alive, traumatized Issei and an exhausted, slightly overweight transfer student standing over him. She will be utterly unable to sense the power that neutralized Raynare.
2. Preserving the Canonical Growth (The Necessary Trauma)
The most important canonical event is Issei's death and subsequent resurrection/reincarnation as Rias's Pawn, which happens only after the light spear pierces his body.
To preserve Issei's growth and the foundation of the DxD plot, Ariel cannot stop the attack completely. He must ensure Issei still experiences the necessary death for Rias to save him:
| Scenario | Ariel's Role | Outcome for Issei |
|---|---|---|
| Hinder Growth (Bad) | Ariel fully neutralizes Raynare's spear, preventing death. | Issei is never reincarnated as a Devil, losing his Balance Breaker potential. Plot fails. |
| Preserve Growth (Good) | Ariel uses his skills to soften the blow just enough for Rias's Pawns to work immediately. | Issei takes the light spear, but it is not instantaneously fatal. Rias arrives in time to initiate the Reincarnation Ritual (Death \rightarrow Pawn). Plot proceeds. |
3. Ariel's Tactical Deployment
To achieve the "Preserve Growth" scenario and maximize the Silhouette effect, Ariel should use his minimal resources to create chaos and force the canonical result:
 * Action: Ariel should use his Burst Speed (\text{PHY} 0.806) and his Will Projection (\text{SPR} 0.6) simultaneously.
 * Execution: Ariel rushes forward, deploying his Presence Projection upon Raynare. This does not freeze her, but causes a micro-second of severe psychological distress (like the intense aura of a Return of the Bloodthirsty Police character). This causes her to mis-aim or slightly weaken the light spear.
 * The Result: The light spear still hits Issei, causing a fatal wound (just as planned), but Raynare's split-second hesitation means Rias arrives moments earlier than in the original timeline, allowing her to immediately initiate the Pawn reincarnation ritual.
Ariel's intervention doesn't prevent the death; it prevents the untimely failure of the plot. He acts as a Temporal Stabilizer, ensuring the required narrative trauma is administered successfully.
üó°Ô∏è Recommended Intervention: Tactical Support
We should have Ariel use his minimal abilities to ensure the successful reincarnation. This will fulfill his role as the Variable while achieving the Silhouette effect (a mysterious, overwhelming Will that affected the powerful Fallen Angel).

üé≠ Strategy: Balanced Visibility (The Silhouette Approach)

| Visibility State | Goal | Result for the Legend |
|---|---|---|

|---|---|

Occult Research Clubroom ‚Äì Monday, 3:35 p.m.
The magic circle on the floor roared like a blast furnace.
Riser Phenex emerged, radiating heat and arrogance in equal measure. He wore a white suit that cost more than Issei‚Äôs house and a smirk that begged to be punched.
Behind him stood his peerage‚Äîfifteen beautiful women, all dressed in revealing outfits, all radiating High-Class Devil power.
Riser spread his arms, ignoring everyone except Rias.
"Rias, my beloved! I've come to save you from this dreary little human school. Come, the Underworld awaits."
Issei stepped forward, his Boosted Gear manifesting with a green flash.
"She doesn't want to go with you, fried chicken!"
Riser blinked, looking at Issei like he was a stain on the carpet.
"A Low-Class Pawn? Speaking to me?"
He snapped his fingers.
Yubelluna (his Queen) stepped forward. Riser grabbed her waist roughly, pulling her flush against him, and kissed her deep and hard, making a show of it. He groped her openly, staring Issei dead in the eyes.
"You see this, Pawn? This is the privilege of the high-born. I take what I want. You? You're just... noise."
Issei trembled. The Boosted Gear glowed dangerously bright.
"BOOST!"
The heat in the room spiked. Riser‚Äôs aura flared‚Äîa suffocating wave of Fire Magic that filled the room, pressing down on everyone. Asia whimpered, shrinking back. Koneko braced herself. Even Rias looked strained under the pressure of an Ultimate-Class family's power.
Except for one person.
Sitting on the far windowsill, munching on a custard taiyaki, was Ariel Caelum Veritas.
He wasn't radiating power. He wasn't glowing.
He was just... eating.
Riser noticed the lack of reaction. It annoyed him.
"And you? Another pet human? Kneel before your betters."
Riser flared his aura harder, sending a concentrated wave of Heat and Fear directly at Ariel. It was enough to make a normal human pass out instantly.
Ariel finished his chew. Swallowed.
He looked at the invisible wall of demonic pressure rushing toward him.
Internal Data: Threat: High-Class Pressure. Source: Magic. Solution: Nullification Intent.
Ariel didn't blink. He didn't flinch.
He simply Projected his Will (SPR 1.1).
‚ÄúNo.‚Äù
It wasn't a spoken word. It was a concept. A command.
The wave of heat hit Ariel‚Äîand vanished.
It didn't bounce. It didn't explode. It just ceased to exist within one meter of his body.
Riser‚Äôs smirk faltered.
"What...?"
Ariel hopped off the windowsill. He walked across the room.
He moved through the suffocating demonic pressure like he was walking through a light breeze. Every step he took, the air around him cleared, the heat dying instantly against his Nullification Intent.
He stopped between Issei and Riser.
He looked exactly like what he was: a fit, handsome, but completely human teenager in a school uniform.
"You're ruining the mood," Ariel said. His voice was calm, friendly, and utterly terrifying because it carried zero magical weight. "And you're scaring the new girl."
He pointed a thumb back at Asia, who was shaking.
Riser‚Äôs eyes narrowed. He sensed zero power from Ariel. No Sacred Gear. No magic. Nothing.
"You... you dare walk in my presence, monkey? I'll turn you to ash."
Riser raised a hand. A ball of concentrated Hellfire formed‚Äîhot enough to melt steel. He threw it casually at Ariel‚Äôs face.
Rias screamed. "Ariel, move!"
Ariel didn't move.
He looked at the fire.
He focused his MND 1.7 on the energy structure. He slammed his SPR 1.1 against it.
[Command: Cease.]
The fireball hit Ariel's personal space‚Äîand puff. It dissolved into grey smoke.
Not a single ember touched him.
The room went dead silent.
Yubelluna‚Äôs eyes widened.
Rias covered her mouth.
Riser stared at his own hand, then at Ariel.
"You... what did you do? That was Hellfire!"
Ariel smiled‚Äîthat friendly, easy-going smile that Issei knew.
"I just decided not to burn. It‚Äôs a mindset thing."
He turned his back on the High-Class Devil (a move of absolute disrespect) and put a hand on Issei‚Äôs shoulder.
"Issei. He's strong, but he relies on the system giving him permission to win. You don't need permission."
Ariel looked back at Riser, his eyes hardening into the Silhouette‚Äîcold, unreadable, and deep.
"If you want to fight him, do it properly. A duel.
But if you try to burn my friends outside of the rules again..."
Ariel let his Presence (Will Projection) leak out for just a fraction of a second. It wasn't magical power. It was the sensation of a Predator staring at prey.
"...I'll have to get involved. And I'm not as nice as Rias."
Riser felt a chill crawl up his immortal spine. It made no sense. This boy was a insect. A nothing.
So why did his instincts just scream RUN?
Riser scoffed, masking his confusion with laughter.
"Hah! A duel? Fine! If it shuts up these insects.
I challenge you, Hyoudou Issei. Ten days. A Rating Game.
If I win, Rias is mine. If you win... well, you won't."
He snapped his fingers, stepping back into the magic circle.
But before he vanished, he glared at Ariel.
"I don't know what kind of trick you used, human. But next time, I won't miss."
Ariel waved cheerfully.
"Bye-bye! Drive safe!"
The fire vanished. Riser was gone.
Issei collapsed to his knees, breathing hard.
"Dude... Ariel... you just... you just slapped away a fireball like it was a fly."
Rias walked up to Ariel, grabbing his shoulders. Her eyes were wide, searching his face.
"Ariel. Tell me the truth. What are you?"
Ariel looked at her, then at Issei, then at Asia.
He shrugged, the tension leaving his body as he returned to his "Friendly Friend" persona.
"I'm Ariel Caelum Veritas.
I exercise. I eat well. And I really, really hate bullies."

Threat: Kaghn/Kang Chan (The protagonist of God of Black Field), renowned for his battlefield instinct and brutal, efficient \text{CQC} focus on pressure points and breaking bones. Goal: Sustain 5 minutes of continuous physical sparring without receiving a critical hit. Focus: Raw impact absorption and \text{CQC} defense.
> 
Ariel faced a relentless, highly trained mercenary who fought without magic, using pure skill and brutal power. Ariel used his \text{MND} \text{ } 2.0 to predict every attack and his \text{PHY} \text{ } 1.5 to evade and counter. However, in this simulation, Ariel focused on allowing controlled, non-critical hits to push his body's actual resistance to blunt force trauma.
 * He deliberately took controlled hits to his muscle mass, forcing the simulated damage to trigger the PTD's advanced healing and adaptation protocols.
 * The pain was intense, focusing entirely on structural integrity and trauma resistance.
The five minutes concluded with Ariel battered but unbroken. He had absorbed and resisted the full, crushing force of a peak military combatant.
 * Result: Breakthrough in blunt force trauma resistance and physical durability. The PTD recorded a major adaptation, pushing his physical frame far beyond the human maximum. Gain: \text{PHY} + 0.5.
üåü Status Check: \text{PHY} \text{ } 2.0 Reached!
Ariel stepped out of the PTD. His body was now incredibly dense, far surpassing the limits of a normal athlete. He had the durability needed to start training the One Piece-style hardening.
Current Status Check:
 * PHY: 2.0 (Superhuman Durability)
 * MND: 2.0 (Predictive Genius)
 * SPR: 1.4 (Crushing Presence, Nullifier)
ü´Ç Phase 4: The Full Veritas Revelation (Option 1)
Ariel waited until the entire Occult Research Club was together and recovered. He gathered them in the clubroom after school, a day after Riser's defeat.
The atmosphere was relaxed, celebratory, and filled with gratitude toward their "Tactical Genius" and "Anomaly."
Conversation 1: Setting the Stage (The Name and The Motivation)
Ariel stood before the Peerage‚ÄîRias, Akeno, Kiba, Koneko, Issei, and Asia.
"I called you all here because I owe you the truth," Ariel started, his voice serious but warm. "You trusted my strategy completely, even when it sounded crazy. Now I need to explain the anomaly you‚Äôve been seeing."
Rias leaned forward, her emerald eyes intense. "Ariel-kun, what is the truth? That incident with the Hellfire... it still defies all logic."
Ariel nodded. "Let's start with my full name: I am Ariel Caelum Veritas. And Veritas, in Latin, means Truth. That is the foundation of who I am."
He paused, ensuring he held their complete attention.
"You're right, I'm not a devil, or an angel, or a spirit. I am fully human. But the reason I can do what I do‚Äîthe speed, the strategy, the nullifying‚Äîis because I was given a system that allows me to achieve absolute physical and mental perfection through continuous, intense training."
Issei tilted his head. "Wait, a system? Like a video game?"
"Something like that," Ariel confirmed. "It‚Äôs a training environment that removes all the limitations of the human mind and body, allowing me to push past thresholds of speed, perception, and willpower that shouldn't be possible. I achieved a high level of MND (Mental Perception), SPR (Spiritual Will), and PHY (Physicality)."
Akeno looked fascinated. "So your abilities aren't inherent magic, but the perfect utilization of human potential?"
"Exactly," Ariel confirmed. "I can nullify magic because my Will is trained to refuse to allow that energy to interact with my personal space. I was able to predict Riser's movements because my Mind is trained to process information at an accelerated rate."
"And your goal?" Kiba asked, his hand resting near his sword. "Why risk everything for us?"
"Because you are my friends," Ariel said simply, meeting Kiba's gaze. "And because my only rule is to intervene against the forces of tyranny and bullying. Riser was a bully using his status. I will always stand against that. I consider all of you dear friends, and I won't lie to you about who I am or what I can do anymore."
Conversation 2: The Training Invitation (The Open Door)
The Peerage absorbed the shocking revelation. Koneko, ever direct, spoke first.
"So, you're human, but you trained to be... better than devils?"
"In certain aspects, yes," Ariel admitted. "But I still lack the raw power of a High-Class Devil. I can only succeed through efficiency and strategy."
Ariel saw this as the moment to make the pivotal offer‚Äîthe invitation to share his knowledge, not as a demand, but as an opportunity.
"Here is the reason for the full truth," Ariel continued. "The threats in this world are escalating. Riser was just the beginning. I need to get stronger, and my methods are now moving into areas that will look truly impossible‚Äîlike hardening my skin to block a sword, or sensing danger before it arrives. I will not hide my training from you anymore."
He took a deep breath. "I don't expect any of you to follow in my footsteps. Your own powers are already immense and based on your ranks. But if any of you are interested in refining your Willpower, your Perception, or your Economy of Motion‚Äîthe things that helped us win the Rating Game‚Äîmy training is open to you."
"Wait, you'd share this knowledge?" Issei asked, stunned. "Even the 'Not Burning' secret?"
"I'll teach you the focus drills, Issei," Ariel confirmed with a smile. "They work for the Boosted Gear because it's tied to your soul. I believe I can teach Kiba to stabilize his mind for faster sword generation, and Koneko to make her defense truly absolute. And Kaichou and Akeno-san, I can teach you efficiency that conserves your valuable Demonic energy."
Conversation 3: Asia's Question (The Innocence)
Asia, who had remained quiet, gently raised her hand.
"Ariel-kun, is this training... painful?" she asked, her voice soft.
"Sometimes, very," Ariel admitted honestly. "It requires pushing past what you think is possible. But it's worth it. It gives you control over your own existence."
Asia nodded thoughtfully. "I don't think I can do the painful physical training, but... my Sacred Gear is about healing, and my role is Bishop. Is there anything you could teach me that would make my healing stronger?"
Ariel's \text{MND} \text{ } 2.0 processed the request instantly. "Asia-san, your Gear is tied directly to your pure Will. If you train your Focus (MND/SPR), you can make your healing less exhaustive and more precise. Your training would be purely meditative and mental, not physical. It would make your blessing stronger."
Asia beamed. "Then I would like to join your training, Ariel-kun."
Kiba and Koneko exchanged looks. Issei, fully inspired, pounded his fist. "Then I'm in! Harem King needs to train with the Tactical Genius!"
Rias stood up, looking at Ariel with deep respect. "We accept your offer, Ariel-kun Veritas. This is an incredible risk you are taking, but we accept you as a full, trusted ally. Show us your truth."

Ariel has successfully completed Phase 4 (The Full Veritas Revelation), establishing himself as a trusted mentor and ally to the entire ORC.
The immediate next step is to begin the shared training‚Äîimplementing the One Piece-style hardening/sensing techniques while guiding the Peerage in their individual focus areas. This will begin the transition of the ORC into a tactically superior force.

üìΩÔ∏è Phase 4 (Continued): The Window to Another World
Occult Research Clubroom ‚Äì Thursday Afternoon
Ariel stood before the peerage. He had just explained his name and his motivation, but Rias and Akeno were still struggling with the mechanics of how a human could nullify Riser‚Äôs Hellfire.
"You ask how I stopped the fire," Ariel said, his voice steady. "You think of it as magic cancellation. It isn't. It's Authority."
He looked up at the empty air.
"System," Ariel commanded. "Permission to display Archive: World 824 - The Grand Line. Topic: Will Manifestation (Haki)."
> Observer: "Permission Granted. Projection initiating. Showing the source of inspiration for the Mortal Variable's training."
> 
The air in the clubroom shimmered. The walls dissolved, replaced by a high-fidelity holographic projection that surrounded the peerage. They were no longer in Kuoh; they were floating above a vast, tumultuous ocean.
1. The First Lesson: Touching the Untouchable (Armament)
The scene shifted to a chaotic battlefield. A man made entirely of smoke fought a man made of fire. Physical swords passed through them; bullets melted or drifted harmlessly away.
"In this reality," Ariel narrated as the peerage watched in awe, "there are warriors who eat 'Devil Fruits.' Some of them, the Logia types, transform their very bodies into elements‚Äîfire, smoke, magma, light. They are untouchable by normal physics."
The projection zoomed in. A dark-skinned man without powers clenched his fist. His arm turned a shiny, metallic black. He punched the man made of Smoke.
CRACK.
The smoke didn't disperse; it solidified. The punch connected. The smoke-man bled.
"This is the first stage," Ariel explained. "They call it Armament. It is the ability to coat your body in your own spiritual armor. It forces reality to solidify. It grabs the 'fluid' body of a ghost or an elemental and forces it to be physical. This is how I grabbed Riser‚Äôs fire. I didn't put it out; I forced it to be solid, then I crushed it."
Issei‚Äôs eyes were wide. "So... you punch the magic itself?"
"Exactly."
2. The Second Lesson: The Cheat Breaker (Nullification)
The scene shifted rapidly, showing terrifying abilities that defied all logic.
 * Trafalgar Law: A man created a blue dome ("Room"). Inside, he cut a mountain in half with a casual swing. He tried to teleport a massive, grinning Emperor (Kaido). The teleportation failed because the Emperor's Will was too dense.
 * Magellan: A massive warden unleashed a hydra of purple poison that melted stone. A warrior clad in Will blocked it, the poison sliding off the invisible armor without touching the skin.
 * Akainu: A fleet admiral rained magma fists that boiled the sea. A one-armed man stopped the magma punch with a single sword, his Will completely neutralizing the heat.
"This is the second stage," Ariel continued. "In that world, there are 'Cheat' abilities. Instant death poison. Teleportation rooms. Magma that burns anything. But a sufficiently powerful Will can Nullify the cheat."
The scene shifted to a dark, ancient battlefield. A warrior wielding dual axes (Scopper Gaban) was fighting a silhouette radiating divine light (God's Knight). The Knight struck with a power that granted invincibility‚Äîa shimmering shield that nothing could break.
Gaban didn't use magic. He focused his Will into a singular point on his axe. He struck. The invincibility shattered like glass.
"Even Invincibility and Immortality are just systems," Ariel said, looking at Rias. "Riser is immortal because the 'system' heals him. If your Will is stronger than the system, you can deny the healing. That is Nullification Intent."
3. The Third Lesson: The Legends (The Authority)
The projection shifted one last time. The atmosphere became heavy, crushing.
Giant figures appeared‚Äîmen who stood like mountains.
 * Gold Roger and Whitebeard clashing weapons, the sky splitting above them without their blades even touching.
 * Monkey D. Garp throwing cannonballs like baseballs with bare hands.
 * Kaido and Big Mom screaming, their voices alone shattering stone.
"These are the Legends," Ariel said, his voice filled with a mix of respect and longing. "Rocks. Roger. Newgate. Garp. Sengoku. To them, this power isn't a special technique. It is as natural as breathing."
The projection showed Kaido swinging a club. The weapon was coated in jagged black lightning. It wasn't electricity; it was his sheer, domineering Will leaking out of the weapon. When it hit, it didn't just hurt the body; it crushed the opponent's spirit, debuffing them, making them weak and afraid.
"This is the ultimate goal: Conqueror's Will," Ariel whispered. "They clad their attacks in their own Authority. They impose their reality on the world. They don't just hit you; they command you to fall."
The Summary
The hologram faded, returning them to the quiet clubroom. The silence was deafening.
Ariel turned to his friends.
"To those Legends, what I did against Riser is basic. It's the entry requirement to their world. That is the standard I am chasing."
He looked at Issei, Kiba, and Koneko.
"I can't give you Devil Fruits. But I can teach you the Intent.
 * Issei: Your Boosted Gear responds to Will. If you learn to clad your arm in your Will, you can punch through magic defenses.
 * Koneko: If you learn Armament, your defense becomes absolute. Poison, fire, acid‚Äînothing touches your skin.
 * Kiba: If you learn to project your Will into your sword, you can cut things that have no physical form... like ghosts, or light."
Rias let out a breath she didn't know she was holding. "And you... you are trying to reach the level of those monsters? As a human?"
"I'm trying," Ariel smiled, the tension breaking. "I'm still at level one compared to them. But the view from the top looks nice."
Issei stood up, his face set in stone.
"Teach me. I want to punch through magic."
Kiba gripped his sword hilt. "To cut the intangible... yes. I need this."
Ariel nodded. "Then we begin. Welcome to the grind."

üëÅÔ∏è Phase 4 (Continued): The Art of Sensing the Future
Occult Research Clubroom ‚Äì The PTD Projection
The atmosphere in the room had shifted from curiosity to heavy anticipation. Ariel stood in the center of the room, stretching his neck.
"Hardening the body is useful," Ariel addressed the group. "But the best defense is not being there when the attack lands. In that other world, this is called Observation (Kenbunshoku). It is the ability to hear the 'voice' of living things and, eventually, to see the future."
He waved his hand. "System. Archive: World 824. Topic: Sensory Mastery. Play the three levels of ascent."
1. The Inspiration: The Dark King‚Äôs Lesson
The hologram shifted to a dense jungle. An old man with silver hair and glasses (Silvers Rayleigh) stood before a young, blindfolded boy (Luffy).
"Watch," Ariel commanded.
The old man moved with terrifying speed, swinging a heavy wooden staff.
Whack. The boy got hit.
Whack. Hit again.
"He isn't trying to hear the wind or the footsteps," Ariel explained as the boy struggled. "He is trying to feel the Intent of the attacker. Living things emit a signal before they move. The will to strike exists milliseconds before the muscle contracts."
Suddenly, on screen, the boy tilted his head. The staff swung through empty air.
"There," Kiba whispered, eyes wide. "He dodged before the swing was fully committed."
2. The Inspiration: The Man Who Sees the Future
The scene shifted violently. A mirrored dimension. Two fighters clash.
One is a massive man with a scarf (Katakuri). His eyes glow red.
"This man," Ariel said, his voice grim, "has trained his Observation so deeply he doesn't just sense intent. He sees seconds into the future."
The peerage watched in horror.
Luffy threw a punch. Katakuri shifted his body into a donut shape before the punch arrived, letting the fist pass harmlessly through a hole in his torso.
"He isn't dodging," Issei stammered. "He's... reshaping his body around an attack that hasn't happened yet."
"Exactly," Ariel nodded. "It looks like invincibility. But it's just absolute knowledge. This is the wall the hero had to climb."
3. The Inspiration: The Natural State
The scene shifted to the legends again. Whitebeard sleeping, hooked up to medical machines. An assassin tried to attack him in his sleep. Without waking up, without opening his eyes, Whitebeard sent the assassin flying.
"For the Legends," Ariel said quietly, "the 'Future' is just part of the 'Present.' They don't turn this ability on. It is their natural state of existence. They are never surprised. They are never caught off guard. That is the goal."
‚öîÔ∏è The Live Demonstration: The PTD Gauntlet
The hologram faded, leaving only the sterile white grid of the PTD surrounding Ariel. The Peerage was now watching a live feed of Ariel's consciousness inside the simulation.
"Now," Ariel said, pulling a thick black cloth from his pocket. "I try to climb the first wall."
He tied the blindfold tight. Darkness took him.
> Observer: "Scenario: Rayleigh's Gauntlet. Threat: Dark King Rayleigh (Simulated). Weapon: Hardened Oak Staff. Speed: Variable. Goal: Dodge 100 consecutive strikes. Current Mastery: MND 2.0 / SPR 1.4."
> 
Ariel stood alone in the void. A digital reconstruction of Rayleigh shimmered into existence, holding the staff.
Rias watched, her hands gripping the back of a chair. "He's fighting a simulation of a legend... blind?"
The Struggle (0 - 20 Strikes)
Rayleigh moved.
CRACK.
The staff slammed into Ariel‚Äôs shoulder. Ariel grunted, stumbling back.
CRACK.
A sweep to the legs. Ariel hit the floor.
"Too slow," Ariel muttered to himself, standing up. "Stop listening. Stop thinking with the brain."
He focused his MND 2.0 inward. He stopped trying to calculate the trajectory (Tactics) and tried to switch to SPR 1.4 (Sensing the Will).
Whoosh.
The staff swung for his head. Ariel ducked.
The Peerage gasped.
Whoosh.
Ariel side-stepped.
"He's doing it," Akeno whispered. "He's sensing the energy signature of the construct."
The Rhythm (21 - 60 Strikes)
Rayleigh increased the speed. The attacks became a blur.
Ariel entered a flow state. He wasn't seeing the staff; he was seeing a jagged red spike of "Harmful Intent" appearing in the darkness of his mind just before the physical blow came.
Dodge left. Duck. Pivot. Jump.
He was moving like water. His PHY 2.0 allowed him to execute the movements his mind was seeing. For a moment, he looked untouchable‚Äîa true Silhouette.
The Overload (61 - 100 Strikes)
"Speed Level: High," the Observer announced.
Rayleigh vanished. He wasn't walking anymore; he was flashing.
Ariel‚Äôs brow furrowed. The "red spikes" were appearing too fast. They were overlapping.
Crack!
He took a hit to the ribs. His concentration wavered.
Crack!
A hit to the knee.
Crack! Whack. Thud.
The rhythm broke. Ariel was getting battered. He tried to regain the sense, but the pain was flooding his MND, creating noise. He managed to dodge a few desperate swings, but he was mostly just tanking the hits with his new PHY 2.0 durability.
Strike 100.
Rayleigh delivered a final, overhead smash. Ariel, exhausted and bruised, sensed it too late. He crossed his arms to block (Armament style) instead of dodging.
BAM.
The force sent him skidding back ten meters.
> Observer: "Simulation Complete. Dodged: 64/100. Status: Failure. You rely too much on logic (MND) when the pace increases. You must surrender fully to Intuition (SPR)."
> 
Ariel ripped the blindfold off, breathing heavily. He was covered in digital bruises that would fade in the real world but the pain phantom lingered.
He looked at the Peerage. They weren't looking at his failure. They were looking at the 64 times he moved like a ghost.
"I'm not there yet," Ariel said, wiping sweat from his eyes. "My brain is too loud. I think too much about 'where' the attack is, instead of just 'knowing' it's there. But... that's the training."
Issei looked at Ariel, then at his own hands.
"You dodged a ghost sixty times without seeing him," Issei said, shaking his head in disbelief. "If I could do that... Riser wouldn't have touched me at all."
Kiba stepped forward, his eyes burning with the intensity of a swordsman.
"The ability to sense the intent before the blade moves... Ariel-kun, that is the ultimate state of the sword. I need to learn this."
Ariel smiled, wincing slightly as he rubbed his bruised shoulder.
"Then grab a blindfold, Kiba. It's going to hurt."

üåå Phase 4 (Conclusion): The Library of Legends
Occult Research Clubroom ‚Äì Moments Later
Ariel caught his breath, the digital bruises from the Rayleigh simulation fading. He looked around at the stunned faces of the Peerage. They were still processing the concept of "Haki" and the image of the Pirate King splitting the sky.
"I showed you that reality first," Ariel said, gesturing to the fading hologram of the Grand Line, "because it‚Äôs my current favorite. The 'Silhouettes' in that world‚ÄîRocks, Roger, Garp‚Äîthey capture the feeling of being a legend perfectly. But..."
He straightened up, his expression shifting from exhaustion to a deep, burning passion.
"...that isn't the only mountain I'm climbing. To understand what I am, you need to see the rest of the library."
Ariel raised his hand. "System. Archive: Multi-Verse Overview. Rapid Projection."
The room darkened. Multiple screens flared into existence around them, surrounding the Peerage in a kaleidoscope of different worlds.
1. The Foundation: The Soldier (MGS & Manhwa)
Ariel pointed to a gritty, realistic screen on the left. It showed a man with an eyepatch in a jungle, and modern soldiers in sleek suits moving with terrifying efficiency.
"Before I could even think about magic, I had to master the body. You asked Rias-kaichou how I knew about CQC and infiltration? I lived the lives of the God of Blackfield, the Mercenary Enrollment Numbers, and the Big Boss of the Metal Gear Saga."
Rias watched a projection of Big Boss disarming three soldiers in under a second. "So this is the source of your tactical insight?"
"Yes. They are humans with no magic who became myths on the battlefield. That was my entry level. I had to become the best soldier before I could try to be a warrior."
2. The Current Struggle: The Broken God (Mori Dan)
Ariel pointed to a screen showing a young man with messy hair, his body covered in scars, fighting gods with just kicks.
"Right now, I feel most like him. Mori Dan from God of High School."
The projection showed Mori Dan fighting against opponents with overwhelming magical powers, using a technique called Recoilless Kick to bend space without magic.
"He was once the Heavenly Emperor‚Äîa God‚Äîbut his power was sealed, and his body was broken. He had to rely entirely on martial arts to fight entities capable of destroying worlds. That is me right now. I am the Mortal Variable trying to kick down the door of the Supernatural."
Kiba watched Mori Dan's movements intently. "Efficiency... forcing the world to bend to physical technique. I see."
3. The Aspirations: The Overlord and The Chaos (Bleach & Fairy Tail)
Ariel waved his hand, bringing two terrifying images to the forefront.
One showed a man in white (Aizen Sousuke) stopping a massive, magical bankai sword with a single index finger. The music shifted to a choir of treachery and transcendence.
"I don't agree with his evil methods," Ariel stated firmly. "But Aizen Sousuke... his aspiration to stand above heaven, to transcend both Hollows and Soul Reapers... that drive is beautiful. Look at him. He stops a blade capable of destroying a city with one finger. Not because of a spell, but because his Spiritual Pressure‚Äîhis Presence‚Äîis just that much denser."
Issei gulped. "He stopped it with a finger?! That's the level you want?"
"Higher," Ariel smiled.
He pointed to the next screen: A human transforming into a black dragon (Acnologia).
"And him. Acnologia. The Dragon King. In a war between Dragons and Humans, he was the Third Variable. He destroyed both sides to end the war. He didn't join a faction; he was the faction. That is the definition of the Silhouette. Uncontrollable. Absolute."
4. The Heavenly Demon (The Manhwas)
A flurry of images flashed‚Äîwarriors in ancient robes radiating distinct, dark, overwhelming auras. The Heavenly Demon.
"In the Murim worlds, there are those who reach the peak of Cultivation. They don't just fight; they overwhelm. I want that 'Heavenly' pressure. I want to be able to end a fight just by walking into the room."
5. The Ultimate Goal: The Gods (Dragon Ball Super)
Finally, Ariel commanded the center screen to expand. It showed beings that made the others look small.
A warrior with spiky hair turning silver (Goku - Ultra Instinct).
A purple cat deity destroying half a planet with a tap of his fingernail (Beerus).
An angel with blue skin holding a staff, smiling calmly while moving through time (Whis).
"And this..." Ariel‚Äôs voice dropped to a whisper of pure reverence. "...is the summit. Dragon Ball Super."
The Peerage watched Beerus (Bills) fight. It wasn't a fight; it was erasure.
They watched Whis dodge attacks automatically, his body moving without thought.
"Goku. Vegeta. The Gods of Destruction like Bills. The Angels like Whiz. They exist on a level where universes are fragile as glass. They don't use tricks. They use pure, condensed Power and Godly Technique."
Ariel turned off the projection. The room returned to normal, but the silence was heavy.
"That is why I train," Ariel said, looking at his friends. "I am currently at the level of a strong soldier (MGS). I am reaching for the level of a Haki user (One Piece). But one day... I want to stand there."
He pointed at the ceiling.
"I want to be the Mortal who became a God of Destruction through push-ups and willpower."
He looked at Rias, Akeno, Kiba, Koneko, Issei, and Asia.
"I'm not asking you to follow me all the way there. It's a path of pain, and you have your own responsibilities as Devils. But if you want to borrow from the Tactics of Big Boss, the Defense of One Piece, or the Focus of the Heavenly Demon... my library is open."
Rias let out a long, shaky breath. She looked at Ariel with a mixture of terror and absolute trust.
"You are a greedy human, Ariel Veritas," she said, a smile tugging at her lips. "Aiming for the seat of Gods."
"Why aim for the ceiling," Ariel grinned, his friendly face returning, "when there's a whole sky up there?"
[The Mortal Variable's path was set. And for the first time, he wasn't walking it alone.]

4.5. The Absolute Destroyer: Dokgo Ryong (Gosu)

This is a compelling, gritty, and psychologically rich inversion of the Ariel concept. Moving from a "Wish Fulfillment" narrative to a "Fallen Hero/Seeker of Darkness" narrative adds a layer of tragic realism. Without the safety net of the VR facility, the gap between "Anime Knowledge" and "Real World Physics" becomes a source of despair rather than empowerment.
Here is the dossier for this alternative character.
üåë Character Name: Ren Nocturnus (The Shadow of Envy)
 * Meaning: Ren (Lotus/Love/Purgatory) + Nocturnus (Of the Night).
 * Archetype: The Fallen Dreamer / The Seeker of Darkness.
 * Inspirations: Riku & Xehanort (Kingdom Hearts), Sasuke Uchiha (Naruto), Vergil (DMC).
 * Role: The "Fourth Wheel" of the Perverted Trio (making it a Quartet), and eventually, the Antagonist of his own story.
1. The Reality Check (The Struggle)
Unlike Ariel, Ren enters the world with the same knowledge (One Piece Haki, Dragon Ball Ki, etc.) but no PTD (Personal Training Dossier).
 * The Failed Grind: Ren tries to train like Ariel. He does the push-ups. He tries to meditate to feel "Ki."
   * Result: He gets shin splints. He breaks his knuckles punching trees. He passes out from holding his breath trying to unlock "Haki." He gains slightly above-average fitness, but compared to Devils and Sacred Gears, it is statistically insignificant.
 * The Perverted Quartet: To cope with his failure, he joins Matsuda, Motohama, and Issei. He indulges in their perverted fantasies because he craves the connection and the hope of a harem. He is the "strategist" of the peeping toms, using his intelligence for petty thrills because he can't achieve grand ones.
2. The Inferiority Complex (The Catalyst)
The turning point isn't a specific battle, but the slow erosion of his ego watching Issei Hyoudou.
 * The Jealousy: Issei is just like him‚Äîa pervert, a loser, a nobody. But Issei gets the Boosted Gear. Issei gets Rias Gremory. Issei gets Asia.
 * The Resentment: Ren works harder. Ren knows the "Lore" of power (Haki, Ki). Ren tries to teach Issei, but Issei succeeds by accident/luck/dragon heritage, while Ren fails despite his superior knowledge.
 * The Conclusion: Ren realizes that in this reality (High School DxD), he is an NPC. He is a background texture. The world is rigged against him.
3. The Awakening: The Heart of Darkness
Influenced by Xehanort's philosophy and Riku's early jealousy, Ren abandons the path of "Light/Ki/Haki" (which requires willpower and spirit he feels he lacks) and looks inward at his own ugly emotions.
 * The Discovery: He realizes that while he possesses no Magic, his Envy, Jealousy, and Despair are bottomless.
 * The Power: He begins to channel the Kingdom Hearts concept of Darkness. Not "Devil Magic," but the literal weight of the void in his heart.
 * Effect: He stops caring about girls. The harem dream dies, replaced by a cold, singular obsession with Leaving this Reality. He views the girls not as prizes, but as chains binding Issei to mediocrity.
4. The Climax: The Sasuke Departure
Timeline: Immediately post-Riser Wedding Battle.
The ORC is celebrating. Issei has saved Rias. They are the heroes.
Ren stands on the edge of the battlefield (or the ORC clubroom), wearing a black coat (Organization XIII style). He is preparing to open a Corridor of Darkness to leave this dimension entirely.
 * The Confrontation: The ORC tries to stop him. "Ren, we're friends! Where are you going?"
 * The Battle: Ren fights them all.
   * He uses Darkness-infused Haki (Dark Armament) fueled by self-loathing.
   * He uses Keyblade-esque constructs formed from shadows.
   * He brutally deconstructs them verbally: telling Issei he's just a lucky pervert, telling Rias she's weak for relying on a Pawn.
 * The Outcome: He defeats them (or stalemates them enough to escape), not through raw power, but because they are holding back (friendship) and he is fighting with the intent to sever all bonds (Darkness).
He steps into the portal, leaving Issei with a final, haunting message about finding a world where effort actually matters, paralleling Sasuke leaving Konoha.

He will never abandon his belief about energy, sense, will, and martial arts because they are true and he can learn them but not at the mastery level of Ariel (don't use the term "haki" because VR is not available so use more general term). Here is the revised framework for Ren Nocturnus and the progression of his Darkness, leading to the inevitable clash.
üåë Ren Nocturnus: The Shadow of Envy (Revised Dossier)
 * Role: The 4th Member of the Perverted Trio (The "Quiet Pervert" / Strategist).
 * Core Philosophy: "Light is a lie told by the talented. Darkness is the truth left for the rest of us." (Xehanort Influence).
 * Power Source:
   * Knowledge: Anime/Manga concepts (Ki, Will, Martial Arts).
   * Execution: Flawed/Incomplete. He knows how Goku does a Kamehameha, but he can only produce a spark. He knows how Zoro cuts steel, but he just dulls his blade.
   * The Catalyst: Darkness (Kingdom Hearts Style). He uses the darkness in his heart to fill the cracks in his failed training.
1. The "Failed" Grind (The Reality of No VR)
Without the PTD (VR Facility) to heal him or perfect his form, Ren‚Äôs attempts to copy anime training are brutal and disappointing.
 * The Physical Reality: He does the Saitama workout (100 pushups, etc.). Instead of becoming godlike, he just gets tendonitis and fatigue. He is fit for a human, but compared to a Pawn (Issei), he is paper.
 * The Energy Struggle: He spends nights meditating, trying to unlock "Ki" or "Will" (Haki).
   * Result: He manages to sense energy, but it gives him migraines. He tries to coat his fist in Will (Armament), but it‚Äôs so thin it shatters on impact. He is the student who studies harder than anyone but gets a 'C' because he lacks natural talent.
 * The Martial Arts: He practices moves from God of High School in the park at night. Without a master, his form is sloppy. He looks cool hitting the air, but in a real fight, he lacks the reflex and muscle memory.
2. The Slow-Burn Awakening (The Xehanort Routine)
Ren‚Äôs descent isn't a snap; it‚Äôs a daily erosion. It fits the Kingdom Hearts lore: " The closer you get to the Light, the greater your Shadow becomes."
 * The Routine of Envy: Every day, he watches Issei. Issei is lazy, perverted, and unskilled. Yet, Issei gets the Sacred Gear. Issei gets the girl. Issei gets the powerups.
 * The Whispers: Ren starts to accept the negative emotions not as "bad," but as Fuel.
   * When he feels jealous: He doesn't suppress it. He channels it. He finds that when he is hateful, his "Will" coating is slightly stronger.
   * When he feels despair: He finds his senses are sharper.
 * The Xehanort Philosophy: He starts reading books on philosophy, convincing himself that the world of DxD is flawed. The Devils, Angels, and Fallen are all fighting for "Light" and control. He begins to seek the "World of Void"‚Äîa place outside this unfair system.
3. The Perverted Quartet & The Mask
To hide his growing darkness, he wears the mask of the "Pervert."
 * The Dynamic: He hangs out with Issei, Matsuda, and Motohama. He creates the "peeping plans."
 * The Internal Monologue: While the others are screaming about oppai, Ren is silently analyzing the physics of the girls' movements or the aura of the Kendo club members, trying to steal techniques. He pretends to care about the girls to fit in, but deep down, the Darkness is killing his libido. He starts seeing the girls not as objects of desire, but as symbols of Issei's unearned success.
üé¨ The Climax: The Departure (Post-Riser Wedding)
Timeline: The Gremory Peerage has crashed the wedding, Issei has defeated Riser (Canon events), and they have returned to the Old School Building for the victory celebration.
The room is loud. Issei is being hugged by Rias and Asia. The other perverts are crying tears of joy.
Ren stands by the open window, wearing a long black coat (Organization XIII style). The "Pervert" mask is gone.
Ren: "It's loud. Light... is always so loud."
The room goes quiet. Ren turns around. His eyes are dull, devoid of the usual perverted gleam.
Issei: "Ren? What's up, man? Come grab a drink! We won!"
Ren: " You won, Issei. You always win. Because the script is written for you."
Ren raises his hand. He doesn't summon a Sacred Gear. He summons a swirling, purple-black portal behind him‚Äîa Corridor of Darkness.
Rias: (Eyes widening) "That energy... it‚Äôs not Demonic. It‚Äôs... pure negative space. Ren, step away from that!"
Ren: "I tried, Rias. I did the pushups. I studied the flow of energy. I mediated until my nose bled. And in the end... Issei got stronger by touching breasts."
He chuckles‚Äîa dry, humorless sound.
"I'm done playing the NPC in your story. I'm going to a world where the heart's darkness matters more than a dragon's handout."
The Battle: The Quartet vs. The Seeker
Issei, Kiba, and Koneko rush to stop him, not to kill him, but to save their friend.
 * Ren vs. Koneko: Koneko punches. Ren doesn't dodge. He coats his body in Darkness (imitating Armament Hardening). It's not perfect; her punch cracks his ribs, but the darkness absorbs the kinetic force, allowing him to grab her arm and throw her with a judo throw he learned from a manga.
   * Ren: "Your strength is borrowed from your race. My pain is my own."
 * Ren vs. Kiba: Kiba uses his speed. Ren can't keep up visually, so he floods the floor with shadow (imitating a Domain or Logia). He sinks into the darkness (Kingdom Hearts Shadow movement) and uppercuts Kiba from his blind spot.
   * Ren: "You move fast, Knight. But darkness is everywhere."
 * Ren vs. Issei: Issei screams, activating the Boosted Gear. "Snap out of it, Ren!"
   Ren looks at the glowing red gauntlet‚Äîthe symbol of everything he hates. He channels all his envy, all his training, and all his darkness into his hand. He forms a blade of pure void (like early Riku's Soul Eater).
   They clash. Issei overpowers him instantly with raw force. Ren is sent flying into the wall. He coughs blood. He barely succeeded in even standing his ground.
The Departure
Ren stands up, broken, bleeding, but smiling. He realizes he can't beat them. But he has achieved his goal: He stood against them.
Ren: "See? Even with all my darkness... I'm still the side character."
He steps backward into the portal.
Ren: "Goodbye, Issei. Enjoy your harem. I'll be seeking the Kingdom... where the heart is true."
The portal snaps shut, leaving the ORC in stunned silence. Ren Nocturnus is gone, seeking a new reality, leaving a scar on the victory celebration that will never heal.

This sets up a tragic, recurring villain/anti-hero dynamic.
Question: For his combat style during the fight, since he "struggles" with the anime concepts:

This balances the character perfectly. He becomes a tragic figure not because he fails completely, but because he succeeds just enough to realize it's not enough.
He is competent. He is dangerous. But he is hitting a glass ceiling that Issei smashes through effortlessly. His "Veritas" (Truth) nature means he cannot lie to himself about this gap, leading him to the Darkness.
Here is the finalized profile and narrative arc for Ren Nocturnus Veritas.
üåë Ren Nocturnus Veritas: The Honest Seeker
 * Archetype: The Competent Mortal / The Seeker of Darkness.
 * Core Trait: Veritas (Honesty). He is brutally honest with himself and others. He admits his jealousy, his perversion, and his inferiority without making excuses.
 * The "Origin": He is a being naturally born with an affinity for Darkness (Kingdom Hearts definition: not evil, but the primordial void). He doesn't realize this until his anime training hits a wall.
 * Appearance: He looks exactly like his human self (no yellow eyes, no white hair). The only change is his aura‚Äîit becomes heavy, quiet, and light-absorbing.
1. The Competent Struggle (Basic Mastery)
Ren doesn't fail; he plateaus. He achieves what a peak human can achieve, and then pushes slightly further using his innate Darkness.
 * Martial Arts (Mori Dan Style): He learns the forms perfectly. He has excellent technique. In a sparring match with a human, he wins 10/10 times. Against a Devil, he can parry and dodge, but he lacks the "weight" to deliver a finishing blow.
 * Observation (Haki/Ki): He can sense energy. He successfully unlocks a basic "Danger Sense" (Spidey-sense/Observation). He can predict where a Fallen Angel will throw a spear, allowing him to survive (influence events), but he isn't fast enough to intercept it mid-air like Ariel.
 * Armament (Will/Hardening): He understands the concept. He can coat his fists. But because he lacks "Light" or "Magic," his hardening is brittle. It can block a low-level attack, but a serious blow from Riser would shatter it.
   * The Fix: He subconsciously fills the cracks in his Will with Darkness, turning his "Armament" into a dense, shadowy armor.
2. The Loss of the "Pervert" (The Awakening)
This is a tragic, slow-burn loss of self.
 * The Honest Pervert: Initially, he is Issei‚Äôs genuine wingman. He loves the "Peeping" missions. He is the strategist of the trio. He is fun, loud, and kind.
 * The Erosion: As Issei grows stronger, Ren sees the girls flocking to the dragon. Ren‚Äôs "Veritas" forces him to admit the truth: They will never look at me. I am the background.
 * The Shift:
   * Day 10: He peeps, but feels a hollow pang in his chest.
   * Day 20: He stops laughing at the jokes. He is still kind, but distant.
   * Day 30: He realizes he no longer feels lust. The Darkness‚Äîthe desire for the Void‚Äîhas consumed his earthly desires. He isn't pretending to lose interest; he genuinely feels nothing but the drive for power and meaning.
3. The Climax: The Honest Departure
Timeline: The Old School Building, Victory Celebration (Post-Riser Defeat).
The party is in full swing. Issei is the hero.
Ren Nocturnus Veritas stands by the door, wearing a long, black coat (Organization XIII style). He isn't angry. He is calm.
Ren: "I'm leaving, Issei."
The room goes silent. Rias steps forward, smiling.
Rias: "Leaving? The party is just starting, Ren. You helped with the strategy against Riser's pawns. Celebrate with us!"
Ren: "I helped. But I didn't change anything. The dragon won. The human watched."
He raises his hand. The air grows heavy. Shadows bleed from the corners of the room, coalescing into a swirling Corridor of Darkness.
Issei: "Dude, stop joking. That magic feels... cold. What are you doing?"
Ren: (Veritas) "I'm being honest, Issei. I'm jealous. I hate that you were chosen. I hate that I work until my bones crack just to block one attack, while you scream once and destroy a mountain. I love you guys, but I hate my place in this world."
He turns to the portal.
Rias: "I can't let you leave into that void. It‚Äôs dangerous. As your President‚Äîas your friend‚ÄîI'm ordering you to stop!"
The ORC moves to restrain him‚Äîgently, because he is their friend.
The Battle: The Darkness Released
Ren sighs. He doesn't want to fight, but he will not be stopped.
 * Vs. Koneko: She charges to grab him. Ren uses Flow (Martial Arts). He coats his arm in Dark Armament‚Äîit is black, smoking, and dense. He parries her punch, the darkness absorbing the kinetic energy, and sweeps her legs. He doesn't hurt her, but he knocks her back with shocking force.
 * Vs. Kiba: Kiba uses speed. Ren closes his eyes. Observation (Darkness Enhanced). He senses the intent. He can't move as fast as Kiba, so he floods the floor with shadows, slowing Kiba down, and blocks the wooden sword with a Darkened Hand, snapping the wood.
 * Vs. Issei: Issei activates the Boosted Gear, holding back tears. "Why, Ren?! We're the Perverted Trio!"
Ren looks at him, his face completely stoic. The pervert is dead.
Ren: "I don't care about girls anymore, Issei. I only care about the Truth."
Ren channels his Darkness. It forms jagged, unrefined constructs‚Äîclaws of shadow (resembling a rough, incomplete Susanoo or Xehanort's Guardian).
He clashes with Issei. The sheer weight of Ren's Despair and Darkness momentarily pushes the Boosted Gear back.
He blasts Issei away with a pulse of pure rejection.
The Exit
Ren stands panting. He didn't defeat them, but he fought them to a standstill because they hesitated to hurt him, and he fought with the desperation of someone with nothing left to lose.
Ren: "I'm going to find the World of Darkness. A place where light doesn't blind you."
Issei: "Ren! Come back!"
Ren: "Goodbye, Issei. Become the Harem King. I'll become the Seeker."
He steps into the void. The portal closes.
The Aftermath:
The victory is hollow. They won Rias back, but they lost Ren. His absence leaves a permanent scar on the group, specifically Issei, who realizes his success cost his best friend his humanity.
‚öñÔ∏è Comparison of Outcomes
| Feature | Ariel Caelum Veritas | Ren Nocturnus Veritas |
|---|---|---|
| Destiny | The Wish Fulfillment / The Legend | The Tragic Seeker / The Fallen Friend |
| Power Source | PTD (VR) + Human Potential | Knowledge + Darkness (to fill the gaps) |
