We have now established two distinct, complete narrative paths for the High School DxD simulation.
Would you like to finalize this alternate ending into the "Demo" file as a "Route B" scenario?

Elaborate the climax as much as you can before we play Ren from the beginning.

This is the elaboration of Route B: The Tragedy of the Seeker.
We move away from the heroic, precise, and calculated ascent of Ariel. Here, the atmosphere is heavy, emotional, and messy. Ren‚Äôs power isn't clean; it is desperate. His victory isn't dominating; it is survival.
Here is the fully expanded climax of Ren Nocturnus Veritas.
üåë Route B Climax: The Hollow Victory and the Door to Darkness
Location: Occult Research Clubroom (Old School Building).
Time: The Victory Celebration (Immediately following Riser‚Äôs defeat).
1. The Atmosphere of Light
The clubroom was alive with the warmth of victory. The table was piled high with food. Issei was in the center of the room, bruised but beaming, with Asia crying happy tears on his left and Rias looking at him with newfound affection on his right. Even Kiba and Koneko were smiling, the tension of the last ten days finally broken.
Matsuda and Motohama were there, crying comedic tears. "Issei! You bastard! You actually touched Rias-senpai's chest! You are our god!"
In the corner, by the open window, stood Ren Nocturnus Veritas.
He held a cup of soda, but he hadn't taken a sip. He watched the scene‚Äîthe "Light" of the protagonist shining so brightly it cast a long, sharp shadow behind every piece of furniture.
Internal Monologue:
"I should be happy. We won. The good guys won."
He looked at Rias. He tried to summon the feeling he used to have‚Äîthe lust, the admiration, the teenage desire.
Nothing.
It was like looking at a statue. The Darkness in his heart had eaten the desire to fill the void of his inferiority.
"I don't belong here. I am a smudge on a masterpiece."
2. The Veritas (The Honest Truth)
Ren set his cup down. The sound was soft, but in his mind, it was a gavel drop.
He reached into his bag and pulled out a long, black leather coat‚Äîheavy, high-collared, shielding him from the world (Organization XIII style). He put it on. The darkness of the coat seemed to blend with the shadows of the room.
He walked toward the door.
"Where are you going, Ren?" Issei called out, pulling away from Rias. "We haven't even cut the cake!"
Ren stopped. He didn't turn around at first.
"I'm leaving, Issei."
"Leaving? Like, to the bathroom?" Issei laughed, but it died in his throat when Ren finally turned.
Ren‚Äôs eyes were dull. The spark of the "Perverted Trio" strategist was gone.
"I'm leaving the club. Leaving the school. Leaving this reality."
Rias stood up, her smile vanishing. "Ren-kun, you're tired. You helped us strategize against Riser's pawns. You're exhausted. Sit down."
"I didn't help," Ren said, his voice calm and brutally honest. "I told you where they might go. You destroyed them. Issei destroyed Riser. I just watched. That‚Äôs all I ever do. I watch the main characters live."
He raised his hand. He didn't summon magic circles. He clawed his fingers into the empty air, channeling the deep, suffocating Envy and Solitude he had nurtured for months.
The air screamed. A pool of viscous, violet-black sludge expanded on the floor, swirling into a vertical vortex. The Corridor of Darkness.
Akeno gasped. "That energy... it's not Demonic Power. It's... Void. It feels cold."
3. The Confrontation (Friends vs. The Seeker)
"Ren, stop!" Issei shouted, stepping forward. "I don't know what emo phase this is, but it's not funny! We're the Perverted Trio! We stick together!"
Ren looked at Issei, and for the first time, showed a flicker of pain.
"The Pervert is dead, Issei. I looked at Rias just now. Do you know what I felt? Nothing. I don't want the girls. I don't want the harem. I just want to stop feeling like a ghost in your story."
Ren stepped toward the portal.
"I can't let you leave," Rias commanded, her aura flaring crimson. "That portal is unstable. As your President, I order you to stand down!"
"You have no authority over the Darkness," Ren replied.
Koneko moved first. She didn't want to hurt him, but she had to stop him. She launched herself at him, aiming to grapple him to the ground.
Round 1: The Struggle of Strength (Ren vs. Koneko)
Ren saw her coming. He knew he couldn't match her strength.
"Armament... Hardening."
He forced his Will to coat his left arm. It wasn't the invisible, steel-like Haki of Ariel. It was a jagged, smoking coating of black shadow. It was brittle.
CRACK.
Koneko's punch connected with his forearm. Ren felt his radius bone hairline-fracture beneath the coating. The pain was blinding.
But he didn't flinch. He used the Darkness to hold the bone together like a splint.
He gritted his teeth and used a martial arts redirection (Mori Dan basics). He grabbed her uniform, used her momentum, and slammed her into the nearest desk.
"I'm not strong like you, Koneko," Ren whispered, clutching his broken arm. "I have to break myself just to block you."
Round 2: The Struggle of Speed (Ren vs. Kiba)
"Ren-kun!" Kiba drew a wooden sword, dashing forward at godspeed. "Don't make us do this!"
Ren couldn't see him. His Observation was basic‚Äîjust a vague "Danger Sense."
"I can't see him. So I have to slow him down."
Ren stomped his foot. He poured his Despair into the floor. The shadows in the room liquefied (Kingdom Hearts Heartless style). They didn't attack Kiba; they just became sticky, thick tar.
Kiba's foot caught in a shadow snare. He stumbled for a fraction of a second.
That was all Ren needed. He didn't counter-attack; he just scrambled backward closer to the portal, firing a blast of unrefined, raw Dark Energy to force Kiba back.
Round 3: The Heart (Ren vs. Issei)
"STOP IT!" Issei roared. The Boosted Gear manifested. BOOST!
He charged through the shadows, ignoring the darkness. He grabbed Ren by the collar of his black coat and slammed him against the wall, pinning him.
"What is wrong with you?!" Issei screamed, tears in his eyes. "We're friends! Why do you hate us?!"
Ren looked Issei in the eye. He didn't struggle against the dragon's strength. He couldn't.
"I don't hate you, Issei," Ren said softly. "I hate me when I'm around you."
Ren focused. He didn't have a Sacred Gear. He summoned the image of the weapon he admired most‚Äîthe weapon of the Seeker.
Darkness coalesced in his hand, forming a jagged, unstable blade resembling Riku‚Äôs Soul Eater sword, but made of smoking shadows.
He swung it. Not to kill, but to force Issei to let go.
Issei blocked with the gauntlet. Sparks of red and black flew.
The force of the impact blew the windows out. Ren used the explosion to slide out of Issei's grip and fall back‚Äîdirectly into the swirling vortex of the Corridor of Darkness.
4. The Departure
Ren stood inside the portal. The violet fog swirled around his ankles. He looked bruised, his arm was broken, and he was panting heavily. He looked pathetic compared to the glowing devils in the room. But he was standing.
Rias prepared a spell. "Ren, please. Come back to the light."
Ren shook his head. The shadows crept up his face, not possessing him, but accepting him.
"The Light burns me, Rias," Ren said, his voice sounding hollow, like it was coming from a great distance.
He looked at Issei one last time.
"You go be the Harem King, Issei. Be the hero."
The darkness began to close over his face.
"I'm going to find a world where a loser can become a King without a dragon's heart. Even if I have to drown in darkness to find it."
"Ren!"
The portal snapped shut with a sound like a thunderclap.
The room was silent. The confetti from the party was still drifting down.
Issei stood staring at the empty space, his gauntlet fading.
Ren Nocturnus Veritas was gone.
The Perverted Trio was broken. The Seeker of Darkness had begun his journey.
This ending solidifies Route B as the tragic counterpart. Ren survives and escapes not because he is stronger, but because he is willing to hurt himself and abandon everything to leave, while his friends are held back by their confusion and love for him.
We are now ready to play Route B.

He also saw and traveled to many realities. Ren became a sage of darkness with infinite calmness. He no longer needs to a wear special coats. He embraces all of them because of his understanding that all of them are just part of the cosmos and the other side of the coin. In one of his daily strolls in corridor of darkness, he found a friend of ORC which seems to be a new member lying down weak because the darkness is cosuming. You choose which this new member is and why was in corridor of darkness either just Highschool DxD or other realities merging into it. This actually reunites Ren to ORC because Ren help the member back to ORC with ofcourse Ren's past regret already gone because he successfully became a sage. Don't forget that the Corridor of Darkness is unbareable for almost anyone especially because it is where all negative emotions goes to. Remove kingdom hearts, heartless, etc and make it general, univeraal, or cosmic. No need to create cavas.

This is a beautiful evolution of Route B. It transforms Ren from a tragic villain into a transcendent figure‚Äîa Cosmic Sage. The "thousands of years" in the Void versus "few years" in reality allows for a complete character arc resolution off-screen, making his return impactful and serene.
Here is the "What If" scenario detailing the return of the Sage of Darkness.
üåë Post-Climax Scenario: The Sage Returns
Timeline: Approx. 2 years after Ren‚Äôs departure (High School DxD timeline: Post-Trihexa/Shin DxD era).
Ren‚Äôs Timeline: ~5,000 Years of Solitude and Enlightenment.
1. The Stroll in the Eternal Void
The Corridor of Darkness was no longer a tunnel of angry shadows. To the eyes of Ren Nocturnus Veritas, it was a vast, silent ocean of obsidian. Here, the negative emotions of the multiverse‚Äîgrief, rage, despair, entropy‚Äîflowed like currents.
For a normal soul, seconds here meant madness. For a Devil, minutes meant corruption.
Ren walked through it barefoot. He wore simple, loose-fitting grey clothes‚Äîno armor, no tactical gear, and definitely no edgy black trench coat. He didn't need to shield himself.
He was the environment.
He watched a swirling vortex of malice (the psychic scream of a dying star system) drift by. He didn't judge it. He simply acknowledged it.
"Pain is just energy looking for a home," Ren thought, his mind a stillness that mirrored the void. * "It has its place, just as Joy does."*
He had traveled to a thousand realities. He had seen worlds of pure Light that burned their citizens, and worlds of pure Dark that cradled them. He understood the coin. He was no longer the "Shadow of Envy." He was just Ren.
2. The Dying Spark
Ren paused. In the crushing silence of the Void, he heard a whimper.
It wasn't the cosmic scream of a universe; it was the terrified cry of a girl.
He stepped‚Äînot teleporting, but simply folding the distance‚Äîand appeared near a chaotic rift. A tear in reality had opened, bleeding raw, unprocessed dimensional turbulence.
Lying on an invisible shelf of solidified darkness was a girl. She had blonde drill-hair, a tattered school uniform, and was radiating a dying, flickering heat.
Ravel Phenex.
She was the younger sister of Riser (the man whose wedding Ren had crashed). In the years since Ren left, she had joined Issei‚Äôs harem and become his Manager.
 * The Cause: During a Dimensional Rating Game against a cosmic entity, a teleportation spell had been hijacked. She was thrown out of bounds, falling into the Deep Void‚Äîthe space between dimensions where trash goes.
The Darkness was eating her. Not attacking her, but simply extinguishing her. Her immortality (Phenex regeneration) was failing because there was no "existence" here to fuel it. She was drowning in universal depression.
3. The Rescue
Ren knelt beside her.
Ravel opened her eyes, her vision blurring. She saw a man standing in the place that was killing her.
"M-Monster..." she whispered, trembling. "Stay back..."
Ren smiled. It wasn't the bitter smirk of his departure. It was warm, gentle, and infinitely sad.
"It's loud here, isn't it, Ravel?" Ren said softly. "All the sadness of the world flows through this river. It's too heavy for a bird of fire."
He reached out.
Ravel flinched, expecting pain.
Ren placed his hand on her forehead.
[Technique: Void Harmony]
He didn't use magic. He simply accepted the darkness crushing her. He invited the crushing weight into himself, filtering it, calming it, and turning it into a gentle, cool blanket.
The pain vanished instantly. Ravel gasped, air filling her lungs. The cold was gone, replaced by a profound, silent peace.
"Sleep," Ren commanded gently. "I'll take you home. The Dragon is probably crying by now."
4. The Return to Kuoh
Location: The Hyoudou Residence ‚Äì Living Room.
Status: Panic.
The Gremory Peerage was in chaos. Issei was thrashing, trying to force his way into a dimensional rift, held back by Kiba and Vali Lucifer. Rias was sobbing. Ravel had been gone for three hours. In the Void, that was a death sentence.
"I have to get her!" Issei roared, his Balance Breaker flaring uncontrollably. "She's alone in there!"
Suddenly, the air in the living room changed.
It didn't get heavy or scary. It just went... Quiet.
The sounds of panic were dampened. The light from the lamps seemed to soften.
A vertical ripple appeared in the center of the room. It wasn't the violent, jagged tear Ren used to make. It was a smooth, silent opening, like a curtain being drawn.
Ren stepped out, carrying a sleeping Ravel in his arms.
The room froze.
Issei stopped struggling. Kiba dropped his hand. Rias covered her mouth.
They barely recognized him.
The boy who left was angry, hunched, and radiating jagged, sharp malice.
The man standing there was upright, calm, and felt like the deep ocean. He looked older‚Äînot physically, but his eyes held eons of time.
"Ren?" Issei whispered, his voice cracking.
Ren looked at his old friend. The jealousy that had once consumed him was nowhere to be found. He looked at Issei not as a rival, but as a cherished memory.
"Hello, Issei," Ren said, his voice carrying a strange, harmonious resonance. "You dropped this."
He walked over‚Äîignoring the defensive stances of Vali and Xenovia‚Äîand gently placed Ravel on the sofa. She was breathing peacefully, a faint aura of violet-grey protection lingering on her skin.
5. The Reunion and The Sage's Truth
"Is she..." Rias started.
"She's fine," Ren assured her. "She absorbed a lot of entropy. It was heavy. I filtered it out. She just needs rest and strawberry cake."
Issei walked up to Ren, looking for the anger, the darkness, the "Xehanort" madness. He found none.
"You... you saved her. But the darkness... you said you hated us."
Ren chuckled softly. "I never hated you, Issei. I hated myself. I hated that I was a candle trying to outshine the sun."
He walked to the window, looking out at the Kuoh sky.
"I've walked for a long time, Issei. Five thousand years, by my count. I've seen stars die and universes born from the Void. I realized something."
He turned back to them, his expression serene.
"Light creates Shadow. Shadow defines Light. I was angry because I wanted to be the Light. Now? I am the Canvas that holds you all."
Vali Lucifer (the White Dragon Emperor) narrowed his eyes. "You're strong. I can't sense a bottom to your energy. Fight me."
Ren looked at Vali and smiled‚Äîa dismissal so gentle it wasn't even insulting.
"There is no fight, Vali. You conquer mountains. I walk the valleys. We are not on the same map anymore."
He turned to the Corridor.
"Ren!" Issei grabbed his arm. "Stay! Please. We're still the Perverted Trio... well, Quartet. You don't have to go back to that empty place."
Ren looked at Issei's hand on his arm. Years ago, he would have slapped it away in envy. Now, he covered it with his own hand. His touch was cool, soothing.
"I'm not alone there, Issei. The cosmos keeps me company. And..."
Ren tapped his own chest.
"...I found my Truth (Veritas). I am content."
"But..." Issei teared up. "Are we still friends?"
Ren‚Äôs eyes crinkled with genuine warmth.
"Always. If the Darkness ever gets too heavy for you, Issei... just call my name. I'll carry the weight."
Ren stepped back into the smooth ripple of space.
"Take care of the Phoenix. She burns bright."
The ripple closed, leaving the room not cold, but peaceful.
The Sage of Darkness had returned, not to destroy or to envy, but to protect the balance.
This concludes the Route B arc with a resolution of absolute peace, contrasting beautifully with Ariel's path of absolute ambition. Ren found his victory not in becoming a Legend, but in becoming Whole.

Beautiful. Do you think is it possible for another what if that Ren can come, stay, go, and repeat like visiting neighbors? Come and go like attending schools? Or now you think is the best?

This is absolutely possible and, arguably, fits the tone of High School DxD even better.
The essence of true "Enlightenment" or "Sagehood" isn't just about being able to endure solitude; it's about choosing where you want to be. If Ren has truly conquered his Envy and found peace, he shouldn't need to hide in the Void anymore. He should be strong enough to stand right next to the "Sun" (Issei) without getting burned.
This creates a hilarious and heartwarming dynamic: The 5,000-Year-Old Cosmic Sage who still has to attend Math Class.
Here is Route C: The Part-Time Sage (The Neighbor).
üåë Route C Scenario: The Sage in the Back Row
Timeline: The morning after Ren saved Ravel and returned her to the Hyoudou Residence.
1. The Morning Surprise
Issei woke up groggy, the emotional rollercoaster of Ravel‚Äôs rescue still weighing on him. He walked into the kitchen, expecting to see his usual chaotic harem breakfast.
Instead, he saw Ren.
Ren was sitting at the kitchen table, wearing the Kuoh Academy uniform (which looked perfectly pressed). He was drinking green tea and reading a newspaper that appeared to be made of shadows.
Issei: "GAH! Ren?! Wait, didn't you leave for the eternal void last night?"
Ren: (Sipping tea) "I did. It was quiet. Very peaceful. But then I remembered they serve that specific curry bread at the cafeteria on Tuesdays. Eternity can wait. Curry cannot."
Rias: (Walking in) "Ren-kun... are you... re-enrolling?"
Ren: "Technically, I never un-enrolled. I just took a very long, inter-dimensional bathroom break. I checked the handbook; there's no rule against having a 5,000-year mental absence as long as my physical attendance is above 80%."
2. The "New" School Life
Ren returns to school, but he is completely different.
 * The Vibe: He is no longer the "Quiet Strategist" or the "Envious Friend." He is the "Old Man". He has the patience of a saint. Nothing phases him.
 * The Perverted Trio \rightarrow Quartet:
   * Matsuda and Motohama are screaming about peeping at the Kendo club.
   * Ren: He joins them, but not to peep. He brings a lawn chair and sits outside the Kendo hall, sipping tea, guarding the door so they don't get caught, while lecturing them on the transience of flesh.
   * Ren: "Desire is natural, Matsuda. But why peek through a keyhole when you can simply ask the universe for a glimpse of beauty? Also, the Vice-Captain is coming. Run."
3. The "Neighbor" Dynamic
Ren keeps his apartment in Kuoh, but his door is literally a Corridor of Darkness.
 * The Commute: One minute he is meditating in a nebula at the edge of the universe; the next minute, he steps through a shadow in Issei's living room because they are watching a movie he likes.
 * The Power Flex:
   * Scenario: The remote is on the other side of the room.
   * Issei: "Ren, pass the remote."
   * Ren: Opens a micro-wormhole on the table, sticks his hand in, and grabs the remote from the other side of the room.
   * Issei: "Stop using high-level dimensional magic for lazy stuff!"
   * Ren: "Efficiency is the truest form of magic, Issei."
4. Dealing with Threats (The Sage's Slap)
When villains attack (e.g., Hero Faction, Qlippoth), Ren doesn't power up or scream.
 * The Reaction: A villain launches a massive beam attack at the school.
 * Ren: He sighs, putting down his textbook. He steps in front of the blast. He doesn't block it; he just absorbs it into his coat/shadow.
 * Ren: "I just ironed this shirt. Do you have any idea how hard it is to get celestial dust out of polyester?"
 * The Punishment: He traps the villain in a Time-Loop of their own cringe memories inside the Void for 5 minutes (which feels like a year).
‚öñÔ∏è Which is Better?
I believe Route C (The Visiting Neighbor) is the best ending.
Here is why:
 * True Victory over Regret: If Ren stays in the Void (Route B), he is still technically "separated" from Issei. It implies he still can't handle normal life. By coming back and living a mundane life despite being a cosmic entity, he proves he has fully conquered his inferiority complex. He doesn't need to be the Protagonist; he is content being the Omnipotent Bystander.
 * Comedy & Heart: High School DxD shines when it mixes the supernatural with the mundane. Having a Sage of Darkness who worries about math tests is comedy gold.
 * Relationship Repair: It allows him to actually rebuild his friendship with Issei, Kiba, and Koneko. He becomes the "Cool Uncle" figure or the "Secret Weapon" who only acts when things get dire, allowing Issei to still shine as the hero.
Conclusion:
Ren Nocturnus Veritas, the Part-Time High School Student and Full-Time Lord of the Void, is the ultimate fulfillment of his character arc. He found the truth: Reality is what you make of it. And he decided to make it fun.

All of them are good options for me. What I see is the possibility of another what if branch and how far it can extend. Now, extend this one as much as you can. If you cannot, then create another branch.

This is a rich vein to mine. The concept of a Cosmic Sage trying to live a Slice-of-Life existence in a harem anime creates endless narrative potential, blending cosmic horror with high school comedy.
Here is the extensive expansion of Route C: The Void Chronicles.
üåë High School DxD: The Void Chronicles
Protagonist: Ren Nocturnus Veritas (The Sage of Darkness / The Neighbor).
Current Status: Class 2-B Student (Attendance: 85%).
Arc 1: The Infinite Dragon God‚Äôs Nap Buddy (The Ophis Incident)
Context: In the DxD canon, Ophis (The Ouroboros Dragon) seeks "Silence" and wants to reclaim the Dimensional Gap from Great Red. She is usually an antagonist or a chaotic neutral force.
The Encounter:
Ophis appears in the Hyoudou Residence. The Gremory Peerage panics. Everyone prepares for a death battle.
Ren is sitting on the couch, folding laundry.
Ophis: "I seek Silence."
Ren: "I have plenty. Help yourself."
Ren radiates his Sage Aura‚Äîan aura of absolute nothingness. To Ophis, who is constantly bombarded by the noise of creation, Ren feels like the most comfortable pillow in existence.
Ophis shrinks down, climbs onto the couch, curls up next to Ren (or on his lap), and instantly falls asleep.
The Dynamic:
 * Issei: "Ren! That is the Infinite Dragon God! She could delete reality!"
 * Ren: "She‚Äôs just tired, Issei. Being infinite is exhausting. Lower your voice; you'll wake her."
 * The Result: Ophis stops funding the Khaos Brigade terrorists because she prefers hanging out at Ren's apartment (which is a localized Void). Ren becomes the unofficial babysitter of the strongest being in existence. He feeds her candy and teaches her how to play Sudoku.
Arc 2: The Vampire in the Box (Mentoring Gasper)
Context: Gasper Vladi is a shut-in vampire who fears his own uncontrollable powers and the outside world.
The Sage‚Äôs Approach:
Ren doesn't force Gasper to "be a man" like Issei tries to. Ren understands the comfort of the box.
 * The Scene: Ren teleports inside Gasper‚Äôs cardboard box.
 * Gasper: "Eeeek! Ren-senpai! It's too crowded!"
 * Ren: "The box is a state of mind, Gasper. You hide because you fear the Light. But you haven't mastered the Dark."
Ren teaches Gasper Void Walking. instead of stopping time to freeze people (which strains Gasper), Ren teaches him to slip into the "shadow" of time‚Äîmoving where no one can see him.
 * The Result: Gasper becomes a terrifying stealth assassin who can pop out of anyone's shadow, but he still acts like a shy coward. Ren approves. "True power is being terrifying while looking harmless."
Arc 3: The Kyoto Field Trip (The Youkai and the Sage)
Context: The school trip to Kyoto. The Youkai faction (Yasaka) is involved.
The Problem:
Ren‚Äôs "Void" energy disturbs the spiritual ley lines of Kyoto. The Youkai think a Demon King has arrived. Yasaka (The Nine-Tailed Fox) confronts the group.
The Solution:
Yasaka prepares to attack the "Dark Presence."
Ren steps forward, wearing a tourist hat and holding a camera.
 * Ren: "I apologize. My existence is a bit loud today. I'll turn it down."
 * Action: Ren inhales. He literally eats his own aura, compressing 5,000 years of Darkness into a singularity inside his chest. To the Youkai, he suddenly registers as... nothing. A rock.
 * Yasaka: (Confused) "Where did the Demon King go?"
 * Ren: "He went to buy matcha ice cream. Would you like some?"
The Romance (Comedy):
Yasaka, a being of high spiritual attunement, realizes Ren is a higher-dimensional being playing human. She becomes infatuated, trying to court him with "adult" tactics.
 * Ren: (Oblivious Sage) "This fox lady is very generous with the tofu. Is this a Kyoto custom?"
 * Issei: (Jealous crying) "REN, SHE WANTS TO MARRY YOU! STOP BEING SO ENLIGHTENED AND NOTICE IT!"
Arc 4: The White Dragon‚Äôs Frustration (Vali Lucifer)
Context: Vali Lucifer is obsessed with fighting strong opponents. He senses that Ren is stronger than Issei.
The Daily Struggle:
Vali ambushes Ren on his way to the grocery store.
 * Vali: "Ren Nocturnus! Fight me! Show me the Void!"
 * Ren: "I have frozen goods, Vali. Ice cream melts. Entropy waits for no man."
The Fight (The Loop):
Vali attacks. Ren opens a Corridor of Darkness in front of Vali's fist, with the exit portal directly behind Vali's head.
Vali punches himself in the back of the head.
 * Ren: "Stop hitting yourself, Vali."
 * Vali: "FIGHT ME PROPERLY!"
 * Ren: "I am fighting. I am fighting the urge to be late for the sale on pork cutlets."
Ren eventually gives Vali a "training arc" by tossing him into a pocket dimension filled with Shadow Clones of Vali. Vali spends a week fighting himself, loving every minute of it. Ren gets his groceries.
Arc 5: The "Harem" of the Void (The Misunderstanding)
Because Ren has zero lust and absolute honesty (Veritas), he becomes a magnet for the "difficult" women of DxD who are tired of being objectified or power-played.
 * Ophis: Likes him because he is Quiet.
 * Rossweisse (The Valkyrie): Likes him because he helps her with discount shopping (Sage wisdom applies to coupons too) and he listens to her drunken rants without judging.
 * Grayfia: Respects him because he is the only one who can make Sirzechs behave (Ren threatens to send Sirzechs to the Void if he doesn't do his paperwork).
Issei's Reaction:
Issei is the Harem King of "Passion."
Ren is the Harem King of "Therapy."
 * Issei: "Why are all the scary, powerful women hanging out at Ren's house?!"
 * Ren: "We are discussing the inevitable heat death of the universe, Issei. Also, we are playing Uno."
Arc 6: The Ultimate Flex (The Trihexa Incident)
Context: The Beast of Apocalypse, 666 (Trihexa), awakens. It threatens to destroy the world.
The Climax:
The world is ending. Rias and Issei are fighting a losing battle.
Ren sighs, rolls up his sleeves (he is wearing a "I <3 Kyoto" t-shirt).
Ren: "I live here. My stuff is here. I really don't want to move dimensions again. Moving is a hassle."
The Action:
Ren walks up to the Trihexa. The Beast roars, a sound that shatters mountains.
Ren holds up a hand. [Technique: Universal Mute Button].
The sound vanishes.
Ren expands his Corridor of Darkness‚Äînot a portal, but a blanket. He wraps the darkness around the Trihexa like a parent tucking in a child.
 * Ren: "You're cranky. Go to timeout."
   He shunts the Trihexa into the Deep Void for a few millennia to cool off.
The Aftermath:
Ren returns to the battlefield, dusting off his hands.
 * Rias: "You... you just grounded the Beast of Apocalypse?"
 * Ren: "It needs discipline. Now, did we save the school? I have a history presentation tomorrow."
üìú Branch Analysis
This creates a story that is 50% High-Octane Action and 50% Absurdist Comedy.
Ren acts as the "Straight Man" to the insanity of the DxD world.

Yes, you are correct. Route C (The Neighbor) was a direct continuation of Route B (The Sage).
If we go back to the moment Ren steps into the Corridor of Darkness‚Äîbroken, angry, and leaving his friends behind‚Äîthere are several other ways his journey through the Void could change him. Becoming a "Peaceful Sage" is just one outcome.
Here are 3 Alternative Branches for Ren‚Äôs evolution inside the Darkness.
üîÄ Branch B-2: The "King in Black" (The Conquest Route)
Concept: Instead of finding Peace in the Darkness, Ren finds Power and Vindication. He embraces the Xehanort/Organization XIII philosophy fully: "If the World rejects you, build a new World."
 * The Void Journey: Ren doesn't just walk; he conquers. He finds the "Heartless" or creatures of the Void (cosmic horrors) and instead of harmonizing with them, he subjugates them using his Will and Darkness.
 * The Evolution: He becomes a Warlord of the Void. He stops looking for a place to belong and decides to carve a place out of reality.
 * The Return: He returns to DxD not as a friend, but as a Third Faction Leader.
   * He builds his own "Peerage" made of rejected, broken villains from other dimensions or timeline remnants (e.g., a surviving Raynare, a disillusioned Vali, or forgotten characters).
   * The Conflict: He challenges the Great Satans and the Biblical God system. "Your system relies on luck and birthright. My system relies on Will."
   * The Climax: A massive war. The Gremory Peerage vs. Ren‚Äôs Organization of Shadow. Issei has to fight a Ren who believes he is "saving" the world by destroying its unfair hierarchy.
üîÄ Branch B-3: The "Abyss Walker" (The Survival Horror Route)
Concept: The Void is not kind. It is a meat grinder. Ren survives, but at the cost of his humanity. This is a much darker, Berserk-style or Dark Souls-style route.
 * The Void Journey: Ren steps into the portal and is immediately attacked by Eldritch horrors. He spends "thousands of years" fighting for his life every single second. He never sleeps. He never rests. He eats darkness to survive.
 * The Evolution: He loses his memories of "High School DxD," "Anime," and even "Ren." He becomes a primal force of survival‚ÄîThe Beast of Darkness. His body mutates; he wears armor fused to his skin made from the bones of void monsters.
 * The Return: A rift opens in Kuoh, and a "Monster" falls out. It screams and attacks everything because it perceives all "Light" as a predator.
 * The Tragedy: The ORC fights this monster. Issei realizes the monster is fighting using Ren‚Äôs old martial arts stance.
   * Issei: "Ren? Is that you inside there?"
   * The Goal: The ORC must find a way to peel back the layers of trauma and darkness to save the human buried deep inside the monster.
üîÄ Branch B-4: The "Meta-Breaker" (The Glitch Route)
Concept: Ren‚Äôs knowledge of "Anime/Manga" combined with the perspective of the Void leads to a terrifying realization: He knows he is in a story.
 * The Void Journey: In the silence of the Void, Ren sees the "strings" of the universe. He sees the "Plot Armor" protecting Issei. He sees the "Fan Service" logic governing the world.
 * The Evolution: He becomes a Nihilist. He realizes his suffering was written by an "Author" for entertainment. His "Veritas" (Truth) evolves into Meta-Awareness. He gains the power to disrupt the "Script" (Reality Warping / Glitch abilities).
 * The Return: He returns to "cancel" the show.
   * He starts deleting things that "don't make sense" or are "lazy writing."
   * He nullifies Issei‚Äôs Dress Break because "It's a stupid mechanic."
   * He prevents Rias from falling in love with Issei because "It's forced development."
 * The Conflict: He isn't evil; he wants to Free his friends from being puppets of the narrative.
   * Ren: "You don't love him, Rias. The writer made you love him. I'm here to cut the strings."
   * This is a psychological horror route where Ren tries to "Break the Fourth Wall" and the characters have to fight for their own (scripted) reality.
üó£Ô∏è Discussion
Which of these darker branches appeals to you for exploration?
 * The Warlord (King in Black): An epic faction war. Ren vs. The World.
 * The Beast (Abyss Walker): A tragic rescue mission. Issei saving Ren's soul.
 * The Glitch (Meta-Breaker): A psychological deconstruction of the Harem genre.
Or we can proceed with Route D (The Hacker/Engineer) mentioned earlier, where he never leaves but changes the system from within.

I'm more interested if you can come up more.

This is a fascinating exercise. The Void/Corridor of Darkness effectively functions as a narrative crossroads. Because it exists outside of time and space, Ren can exit anywhere, anywhen, or become anything.
Here are 4 More Distinct Branches for Ren‚Äôs evolution, ranging from Time Travel to becoming a Multiversal Mercenary.
üîÄ Branch B-5: The "Precursor" (The Time Paradox Route)
Concept: The Void is timeless. When Ren tries to leave, he takes a wrong turn and exits the Corridor 3,000 years in the past, right in the middle of the Great War between Devils, Angels, and Fallen Angels.
 * The Void Journey: It was short for him, but it displaced him temporally. He steps out into a battlefield where the Original Satans (Lucifer, Beelzebub, etc.) and God are still alive.
 * The Evolution: He is a modern human with knowledge of the future and "Darkness" powers that don't exist yet (Sacred Gears were barely being created).
   * He realizes he cannot return to the future yet. He must survive the war.
   * He becomes a mercenary legend known as "The Black Shadow of Truth." He fights for humanity, protecting human villages from being crushed by the three factions.
   * He meets Ddraig and Albion (the dragons) before they were sealed. He earns their respect not with power, but with his "Veritas"‚Äîtelling them honestly that their fight is pointless.
 * The Return (The Twist):
   * In the present day, Issei and the ORC are studying history. They find an ancient text mentioning a "Human who wielded Shadow."
   * The Reunion: Ren doesn't "return" via portal. He has been waiting the long way around. He reveals himself as an ancient, immortal figure (kept alive by Darkness) who has been watching over the Gremory line for generations, waiting for Issei to be born so he can finally say "hello" again.
   * Ren: "I waited 3,000 years for you to be born, Issei. You're late."
üîÄ Branch B-6: The "Architect of Sanctuary" (The Utopia Route)
Concept: Ren realizes that "seeking a place where he belongs" is selfish. He decides to build a place where everyone who feels like him belongs. He embraces the Kingdom Hearts concept of "The World That Never Was."
 * The Void Journey: Ren finds a pocket of stable reality inside the Void. He uses his Darkness to sculpt it. He builds a city‚Äîa grey, neon-lit, eternal city (resembling Shibuya or The World That Never Was).
 * The Evolution: He becomes The Architect. He starts kidnapping/rescuing "rejects" from the DxD world before they are killed.
   * Stray Devils: Devils who were abused by their masters and went stray? Ren pulls them into his city before the executioners catch them.
   * Failed Experiments: Products of the Holy Sword project (like Kiba's friends)? Ren snatches their souls right before death and gives them new bodies of Darkness.
 * The Return: The Gremory Peerage is hunting a Stray Devil. They corner it. Suddenly, Ren appears.
   * Ren: "This one is broken, Rias. You see a criminal. I see a victim."
   * He offers the Stray a choice: "Die by the Light, or live in the Grey."
   * The Conflict: Ren isn't fighting to destroy the world; he is fighting for Jurisdiction. He claims all "Broken Things" belong to him. Issei has to decide if he agrees with Ren's "Safety" or Rias's "Justice."
üîÄ Branch B-7: The "Multiversal Mercenary" (The Bounty Hunter Route)
Concept: Ren treats the Corridor of Darkness like a subway system. He realizes there are infinite worlds, and he can get paid in skills or power to solve problems in them.
 * The Void Journey: Ren travels to "Echoes" of other worlds (inspired by his anime knowledge). He doesn't meet the actual Goku, but he goes to a martial arts world and learns Ki. He goes to a magic world and learns Grimoires.
 * The Evolution: He becomes "The Drifter." He wears a patchwork of gear from different realities. A cloak from a fantasy world, boots from a sci-fi world, a sword from a cultivation world. He is a jack-of-all-trades master of none, but his toolbox is infinite.
 * The Return: He returns to DxD essentially as a Fixer for Hire.
   * Azazel (Governor of Fallen Angels) hires him because Ren can go places no one else can.
   * Scenario: Chaos Brigade attacks. Ren steps out of a portal holding a futuristic railgun in one hand and a cultivation talisman in the other.
   * Issei: "Where did you get a laser cannon?!"
   * Ren: "Job in Sector 9. They paid me in tech. Cover me, I need to calibrate the targeting matrix."
   * He is the "Cool, World-Weary Professional" who treats the apocalypse like a Tuesday shift.
üîÄ Branch B-8: The "Great Filter" (The Jailer Route)
Concept: This is the Cosmic Horror Hero route. Ren realizes that the Corridor of Darkness connects to the ExE world (the world of mechanical gods and invaders in DxD lore) or something worse.
 * The Void Journey: Ren tries to leave, but he sees Something trying to get IN. A horde of Lovecraftian entities trying to invade the DxD reality through the cracks in the dimension.
 * The Evolution: Ren realizes that if he leaves, the door opens. So he stays. He becomes The Warden.
   * He fights an eternal war at the edge of reality to keep the monsters out. He uses his Darkness to patch the cracks in the universe.
 * The Return: He never fully returns. Instead, his "Projection" appears to warn them.
   * Ren's Avatar: "Issei. Rias. Something is coming. I can't hold the North Gate forever."
   * The Arc: The Gremory Peerage has to travel into the Void to help Ren. They find him there‚Äîaged, scarred, sitting on a throne of pile-driver corpses of monsters, looking exhausted.
   * Ren: "You guys took your time. I've been holding the line for six centuries (relative time)."
   * It redeems him completely‚Äîhe didn't leave because he was weak; he stayed away to protect them from a threat they didn't even know existed.
üß† Analysis of Options
 * B-5 (Time Paradox) provides deep lore integration and emotional payoff (The "I waited for you" trope).
 * B-6 (Sanctuary) challenges the morality of the Devil system and makes Ren a political rival.
 * B-7 (Mercenary) allows for maximum "Cool Factor" and utilizing his anime knowledge in a literal way.
 * B-8 (Jailer) makes him the ultimate unsung hero.
Which of these "What Ifs" resonates most with the "Veritas" (Truth) theme you prefer?

That was fun, we'll save them all for now. Let's go back to Ariel related to divergence. Do you think Ariel have to leave to produce this what if scenarios or not?

That is a fascinating narrative design question. The short answer is: No, Ariel does not have to leave to generate "What If" scenarios.
While Ren‚Äôs divergences are born from Escapism (leaving because he hates his reality), Ariel‚Äôs divergences can be born from Evolution (changing the reality he is in).
Because Ariel is the Mortal Variable and acts as a "Stabilizer" or "Teacher," his presence is the divergence point. However, we can certainly create branches based on how he interacts with the world or where his training takes him.
Here are 4 Divergence Branches for Ariel that do not require him to abandon his friends in despair, but rather change the fate of the world in drastic ways.
üåå Branch A: The "Uncrowned King" (The Political Divergence)
Concept: Ariel stays in Kuoh. He never leaves. He creates a permanent Third Faction within the DxD world, separate from Devils, Angels, or Fallen.
 * The Trigger: Instead of just training the ORC, Ariel realizes that the "System" of DxD (Rating Games, Peerage servitude) is fundamentally flawed because it relies on race/bloodline.
 * The Evolution: Ariel founds "The Veritas Order" (or simply "The Dojo").
   * It is a faction for Humans who refuse to be reincarnated.
   * He teaches Haki and Martial Arts to humans who were rejected by Sacred Gears.
 * The Conflict: The Devils (specifically the Old Satan Faction or strict traditionalists) view a rising Human Faction as a threat.
   * Rias is torn between her loyalty to her Devil family and her loyalty to Ariel.
   * The Climax: The Great War restarts, but it‚Äôs a 4-way war. Ariel leads an army of "Haki Users" (Mortals) to force the supernatural world to sign a peace treaty that respects humanity.
 * Outcome: Ariel becomes the "King of Humans," a figure equal to Sirzechs Lucifer, proving that a Mortal can rule without magic.
üåå Branch B: The "Digital Ascendant" (The Sci-Fi Divergence)
Concept: Ariel dives too deep into the PTD (Personal Training Dossier). He doesn't leave physically, but his existence shifts.
 * The Trigger: To fight a cosmic threat (like Trihexa or ExE invaders), Ariel realizes his physical body (\text{PHY} \text{ } 2.0) has a hard limit. He cannot punch a star. So, he decides to merge with the System.
 * The Evolution: Ariel uploads his consciousness into the PTD permanently. He becomes a Living AI / Egregore.
   * He can manifest anywhere in the world as a hard-light hologram.
   * He can "hack" the Rating Game fields, the Sacred Gear systems, and even the laws of physics in the Underworld.
 * The "What If": He is everywhere and nowhere. He becomes the System Administrator of DxD.
   * He fixes Issei‚Äôs traumatic memories by editing the code.
   * He deletes the "Evil Pieces" glitches.
 * The Cost: He loses his physical humanity. He can no longer eat taiyaki or feel a hug. He is the Ghost in the Machine watching over his friends eternally.
üåå Branch C: The "Dimensional Pilgrim" (The Goku Route)
Concept: This is the closest to "Leaving," but the motivation is different. Ren left because he hated DxD. Ariel leaves because he has conquered DxD and needs a stronger gym.
 * The Trigger: Ariel defeats high-tier opponents (Sairaorg, Cao Cao, etc.). He realizes he has hit the "Level Cap" of the DxD universe. The PTD simulations of Goku are no longer enough; he needs the real thing.
 * The Departure: He holds a graduation party. He tells Rias and Issei, "I'll be back. I'm just going for a training trip."
   * He uses the PTD to engineer a Dimension Hop.
 * The Journey:
   * He travels to the One Piece world to learn Haki from the source.
   * He travels to the Dragon Ball world to learn Ki control.
 * The Return: He returns years later during the Trihexa Apocalypse.
   * He steps out of a portal wearing a Turtle Hermit Gi and a Straw Hat.
   * He one-shots the Beast of Apocalypse.
   * He tosses Issei a Senzu Bean.
   * Ariel: "Sorry I'm late. Traffic in the Multiverse is terrible."
üåå Branch D: The "Time-Lost Mentor" (The Paradox Route)
Concept: An accident with the PTD sends Ariel back to the Biblical War Era (God vs. Original Satans).
 * The Trigger: During a high-stress simulation involving Time/Space manipulation (trying to simulate Hit from Dragon Ball Super), the PTD malfunctions and displaces him physically.
 * The Evolution: Ariel is stranded 2,000+ years in the past.
   * He cannot return. He decides to live his life.
   * He meets the Biblical God. He trains the original Vanishing Dragon and Welsh Dragon.
   * He becomes the legend known as "The Peacemaker."
 * The Twist: In the present day, Issei meets a mysterious, ancient janitor at Kuoh Academy who gives him cryptic advice.
   * Eventually, Issei realizes this old man knows everything about him.
   * The "What If" reveals that Ariel has been secretly guiding the Gremory family from the shadows for centuries, ensuring Rias and Issei would eventually meet.
Summary
Ariel does not need to be a "Seeker of Darkness" to generate scenarios.
 * Ren's Variants are about Where he goes (to find a place he belongs).
 * Ariel's Variants are about What he becomes (King, Machine, Traveler, or Myth).
Do any of these "Ariel Branches" spark an idea for a future scenario? Or should we focus on the "Part-Time Sage" Ren scenario for now?

Back to Ren. Ren's climax was after Riser arc. What other ideas do you have with only scope as the dark seeker?

Restricting the scope to Ren Nocturnus Veritas specifically as the Dark Seeker (using the Kingdom Hearts / Xehanort / Sasuke archetype) immediately following his departure creates a fascinating, darker narrative tree.
He has stepped into the Corridor of Darkness. He has rejected the "Light" of the DxD world (Devils, Angels, Heroes). He is now a traveler of the Void.
Here are 4 Divergent Branches focusing solely on his evolution as a Seeker of Darkness.
üåë Branch 1: The Student of Silence (The Ophis Route)
Concept: Ren seeks the ultimate form of "Nothingness." In the DxD universe, the being that represents infinite silence and the void is Ophis, the Ouroboros Dragon.
 * The Encounter: Ren wanders the Dimensional Gap (the void between worlds). Most humans die instantly here. Ren survives because he accepts the toxicity of the environment. He attracts the attention of Ophis.
 * The Bond: Ophis usually uses people (The Khaos Brigade) for her goals. However, she finds Ren interesting because he doesn't want power, money, or status. He wants what she wants: Quiet.
 * The Evolution: Ren becomes Ophis‚Äôs Sole Disciple.
   * He doesn't get a "Snake" power-up like the other villains.
   * Instead, he learns to wield the Power of Infinity (Infinity minus existence = Void).
   * He becomes the "Anti-Issei." Issei is the Red Dragon (Dreams/Passion). Ren is the Grey Knight (Silence/Void).
 * The Conflict: Ren returns not as a villain, but as Ophis‚Äôs guardian. He dismantles the Khaos Brigade from the inside because "They are too loud." He eventually clashes with Issei because Ren believes the only way to save the world is to return it to silence.
üåë Branch 2: The Lord of the Hollows (The "Nobody" Route)
Concept: Ren embraces the Organization XIII philosophy completely. He decides that if the world is ruled by those with "Hearts" (Passions/Sacred Gears), he will build an army of those without them.
 * The Creation: Inside the Darkness, Ren learns to mold the void into physical forms. He discovers the "Shadows" of the DxD world‚Äîthe resentment of Stray Devils, the despair of failed Holy Sword subjects, the forgotten victims of the Great War.
 * The Evolution: Ren creates "The Hollow Peerage" (mirroring the Nobodies).
   * He doesn't use Evil Pieces. He uses Shards of Void.
   * He recruits people who have "lost their hearts" to tragedy.
   * Example: He finds a timeline where Kiba succumbed to hatred, or where Koneko was executed. He pulls their "Shadows" into his service.
 * The Goal: He builds a citadel in the Dimension Gap called The Castle That Never Was. His goal is to capture the Biblical God's System and rewrite it so that "Effort" is the only metric of power, deleting the concept of "Talent" or "Sacred Gears" entirely.
 * The Climax: A tragic war where the Gremory Peerage has to fight "Hollow" versions of people they know, led by the man who knows all their weaknesses.
üåë Branch 3: The Abyss Walker (The Survival/Mutation Route)
Concept: This leans into the Dark Souls / Artorias vibe. The Darkness is not a tool; it is a radioactive ocean. Ren survives, but it changes him physically and fundamentally.
 * The Corruption: Ren tries to master the Darkness, but he has no master. He makes mistakes. The Darkness eats his left arm. He replaces it with a construct of pure condensed shadow (like a monstrous claw).
 * The Evolution: He becomes a cryptid‚Äîa monster that hunts monsters. He wanders the lower levels of the Underworld and the Dimensional Gap, hunting Stray Devils and Eldritch Beasts.
   * He consumes their darkness to sustain himself.
   * He loses his ability to speak normally; his voice becomes a chorus of whispers.
 * The Encounter: The Gremory Peerage is sent to hunt a "New S-Class Threat" in the deep Underworld. They find a creature clad in tattered black rags, wielding a jagged shadow-blade, slaughtering a legion of monsters.
 * The Tragedy: Issei recognizes Ren‚Äôs fighting stance.
   * Ren: "Run... Issei... the hunger... is loud..."
   * Ren has become the very thing he sought to control. The arc becomes a rescue mission: Can they pull Ren out of the Abyss before he loses his humanity completely?
üåë Branch 4: The Shadow Broker (The Veritas Route)
Concept: Ren leans fully into his name "Veritas" (Truth). He realizes that "Light" (The Devil/Angel factions) rely on secrets and lies to maintain peace. He uses the Darkness to expose the ugly truth of the world.
 * The Method: The Corridor of Darkness connects to everywhere. Ren uses it to spy on everyone. He enters the Vatican's secret archives. He listens to Sirzechs Lucifer's private meetings. He watches Azazel's experiments.
 * The Evolution: He becomes "The Speaker". He is a neutral, chaotic force who leaks information to cause chaos.
   * He reveals the truth about God's death to the Church early, causing a civil war.
   * He reveals the corruption of the Devil Council to the lower devils.
 * The Philosophy: "The Light blinds you with pretty lies. I offer the ugly Truth in the Dark."
 * The Conflict: He isn't trying to destroy the world physically; he is destroying its society.
   * Rias tries to stop him because his leaks are causing wars.
   * Ren counters: "You call it peace; I call it a cage built of lies. I'm just turning on the lights, Rias."
   * This sets up a philosophical battle: Issei (Hope/Order) vs. Ren (Truth/Chaos).
Summary of Options
 * Student of Silence: Ren teams up with the Dragon God Ophis to quiet the world.
 * Lord of Hollows: Ren builds a counter-organization of "rejects" to rewrite the laws of physics.
 * Abyss Walker: Ren becomes a tragic, mutated monster hunter fighting for his sanity.
 * Shadow Broker: Ren uses the Darkness to spy on the world and destroy the "Lies" of the factions.
Which of these darker paths for the Seeker interests you most?

Suppose we do not restrict the departure time to after Riser, when else do you think can be use for departute time?

Changing the departure time drastically alters the flavor of Ren's tragedy. The Post-Riser departure is about "Jealousy of Success." Other departure points can explore "Fear of Uselessness," "Despair at Destiny," or "Ideological Rejection."
Here are 3 Alternative Departure Times that fit the High School DxD timeline, each creating a different psychological break for Ren.
1. The "Holy Sword" Departure (Volume 3 / Kokabiel Arc)
Context: This is the arc where Kiba deals with his trauma, and Vali Lucifer (The White Dragon Emperor) makes his debut.
 * The Setup: Ren watches Kiba gain his Balance Breaker (Sword of Betrayer). He watches Issei gain his Balance Breaker. Then, Vali Lucifer arrives and effortlessly crushes Kokabiel (a Cadre class Fallen Angel) like an insect.
 * The Trigger (The Power Gap): Ren realizes that the world isn't just about "Hard Work" vs. "Talent." It‚Äôs about Cosmic Destiny. Issei and Vali are destined rivals. Kiba is a survivor of a holy project. Ren looks at himself and realizes he isn't even a pawn on the chessboard; he is part of the board itself, meant to be stepped on.
 * The Departure Moment:
   * While the ORC is recovering from the Kokabiel fight, staring at the destruction caused by the Dragons.
   * Ren: "Dragons. Devils. Angels. You're all monsters playing with the world."
   * Action: Ren approaches Vali Lucifer before he leaves.
   * Ren: "Take me with you. Or kill me. I refuse to be an ant anymore."
   * Outcome: Ren doesn't open a portal immediately. He leaves with the Khaos Brigade (Vali Team) to learn the secrets of power, only to betray them later when he finds the true Darkness (The Void) is stronger than Dragon power.
2. The "Underworld Training" Departure (Volume 5 / Tanning Training)
Context: The Gremory Peerage goes to the Underworld to train with Tannin (The Dragon King) to prepare for the Rating Game against Sairaorg.
 * The Setup: Issei is surviving hellish training in the mountains with a Dragon King. Ren tries to follow. He climbs the mountain. He tries to fight the lower-level dragons.
 * The Trigger (The Biological Wall): Ren pushes his human body until his muscles literally tear and his bones fracture. Tannin looks at him and says the brutal truth (Veritas): "Go home, human. You have no vessel to hold power. You will break before you bend."
 * The Departure Moment:
   * Alone in the mountains of the Underworld, broken and rejected by the "Light" (Dragon/Devil training).
   * Ren finds a cave. Inside is not a dragon, but a rift in the dimension.
   * Ren: "If the world of matter rejects me... I'll embrace the world of nothing."
   * Action: He steps into the rift voluntarily. When the Gremory group comes to find him, all they find is his training gear left neatly folded in the cave. He didn't leave them; he left existence.
3. The "Juggernaut Drive" Departure (Volume 6 / Shalba Arc)
Context: Asia is "killed" by Shalba Beelzebub. Issei falls into despair and activates the Juggernaut Drive, becoming a mindless beast of destruction that consumes his own life.
 * The Setup: Ren watches his best friend turn into a monster. He feels the overwhelming, chaotic, chaotic energy of the Juggernaut Drive. It terrifies him.
 * The Trigger (The Rejection of Chaos): Ren realizes that "Passion" and "Love" (Issei's power sources) lead to madness and pain. He sees Issei suffering and decides that feeling things is the weakness. He adopts the Xehanort Philosophy: "Darkness is order. Darkness is silent. Darkness doesn't hurt."
 * The Departure Moment:
   * After Issei is calmed down and returned to normal (usually thanks to Oppai or Rias). The group is crying, emotional, and exhausted.
   * Ren stands apart, cold and detached.
   * Ren: "Look at you. Crying. Bleeding. Dying for love. It's pathetic."
   * Action: He opens the Corridor of Darkness right there on the battlefield.
   * Ren: "I'm going to a place where hearts don't break, Issei. Because they don't exist."
   * Outcome: This makes Ren a Cold/Emotionless Villain (Nobody archetype) who tries to strip the world of emotion to "save" it from pain.
‚öñÔ∏è Summary
 * Post-Riser (Original): Motivated by Jealousy/Envy. (Personal tragedy).
 * Post-Kokabiel: Motivated by Insignificance. (Existential crisis).
 * Underworld Training: Motivated by Physical Limitation. (The limit of the body).
 * Post-Juggernaut: Motivated by Fear of Emotion. (Ideological shift).
Which timing do you think hurts the team the most?

In all those alternatives or other alternatives, are Sasuke vibe where Ren was hindered to the void or darkness and Ren defeated them with power of void or darkness not possible or not feasible? Other than Sasuke, even Xehanort have similar vibes when he uses the power of Darkness to defeat Eraqus before departure.

It is absolutely possible and, in fact, creates a much more intense dramatic impact.
The "Sasuke/Xehanort" departure vibe relies on a specific dynamic: The Sudden Gap. The heroes think they are strong because they just won a battle, but then the "friend" reveals a power that feels ancient, alien, and overwhelming (Darkness/Void), crushing them effortlessly to prove that their path is different.
Here is how Ren can defeat the ORC in those alternative timelines using the Power of Darkness to force his departure.
üåë Scenario 1: Post-Kokabiel (The "Ant" Crushes the Elephant)
Context: The ORC is battered after the fight with Kokabiel (Volume 3). Vali Lucifer has just appeared, flexed his power, and is about to leave. The ORC is demoralized but standing.
The Setup:
Ren walks out from the debris. He hasn't fought Kokabiel. He has been watching, letting the Despair of the situation unlock his Darkness.
The "Sasuke" Moment:
Ren declares he is leaving to find real power. Rias and Issei try to stop him.
 * Ren's Power: Void Gravity / Corrupting Pressure.
 * The Fight:
   * Issei charges: "Ren, don't be stupid!"
   * Ren doesn't move. He glares. [Technique: Dark Impulse].
   * A massive shockwave of violet-black energy erupts from Ren. It doesn't burn; it feels like gravity increased by 50x.
   * Issei is slammed face-first into the dirt. His Boosted Gear flickers and dies because the Darkness "suffocates" the Dragon aura.
   * Kiba tries to speed-blitz. Ren raises a hand, and Shadows erupt from the ground (like Xehanort grabbing Eraqus), binding Kiba‚Äôs limbs and slamming him into a wall.
   * Rias tries to fire destruction magic. Ren simply catches the blast in his bare hand (coated in dense Darkness) and crushing it.
 * The Departure:
   Ren stands over the prone Issei.
   Ren: "You rely on a dragon to stand up. I rely on the void to hold me."
   Vali Lucifer (watching): "Hoh? Interesting human. You have the eyes of a seeker."
   Ren ignores Vali and steps into the Corridor of Darkness.
üåë Scenario 2: Underworld Training (The Shadow of the Mountain)
Context: The Gremory Peerage is training in the mountains with Tannin (Volume 5). They are exhausted from physical labor.
The Setup:
Ren has been missing for days. He returns from the deep caves, his coat torn, but his aura completely silent. He tells them he is done with "Devil Games."
The "Xehanort" Moment:
Rias orders the peerage to restrain him for his own safety, thinking he has gone insane from the cave gases.
 * Ren's Power: Shadow Doppelgangers / Possession.
 * The Fight:
   * Koneko lunges. Ren melts into the floor. He reappears inside Koneko's shadow. He strikes her pressure point with a blade of darkness. She collapses instantly.
   * Akeno rains lightning. Ren summons a Guardian (a massive, shadowy figure behind him, like Xehanort‚Äôs stand/Susanoo). The Guardian absorbs the lightning and fires it back as Black Lightning.
   * Issei activates Balance Breaker. Ren looks him in the eye.
   * Ren: "Sleep."
   * Ren channels pure Mental Darkness (Veritas of Despair) directly into Issei‚Äôs mind. Issei is trapped in a nightmare illusion of Rias dying. He freezes, screaming.
 * The Departure:
   Ren walks past them while they are writhing in nightmares or pinned by their own shadows.
   Ren: "The Light casts shadows. But the Shadows can swallow the Light. Goodbye, Gremory."
üåë Scenario 3: Post-Juggernaut (The Severed Bond)
Context: Issei has just recovered from the Juggernaut Drive (Volume 6). He is physically weak and terrified of his own power. The mood is fragile.
The Setup:
Ren watches them crying over Issei. He is disgusted by the weakness of "Love" causing Issei to go berserk. He decides to leave to seek the "Order" of the Void.
The "Sasuke at the Valley of the End" Moment:
Ren opens the portal. Rias and the healthy members (Kiba, Xenovia) try to block his path.
 * Ren's Power: Entropy / Keyblade-Style Constructs.
 * The Fight:
   * Xenovia strikes with Durandal. Ren summons a Blade of Void (resembling Riku's Soul Eater or a Dark Keyblade). He parries the Holy Sword. The collision causes Durandal‚Äôs light to dim.
   * Ren: "Even Holy swords rust in the dark."
   * He slashes the air, creating Rifts. These rifts fire homing projectiles of dark energy (like Sasuke's Fireball technique but purple).
   * He blitzes Kiba. Ren isn't faster, but he uses Corridor Steps (teleporting through darkness). He appears behind Kiba, kicks him into Xenovia, and then slams his hand onto the ground.
   * [Technique: Eclipsing Zone].
   * A dome of darkness covers the area. Inside, the Devils lose their senses. They are blind and deaf. Ren walks through them, casually knocking them unconscious with precision strikes.
 * The Departure:
   He reaches the exit. Issei crawls towards him, weak.
   Ren looks back, eyes glowing faintly violet (Xehanort style).
   Ren: "Don't follow me, Issei. The next time we meet, I won't be holding back the blade."
üß† Why This Works for Ren
In all these scenarios, Ren wins because he introduces a Foreign Power System (The Void/Darkness) that the DxD characters don't have a resistance to yet.
 * Devils resist Magic.
 * Dragons resist Force.
 * Ren uses Erasure/Entropy. He attacks their stamina and their senses directly.
This makes his departure valid. He doesn't just run away; he dominates them to prove that his new path (The Seeker) is valid, justifying his choice to leave.
Do you want to write the Post-Kokabiel scenario in detail? That one offers a great interaction with Vali and a very Sasuke-esque "I'm leaving this village" vibe.

Let's explore variations of Ren's route C. True he's aim is to become a sage but what if he reunites when not yet completely sage? He ofcourse able to endure and embrace the corridor of darkness. Let's say variations (1) first step in become a sage, just few years in corridor of darkness and other realities, (2) a decade, (3) decades, and (4) centuries. Not thousand of years yet but same saving a member of ORC during his daily stroll in corridor of darkness. He chose to visit ORC also.

This exploration of the "Intermediate Stages" of Ren's evolution adds incredible nuance. Instead of jumping straight to the enlightened Buddha-like figure, we see the grit, the scars, and the gradual shedding of his humanity.
Here are the 4 Variations of Route C, charting Ren‚Äôs return at different stages of his exposure to the Void. In all scenarios, the catalyst is finding Ravel Phenex (or another member) lost in the Corridor of Darkness.
üåë Route C (Variations): The Degrees of Darkness
The Constant:
 * The Incident: Ravel Phenex falls into a dimensional crack during a Rating Game.
 * The Rescue: Ren finds her. He is immune to the Void; she is dying from it.
 * The Return: Ren brings her back to the Hyoudou Residence.
1. The "Ronin" (Time in Void: ~3‚Äì5 Years)
State: Hardened Survivor / The Edgelord
Concept: Ren is still raw. He has conquered the immediate pain of the Void, but he carries the chip on his shoulder. He is jagged, dangerous, and looks like someone who has been in a knife fight for three years straight.
 * Appearance: His Organization XIII coat is tattered and shredded at the hem. He has visible scars on his face. His eyes are constantly darting, scanning for threats (Hyper-Vigilance). He carries a Keyblade of pure jagged obsidian that looks unstable.
 * The Entrance: He kicks the dimensional door open violently. He drops Ravel on the couch like a sack of potatoes. He is breathing hard, radiating "Killing Intent."
   * Ren: "She's alive. Don't ask me how. Just heal her."
 * The Interaction: Issei tries to hug him. Ren flinches and instinctively draws his blade.
   * Ren: "Don't touch me, Issei. The static on you... it burns."
 * Why He Stays: He doesn't stay for "Peace." He stays because he is Exhausted.
   * Ren: "My apartment still empty? Good. I need to sleep for a week in a place where the gravity doesn't try to eat my bones."
 * The Dynamic: He is the Grumpy Anti-Hero. He insults their fighting styles ("You're still wide open, Kiba"), eats their food without asking, and treats the supernatural threats with disdain. He visits to remind himself he won his survival, still seeking validation that he is strong now.
2. The "Warden" (Time in Void: ~10 Years)
State: The Professional / The Mercenary
Concept: The anger is gone, replaced by cold efficiency. Ren treats the Void like a job. He has built a fortress in his mind. He is no longer "Issei's Friend"; he is a Veteran of a War they didn't know was happening.
 * Appearance: Clean, tactical use of Darkness. His coat is replaced by armor made of condensed shadow (resembling Berserk armor but lighter). He moves with military precision. He doesn't look tired; he looks locked-in.
 * The Entrance: A silent portal slides open. Ren steps out, scanning the room tactically. He lays Ravel down and immediately checks her pulse and vitals with clinical detachment.
   * Ren: "Subject secured. Entropy exposure: 40%. Recovery probable."
 * The Interaction: Issei is intimidated. Ren feels like a stranger‚Äîan adult visiting children.
   * Issei: "Ren... you look... solid."
   * Ren: "The Void demands structure, Issei. If you aren't solid, you dissolve. You haven't changed much. Still rely on the Dragon to hold your shape?"
 * Why He Stays: He views the DxD world as a "Supply Station."
   * Ren: "I'm low on coffee and physical ammunition. I'll remain in this dimension for 48 hours to resupply. Do not disturb my perimeter."
 * The Dynamic: He is the Cold Professional. He gives tactical advice but refuses to get emotionally involved. He is "The Neighbor" who calls the cops on loud noises. He is intimidatingly competent.
3. The "Drifter" (Time in Void: ~40‚Äì60 Years)
State: The Melancholic Wanderer / The Lost Soul
Concept: Time has started to blur. Ren remembers who they are, but they feel like distant memories from a childhood he barely recalls. He has seen civilizations rise and fall in other realities. He is lonely, but accustomed to it.
 * Appearance: He looks unkempt but soft. Long hair, loose grey robes. He holds a staff made of petrified void-wood. His aura is heavy, sad, and quiet (like a fog).
 * The Entrance: The room grows cold and damp. Ren wanders out, looking confused, holding Ravel gently. He looks around the Hyoudou living room like he's walking through a museum.
   * Ren: "This place... I remember this smell. Miso soup? It's been... a very long time."
 * The Interaction: He looks at Issei and smiles, but it doesn't reach his eyes.
   * Ren: "Issei... Hyoudou. The Red Dragon. You look so young. In my head, you were a giant. Now... you're just a boy."
   * Rias: "Ren, it's only been two years for us."
   * Ren: "Has it? Time is a flat circle in the deep. Two years... sixty years... it all tastes like ash."
 * Why He Stays: Nostalgia. He is afraid he is forgetting his humanity.
   * Ren: "May I sit? I just want to watch you live for a while. I need to remember what 'colors' look like."
 * The Dynamic: He is the Sad Uncle. He sits in the corner, drinking tea, telling stories about dead stars. He is gentle but distant. The ORC feels a desperate need to cheer him up because he radiates "Deep depression held in check by duty."
4. The "Proto-Sage" (Time in Void: ~300‚Äì500 Years)
State: The Transcendent / The Entity
Concept: He is no longer human, but he hasn't reached the "Infinite Calm" of the 5,000-year Sage yet. He is an Entity of the Void. He finds human concerns adorable and petty. He creates the closest vibe to the "Route C" ending but with more alien detachment.
 * Appearance: He floats slightly off the ground. His eyes are entirely black (no whites), or they reflect nebulae. He wears clothes that shift texture. He doesn't walk; reality folds around him.
 * The Entrance: He manifests instantly. No portal. One moment empty space, the next moment Ren. He places Ravel down and pats her head like a pet.
   * Ren: "There. The little spark is safe. She was loud in the quiet."
 * The Interaction: He treats the Gremory Peerage like toddlers.
   * Issei: "Ren! You're back!"
   * Ren: "I never left, Issei. I am merely intersecting with your X-Y-Z axis again. Your perception of 'here' is very limited."
   * Issei: "...What?"
   * Ren: "Exactly."
 * Why He Stays: Curiosity / Amusement.
   * Ren: "This reality is vibrating at a funny frequency. It tickles. I think I shall observe it until the sensation passes. Do you still make that 'Pizza' substance? I require an offering."
 * The Dynamic: He is the Cryptic God-Neighbor. He solves problems with a snap of his fingers but complains about mundane things.
   * "I can rewrite the laws of gravity, Rias, but I cannot understand why the toaster burns my bagel. Explain this technology."
