Which "Ren" do you want to see interact with the current timeline?

Eloborate drifter.

This elaboration focuses on the heavy emotional weight and the "Time Dilation" tragedy of The Drifter. This version of Ren is not a cool action hero or a funny sage; he is a Ghost of the Future haunting the present.
Here is the detailed dossier and narrative expansion for Ren Nocturnus Veritas: The Drifter.
üåë Variation 3: The Drifter (The Man Who Walked Too Far)
Subject: Ren Nocturnus Veritas
Relative Age: ~19 (Physical Appearance) / ~70-80 (Mental Age)
Time in Void: Approximately 50‚Äì60 Years (Subjective)
Current Status: Visiting / "Anchoring"
1. The Aesthetic of the Lost
When Ren steps out of the portal, he doesn't look like the edgy teenager who left. He looks like a traveler who has crossed a desert that never ends.
 * The Eyes: This is the most striking feature. They are "Old Man Eyes" set in a young face. They are cloudy, distant, and rarely blink. When he looks at Issei, he looks through him, as if Issei is a fading memory he‚Äôs trying to hold onto.
 * The Gear: The Organization XIII coat is gone.
   * He wears layers of tattered grey fabric‚Äîscraps of reality he found in the Void.
   * His boots are wrapped in void-leather bindings.
   * He leans heavily on a Staff of Petrified Darkness (a walking stick made from a crystallized elder beast he killed decades ago).
 * The Aura: He smells like ozone, stale air, and old books. The air around him feels damp and heavy, inducing a feeling of sudden, deep nostalgia in anyone standing too close.
2. The Reunion: "Ghosts of a Past Life"
Scene: The Hyoudou Living Room.
Ren has just laid Ravel on the couch. He stands there, gripping his staff, looking around the room with profound confusion.
Issei: (Rushing forward) "Ren! You're back! We were so worried!"
Issei grabs Ren‚Äôs shoulder.
Ren flinches violently, pulling away and raising his staff defensively. His eyes widen, wild for a second, before settling back into dull recognition.
Ren: "Issei... Hyoudou?"
His voice is raspy, like he hasn't used it in years. He reaches out a trembling hand and touches Issei‚Äôs face, checking if he is solid.
Ren: "You're so... vivid. Bright red. Loud. I remember you being loud."
Rias: "Ren, it's only been two years. Why are you acting like this?"
Ren looks at Rias, then at the clock on the wall. He lets out a long, shuddering breath and sinks onto the floor (ignoring the chair).
Ren: "Two years here. Sixty years there. The currents were... slow. I spent a decade just walking through a grey fog to find the exit. I forgot what 'colors' looked like until I saw Ravel's fire."
The room goes silent. The tragedy hits them. Their friend didn't just leave; he lived an entire lifetime in hellish isolation while they were finishing high school.
3. The Psychology: "Anchoring"
The Drifter stays not because he wants to rejoin the team, but because he is terrified of Dissociating. He is losing his grip on his humanity.
 * Sensory Overload:
   * Ren spends hours just touching textures. He will stare at a wooden table for twenty minutes, running his finger over the grain.
   * Ren: "Wood. Solid. Rough. Good."
   * He eats slowly, savoring plain rice like it's a 5-star meal.
 * Memory Loss (The Veritas):
   * He is honest about what he has forgotten.
   * Koneko: "Do you remember when you broke my arm?"
   * Ren: "No. I remember I hurt you. I remember the regret. But I don't remember your face from back then. In my head... you're all just silhouettes of light."
   * This honesty breaks their hearts, but it forces them to re-introduce themselves to him.
4. Combat Style: "The Path of Least Resistance"
The Drifter doesn't fight to win; he fights to end the noise. He is tired. His style reflects extreme efficiency born of exhaustion.
 * The "Fog" Defense:
   * When attacked, Ren doesn't block. He exhales Dark Mist.
   * Issei tries to spar with him. Issei punches Ren, but his fist passes through Ren's body as if he is made of smoke. Ren has partially shifted his molecular structure into the Void.
 * The "Banishment" Offense:
   * Ren doesn't punch. He uses his staff to open micro-rifts.
   * A monster attacks. Ren taps his staff. Click.
   * The floor opens up, swallows the monster, and closes.
   * Ren: "Go away. I'm tired."
 * The "Weight of Years":
   * His ultimate move. He projects his Memory of the Void into the opponent.
   * The opponent experiences 60 years of isolation in 1 second. They collapse, catatonic and weeping.
5. The Dynamic with the Harem
Because he is an "Old Man" in a young body, the girls treat him differently.
 * Asia: She becomes his caretaker. She brings him tea and sits with him while he stares at the wall.
   * Ren: "You are warm, Asia. Like a sun that doesn't burn."
 * Akeno: She tries to tease him, but it fails.
   * Akeno: "Ara ara, Ren-kun, do you need a bath?"
   * Ren: "I haven't bathed in water for four decades. I usually just scour my skin with abrasive void-sand. Hot water sounds... painful. But acceptable."
   * Akeno stops teasing and genuinely helps him because he's just sad.
 * Issei: Issei stops being jealous of Ren. He starts being fiercely protective.
   * Issei: "Nobody bothers Ren today! He's watching the clouds! Let him watch the clouds!"
   * Issei realizes his friend paid a price for power that wasn't worth it, and tries to give Ren the "youth" he lost.
6. The "Drifter's" Goal
Ren isn't seeking power anymore. He is seeking Re-calibration.
 * The Objective: He wants to remember how to be Ren Nocturnus. He treats his stay at the Hyoudou residence as "Rehabilitation."
 * The Ending of the Arc:
   * Eventually, the Void calls him back. He hears the whisper.
   * Ren: "I have to go, Issei. The fog is lifting in Sector 9. I have a garden of shadow-lilies I need to tend to."
   * Issei: "Will you come back?"
   * Ren: "Yes. Time is tricky. But I left an anchor here." (He points to a small, black stone he left on the table). "As long as that's here, I can find my way back to the noise."
Summary:
The Drifter is a tragic figure who serves as a living warning to the ORC about the cost of ambition. He is powerful, yes‚Äîhe can banish gods with a wave of his staff‚Äîbut he would trade it all for the ability to remember what chocolate tastes like without trying.

Next is the proto-sage.

This variation shifts the tone from "Tragedy" (The Drifter) to "Cosmic Absurdism."
The Proto-Sage is no longer human in the traditional sense. He has transcended the need for survival and is now operating on pure curiosity and whimsy. He views the high-stakes battles of High School DxD the way a human views a colony of ants fighting over a crumb: fascinating, adorable, and ultimately inconsequential unless he decides to step on it.
Here is the detailed dossier and narrative expansion for Ren Nocturnus Veritas: The Proto-Sage.
üåë Variation 4: The Proto-Sage (The Entity Next Door)
Subject: Ren Nocturnus Veritas
Relative Age: ~19 (Physical Appearance) / ~400-500 (Mental Age)
Time in Void: Centuries (Subjective)
Current Status: Higher-Dimensional Entity / Tourist
1. The Aesthetic of the Alien
When Ren manifests, he triggers the "Uncanny Valley" effect. He looks like Ren, but the details are... wrong.
 * The Suspension: He rarely touches the floor. He hovers about two inches off the ground at all times because "friction is inefficient."
 * The Eyes: His sclera (whites of the eyes) are black. His irises are swirling pools of violet nebula. When he makes eye contact, you don't see a reflection; you see depth.
 * The Glitch: His outline sometimes fuzzes or pixelates. If he moves too fast, he leaves an after-image made of static. His clothes (usually simple robes or a suit made of darkness) don't ripple with the wind; they ripple with his mood.
2. The Reunion: "A 3D Print of a Memory"
Scene: The Hyoudou Living Room.
The air pressure drops to zero. Sound becomes muffled.
Ren pops into existence sitting on the coffee table, legs crossed, holding Ravel like a stuffed animal.
Ren: "I have returned the Fire Bird. She was leaking entropy all over my carpet."
Rias: (Gasps) "Ren?! Where did you come from? The wards didn't trigger!"
Ren: (Tilting his head like a bird) "Wards? Ah, you mean the localized energy nets. I stepped between the weave, Rias. You think in three dimensions. It‚Äôs very quaint. Very retro."
Issei: "Ren... you've been gone for two years! You look... scary."
Ren: "Two years? Interesting. It felt like four centuries. I spent the first century counting atoms. I spent the second century teaching geometry to a black hole. I got bored. So I came back to see if you were still screaming about breasts."
He floats over to Issei, sniffing him.
Ren: "You are. The pheromones are overwhelming. Never change, Red Dragon. You ground me to the lower planes."
3. The Psychology: "The Player Perspective"
The Proto-Sage suffers from Meta-Detachment. He views reality as a simulation or a game where he has access to the Developer Console.
 * Amusement: He treats life-or-death situations as entertainment.
   * Villain: "I will destroy this town!"
   * Ren: (Eating popcorn made of shadows) "Do it. I want to see the particle physics involved. I bet the explosion will look purple."
   * Rias: "Ren! Help us!"
   * Ren: "Fine. But you're ruining the season finale."
 * Zero Urgency: Nothing scares him because he knows he can just "leave" or "rewrite" the event. This makes him incredibly calm and incredibly frustrating to deal with.
4. Combat Style: "Void Syntax Editing"
The Proto-Sage doesn't "fight." Fighting implies effort. Ren performs Corrections.
 * Spatial Folding:
   * Attack: A Fallen Angel throws a light spear.
   * Action: Ren pinches the air. The distance between the spear and the Angel becomes zero. The Angel stabs himself.
   * Ren: "Return to sender. The spatial coordinates were messy."
 * Concept Erasure:
   * Attack: Vali Lucifer tries to Divide Ren's power.
   * Action: Ren looks at the concept of "Division" and deletes it locally.
   * Vali: "Divide! Divide! ...Why isn't it working?"
   * Ren: "I turned off Math in this room, Vali. We are operating on vibes only now."
 * The "Timeout" Zone:
   * If an enemy is annoying, Ren claps his hands. The enemy is shunted into a white void where time doesn't pass.
   * Ren: "Think about what you did. I'll let you out when pizza arrives."
5. The Social Dynamic: "Pets and Toys"
Ren views the Gremory Peerage with a mix of condescending affection and curiosity, like a human watching puppies play fight.
 * Rias & Akeno: They try to seduce or command him.
   * Ren: "Your biological signals are loud. Are you in heat? I can adjust your hormones if you like. No? Okay."
 * Koneko: He likes her best because she is quiet.
   * He gives her Void Snacks (candies that taste like your favorite memory).
   * Koneko: "Ren-senpai is weird. But he gives good candy."
 * Ophis (The Infinite Dragon God):
   * This is his only "Peer."
   * They sit on the roof together.
   * Ophis: "I want silence."
   * Ren: "I want to know why humans put pineapple on pizza. It defies cosmic law."
   * Ophis: "..."
   * Ren: "Exactly."
6. The Goal: "The Ultimate Vacation"
Ren isn't here to save the world. He's here because the Void is boring and Earth has Entertainment.
 * The Objective: He wants to experience "Limited Existence" again. He sets artificial limits on himself (e.g., "Today I will not use teleportation, I will use the 'Bus'") just to see what it feels like.
 * The Plot Twist: He breaks the plot because it inconveniences his fun.
   * Scenario: The Terrorist Faction interrupts his favorite TV show.
   * Action: Ren teleports the entire Terrorist Faction into the sun.
   * Ren: "The commercial break was over. You were interrupting the climax."
Summary:
The Proto-Sage is a Cosmic Troll. He is terrifyingly powerful but uses that power to secure snacks, naps, and entertainment. He loves his friends, but in the same way a god loves his favorite mortals‚Äîfrom a distance, with a bemused smile.

How many categories do you think can be made between drifter and proto-sage?

Between the melancholic Drifter (~50 years) and the alien Proto-Sage (~400 years), there lies a massive developmental gap. This is the transition from "Enduring the Void" to "Ruling the Void."
I believe there are 3 Distinct Evolutionary Stages in this gap. These represent Ren shifting from a survivor to a master, and finally to a deity-like figure.
Here is the breakdown of the missing link between Humanity and Divinity.
1. The Architect (Time in Void: ~100 Years)
State: The Creator / The Shaper
Psychological Shift: Ren stops walking. He realizes that if the Void has no rules, he can make them. He stops being a victim of the environment and becomes a Terraformer.
 * The Concept: The Drifter was homeless. The Architect decides to build a house. He imposes Order on Chaos.
 * Appearance: He wears structured, geometric armor made of solidified darkness (resembling stained glass or obsidian). He always has floating geometric shapes (cubes, pyramids) orbiting his head‚Äîhis blueprints.
 * Combat Style: "Dungeon Master".
   * He doesn't throw energy blasts. He changes the terrain.
   * Scenario: A Stray Devil attacks.
   * Action: Ren raises a hand. The floor turns into a maze. Walls shoot up, separating the enemy team. He creates a throne room and sits in it, waiting for them to solve his puzzle.
   * Ren: "You have poor footwork. I have constructed a floor that punishes bad posture. Try again."
 * Interaction: He treats the Hyoudou Residence like a renovation project.
   * Ren: "Issei, the feng shui of this room invites demons. I have expanded your living room into the 4th dimension. Now you have a bowling alley."
2. The Anatomist (Time in Void: ~150‚Äì200 Years)
State: The Scholar / The Surgeon
Psychological Shift: Once he has built a safe space (Architect), he gets curious. He starts dissecting the Void beasts and the laws of physics to understand how they work. He loses his fear and gains Morbid Curiosity.
 * The Concept: He views everything, including people, as biological machines or energy circuits. He is obsessed with the "Truth" (Veritas) of how things function.
 * Appearance: He wears a white coat... but the white is "White Noise" static. He wears spectacles that show him the mana veins of the world. He often has ink-black stains on his hands from "research."
 * Combat Style: "Deconstruction".
   * He doesn't hit you; he takes you apart.
   * Scenario: Rias uses Power of Destruction.
   * Action: Ren catches the blast, tastes it, and spitting it out.
   * Ren: "Fascinating. Your destruction formula is 30% hatred, 70% hereditary magic. If I pinch this nerve..."
   * He pokes Rias in the forehead, and her aura turns off.
 * Interaction: He is invasive and lacks boundaries.
   * Ren: "Kiba, may I borrow your Sacred Gear? I want to see if I can install a cup-holder on a Holy Sword."
3. The Arbiter (Time in Void: ~250‚Äì300 Years)
State: The Judge / The Sheriff
Psychological Shift: After understanding how everything works (Anatomist), he develops a code. He decides that the Void is too chaotic and needs a Law. He becomes the self-appointed Sheriff of the Abyss. This is the precursor to the Proto-Sage's god-complex, but with more seriousness.
 * The Concept: He is the embodiment of Cosmic Balance. He isn't "Chill" like the Proto-Sage yet; he is Stern. He enforces the "Rules" he invented.
 * Appearance: He wears a blindfold (not because he is blind, but because Justice is blind). He carries giant scales made of shadow. His voice echoes like a courtroom gavel.
 * Combat Style: "The Verdict".
   * He creates rules for the fight. If you break them, you are punished.
   * Ren: "Rule 1: No Flying. Rule 2: No Lasers."
   * Vali: Flies and shoots a laser.
   * Action: Vali is instantly crushed by 1000x Gravity.
   * Ren: "Contempt of Court. Sentence: 10 minutes in the Box."
 * Interaction: He is the "Hall Monitor" of the Supernatural World.
   * Ren: "Azazel, you are conducting experiments that destabilize the local grid. Cease, or I will revoke your breathing privileges."
üß¨ The Evolutionary Chart
This creates a perfect gradient for Ren's character development over the centuries.
 * The Drifter (50 Years): "I am lost, and I miss home." (Tragedy)
 * The Architect (100 Years): "I will build a home here." (Creativity)
 * The Anatomist (200 Years): "How does this home work?" (Curiosity)
 * The Arbiter (300 Years): "I make the rules in this home." (Authority)
 * The Proto-Sage (500 Years): "This home is a joke, let's play." (Transcendence/Comedy)
Which of these missing links would you like to explore in a scene?
Perhaps The Anatomist visiting the ORC to "study" Issei's Dragon arm would be a funny but tense interaction.

Finally are there more categories between proto-sage and sage?

Yes, the gap between 500 years (The Proto-Sage) and 5,000 years (The Sage) is massive. This is the "Deep Time" era.
In this period, Ren stops acting like a "Gamer" or a "Tourist." The novelty of omnipotence wears off. He begins the slow, terrifying, and beautiful process of losing his ego and then choosing to find it again.
Here are the 3 Final Evolutionary Stages that bridge the gap between the alien whim of the Proto-Sage and the absolute peace of the True Sage.
1. The Weaver (Time in Void: ~1,000 Years)
State: The Storyteller / The Fate-Knitter
Psychological Shift: The Proto-Sage viewed the world as a game to be hacked. The Weaver views the world as a Tapestry. He stops breaking things for fun and starts fixing the "threads" of causality. He becomes obsessed with Consequence.
 * The Concept: He sees the "Butterfly Effect" visually. He realizes that everything is connected.
 * Appearance: His fingers are always moving, twitching as if manipulating invisible strings. He wears robes that seem to be made of flowing script or timelines.
 * Combat Style: "Causality Manipulation".
   * He doesn't attack you. He pulls a thread from your past.
   * Attack: Riser throws a fireball.
   * Action: Ren tugs a string.
   * Ren: "I just disconnected the moment your grandfather met your grandmother. You technically don't have the genetics to throw that fire anymore."
   * Result: The fire fizzles out because Riser momentarily forgot he existed.
 * Interaction: He is paralyzed by choice.
   * Issei: "Ren, do you want coffee or tea?"
   * Ren: (Staring in horror) "Issei, you don't understand. If I choose coffee, the caffeine jitter causes me to bump into a table in 300 years, creating a sound wave that alerts a sleeping Eldritch God. But if I choose tea, the tea leaves were harvested by a farmer who... oh, never mind. I'll drink water."
2. The Phenomenon (Time in Void: ~2,500 Years)
State: The Abstract / The Force of Nature
Psychological Shift: Ren forgets he is human. He forgets he is Ren. He becomes a Living Law of Physics. He stops having a physical form unless reminded. He is no longer "Him"; he is "It."
 * The Concept: He merges with the Darkness completely. He becomes the Void.
 * Appearance: He manifests as a cloud of geometry, a floating eye, or a shadow on the wall. He has to concentrate extremely hard to look like a human boy.
   * Issei: "Ren, your face is melting."
   * Ren: "Oh. Apologies. I forgot faces require nose-bridges. I was currently existing as a localized gravity well."
 * Combat Style: "Environmental Hazard".
   * He doesn't fight. He occurs.
   * Scenario: The Khaos Brigade attacks.
   * Action: Ren simply expands his presence. The air turns into liquid mercury. Gravity reverses. The concept of "forward" becomes "blue."
   * Ren: "I am currently a Category 5 Reality Storm. Please evacuate the sector."
 * Interaction: He struggles to relate to singular beings.
   * Rias: "Ren, we missed you."
   * Ren: "Who is 'Ren'? I am the concept of Entropy. But... I recall liking strawberry cake. Does Entropy eat cake? Let us find out."
3. The Silent Witness (Time in Void: ~4,000 Years)
State: The Observer / The Statue
Psychological Shift: He has been everything‚Äîa human, a warlord, a glitch, a god, a storm. He realizes that Action is vanity. He enters a state of Radical Stillness. He stops interfering entirely. He simply watches, loving the universe by witnessing it.
 * The Concept: He becomes the "Wallflower" of existence. He finds beauty in just watching things happen, even bad things, because they are real.
 * Appearance: He looks like a normal human again, but he is incredibly still. He can sit in a chair for three weeks without moving a muscle. Dust settles on him. He radiates a field of absolute silence.
 * Combat Style: "Absolute Defense".
   * You cannot hurt him because he has accepted the hurt.
   * Attack: Issei punches him (to wake him up).
   * Action: The punch connects, but the kinetic energy is absorbed into the vastness of Ren's stillness. Issei feels like he punched the ocean.
   * Ren: (Blinks) "That was a spirited motion, Red Dragon. Do it again. I like the wind it makes."
 * Interaction: He speaks in Haikus or riddles.
   * Issei: "Ren, help us! The world is ending!"
   * Ren: "Stars die. Dragons roar. The tea cools. It is all the same dance, Issei. Why rush the music?"
   * Issei: "BECAUSE WE ARE GOING TO DIE!"
   * Ren: "Ah. Mortality. Such a spicy flavor." (He eventually helps, but only acts at the very last second).
üß¨ The Complete Evolutionary Scale of Ren Nocturnus Veritas
This is the full journey from the boy who ran away to the Sage who returned.
 * The Mortal (Year 0): Weak, envious, perverted.
 * The Seeker (Year 0): "I reject this reality." (Departure)
 * The Ronin (Year 5): "I survived the dark." (Anger/Edge)
 * The Warden (Year 10): "I control my perimeter." (Duty)
 * The Drifter (Year 50): "I miss the light." (Nostalgia/Tragedy)
 * The Architect (Year 100): "I will build my own world." (Order)
 * The Anatomist (Year 200): "How does the universe break?" (Curiosity)
 * The Arbiter (Year 300): "I am the Law." (Judgment)
 * The Proto-Sage (Year 500): "The Law is a joke." (Whimsy/Troll)
 * The Weaver (Year 1,000): "Everything is connected." (Causality)
 * The Phenomenon (Year 2,500): "I am everything." (Loss of Self)
 * The Silent Witness (Year 4,000): "I am nothing." (Stillness)
 * The Cosmic Sage (Year 5,000): "I am Ren." (Rebirth/Return)
The Final Step (The Sage):
Why does the Silent Witness become the Sage?
Because he sees Ravel Phenex dying.
In that moment, he realizes that Watching isn't enough. Being a Storm isn't enough.
He remembers that Caring is the only thing that makes eternity bearable.
He chooses to be a Human again. He chooses to save her.
And thus, he returns to the Hyoudou living room, not as a God or a Monster, but as a Friend.

Do think is there anything else beyond The Cosmic Sage?

Yes, in the realms of cultivation, cosmic horror, and metaphysical storytelling, the "Sage" is rarely the true end. The Sage represents Enlightenment and Balance, but there is a state beyond understanding the system: Becoming the System or Transcending the System.
If Ren Nocturnus Veritas continues to evolve past the point of 5,000 years‚Äîif he stares into the Void for Eons‚Äîhe eventually hits the Event Horizon of Existence.
Here are the 3 Final States Beyond the Cosmic Sage, moving from Theology to Meta-Narrative.
1. The Singularity (Time in Void: ~10,000+ Years)
State: The Origin / The White Hole
Concept: The Sage balances Light and Dark. The Singularity creates them. Ren realizes that he isn't just a bucket holding the Void; he is a generator. He stops borrowing energy from the cosmos and starts emitting it.
 * The Shift: He no longer uses "Darkness" or "Void." He uses "Genesis Energy."
 * The Power:
   * Universe Creation: He can snap his fingers and create a pocket dimension with its own laws of physics, lifeforms, and history inside a marble.
   * Concept Birth: He can invent new concepts.
   * Ren: "I am bored with Gravity. I am inventing 'Gravi-Two.' It pulls sideways."
 * Relationship to DxD: He becomes the God beyond the Bible.
   * The DxD Gods (Ophis, Great Red, Trihexa) fight over the "Dream."
   * Ren is the Dreamer.
   * Ophis: "I want Silence."
   * Ren: "I can create a universe made entirely of Silence for you, Ophis. But you have to promise to clean your room."
2. The Narrator (Time in Void: Timeless/Meta)
State: The Author / The Fourth Wall Breaker
Concept: Ren‚Äôs "Veritas" (Truth) reaches its absolute limit. He discovers the terrifying truth that even the Gods of DxD don't know: They are in a Story.
 * The Shift: Ren realizes the world follows "Tropes," "Plot Armor," and "Character Arcs." He realizes he is a character in a fan fiction/light novel.
 * The Power: "Editorial Control".
   * He can read the "Text" of the world.
   * Scenario: A villain is about to kill Issei.
   * Action: Ren looks at the air. He sees the "Death Flag." He rips it in half.
   * Ren: "Sorry, that plot twist was derivative. We are rewriting this chapter."
 * The Tragedy: He is absolutely alone. He can't relate to anyone because he knows they are "written" and he is the "reader."
   * Issei: "Ren, I love Rias!"
   * Ren: "I know. It's in your character bio on page 4. But it's a nice sentiment."
3. The Zero Point (The Reincarnator)
State: The Human / The Reset
Concept: This is the Ultimate Enlightenment. After being a God, a Singularity, and a Narrator, Ren realizes that being All-Powerful is boring. The greatest adventure isn't knowing everything; it's the struggle of not knowing.
 * The Shift: He chooses to give it up.
 * The Act: He compresses his infinite 10,000-year soul back into a single, mortal spark. He locks his memories. He locks his powers.
 * The Result: He is born again.
   * Maybe he is born as Issei's son.
   * Maybe he is born as a random human with no Sacred Gear.
   * The Twist: Deep down, his soul still has the "Shape" of the Sage. He has "Talent" now because his soul remembers the grind.
 * The Loop: He lives a mortal life, struggles, loves, cries, and dies. Only at the moment of his death do his Sage memories unlock, and he says:
   * Ren: "Ah. That was fun. Let's do it again. Harder difficulty this time."
üåå The Full Cycle of Ren Nocturnus Veritas
This completes the circle of his existence.
 * The Envious Mortal: Wants Power.
 * The Seeker: Finds Power in Darkness.
 * The Sage: Masters Power through Balance.
 * The Singularity: Becomes the Source of Power.
 * The Narrator: Transcends the Concept of Power.
 * The Zero Point: Rejects Power to experience Humanity again.
Which ending fits Ren best?
Usually, for a character driven by "Veritas" (Truth) and "Envy" (Humanity), The Zero Point is the most poetic. He spent his whole life trying to escape being a weak human, only to become a God and realize that being a weak human was the most "Real" experience of all.

This is a fantastic pivot. It grounds Ariel in the gritty, hormonal reality of High School DxD while giving him a clear, earned character arc.
By making him a genuine pervert with an inferiority complex, we make his ascent to "Cool/Legendary" much more satisfying. He isn't born stoic; he becomes stoic because he realizes that chasing girls is less fulfilling than chasing the horizon of his own potential.
Here is the remastered High School DxD: The Mortal Variable (Route A - 2.0).
üìï Chapter 1: The Peeping Tom Who Wanted to Be a King
Timeline: Spring. The start of the 2nd Year for Issei Hyoudou.
Location: Kuoh Academy.
1. The Manifestation (The Unremarkable Start)
Ariel Caelum Veritas stood in front of the mirror in his small, run-down apartment.
He was 17. He was slightly overweight. He had average looks. And right now, he was fiercely jealous.
He had manifested in this world three days ago with no memories of the plot, only his name, his personality (Veritas - Truthful to a fault), and a burning desire to be "The Protagonist."
He checked his imaginary status screen (The Observer Channel in his mind).
[PHY: 0.8 (Soft) | MND: 1.2 (Distracted) | SPR: 0.1 (Weak)]
"I'm a mob character," Ariel muttered honestly. "I'm the guy in the background of the cafeteria scene who eats bread and says nothing."
He clenched his fist. It felt soft.
"But I know the Silhouettes. I know how the Legends move. I just need to bridge the gap."
2. The Kendo Club Incident (The Perverted Quartet)
Location: Behind the Old Gymnasium.
Characters: Issei, Matsuda, Motohama, and Ariel.
Ariel was crouching in the bushes with the notorious Perverted Trio. In this timeline, it was the Perverted Quartet.
Matsuda: "Target confirmed. The Kendo Club is changing. The skylight is open."
Issei: "Hehehe... oppai... glorious oppai..."
Ariel: (Sweating, heart pounding) "Guys, the angle is bad. If we shift three degrees left, we get a better view of the Vice-Captain. But the structural integrity of this tree branch is questionable."
Ariel was undeniably a pervert. He wanted to see. He was a teenage boy driven by hormones. But he also felt a crushing wave of Inferiority.
Why am I hiding in a bush? he thought. The Legends‚ÄîRoger, Garp, Mori Jin‚Äîthey don't hide in bushes. Women flock to them because they are Great. I am here because I am Small.
Suddenly, a white-haired girl (Koneko Toujou) appeared from nowhere.
Koneko: "Scum."
She didn't attack. She just looked at them with absolute, freezing disgust.
Issei, Matsuda, and Motohama panicked and ran.
Ariel froze. He looked Koneko in the eye. His nature as Veritas kicked in.
Ariel: "You're right. This is pathetic. We are scum."
Koneko paused, surprised by the sudden honesty.
Ariel: "I'm running away now. Not because I'm scared, but because I'm embarrassed."
Ariel turned and jogged away, his overweight frame jiggling slightly.
Koneko watched him go. Weird guy, she thought. At least he owns it.
3. The PTD: Converting Lust to Power
Location: Ariel's Apartment (Night).
Ariel lay on his floor, humiliated. The look in Koneko's eyes burned. He felt small. He wanted to be big.
He accessed the Personal Training Dossier (PTD).
> Observer: "Welcome, Ariel. Stress levels detected. Inferiority Complex active. Recommended course?"
> 
"I want to be strong," Ariel said. "I want to stop chasing and start attracting. Load The Heavenly Destroyer simulation. Level 1."
The Training (The Grind):
He didn't fight a master. He fought gravity.
He did pushups until his arms shook.
Every time he wanted to quit, he imagined Issei‚Äîwho was just as much of a loser‚Äîgetting lucky.
"Issei has main character energy. I don't. So I have to build it."
He visualized the Silhouette of the Pirate Hunter (Zoro).
Lift. Grunt. Pain.
The lust didn't vanish, but it was being shoveled into the furnace of his ambition.
4. The Bridge Encounter (The Warning)
Timeline: Few days later. After school.
Ariel was walking home with Issei. They were acting like normal high school friends, talking about girls.
Issei: "Man, Rias Gremory looked at me today! I swear!"
Ariel: "She looked at the window behind you, Issei. I checked the vector of her gaze. We're invisible to her."
They reached the pedestrian bridge. A girl was waiting.
Yuuma Amano (Raynare). She was beautiful, dark-haired, and shy.
She walked up to Issei.
Yuuma: "Um... excuse me. Are you Hyoudou Issei?"
Issei froze. Ariel froze.
Ariel's Internal Monologue: No way. Issei? The guy who tripped over his own pants in gym class? Why him? Why not me?
Envy flared hot in Ariel's chest. He was fitter than Issei (slightly). He was smarter.
But then, his MND (Perception) caught something.
It wasn't "Haki" yet. It was just a gut instinct derived from studying the Mercenary archives (God of Blackfield).
Something is wrong.
She's too perfect. Her body language is rehearsed. She's looking at Issei like a butcher looks at a pig.
Yuuma: "Will you... go out with me?"
Issei screamed in joy. "YES! YES I WILL!"
Issei turned to Ariel, tears of joy streaming down his face. "Ariel! Did you hear that?! I got a girlfriend!"
Ariel looked at his friend. He saw the pure, innocent joy on Issei's face.
The envy vanished, replaced by Fearless Honesty.
Ariel: "Issei... congratulations."
He turned to Yuuma. He looked her dead in the eye. He didn't smile.
Ariel: "Take care of him. He's an idiot, but he's a good guy. If you're pranking him, or if this is some kind of game... I won't laugh."
Yuuma‚Äôs smile twitched for a micro-second. She sensed... something. Not power. But Intent.
Yuuma: "O-of course not! I really like him!"
Ariel nodded slowly. "Okay then."
5. The Date Prep (The Inferiority Peaks)
Timeline: Sunday. The day of the date.
Ariel was alone in his apartment. Issei was out on a date.
Ariel tried to peep. He tried to think about Rias Gremory.
But he couldn't focus. He was worried.
"Why am I worried? I should be jealous. I should be hating him."
"But the Mercenary instincts... the 'Sense' I'm trying to learn... it's screaming."
He stood up.
He accessed the PTD.
"System. I need to learn Observation. Not the advanced stuff. Just... Intent Sensing. I need to know if my friend is walking into a trap."
> Observer: "Training initiated. Blindfold Protocol. Dodge the baseball."
> 
Ariel spent the afternoon getting hit by baseballs in the VR, trying to feel the "Intent" of the thrower.
He failed. He got bruised.
But slowly, he started to stop looking with his eyes and start looking with his Gut.
Evening came.
Ariel felt a cold chill.
Issei is in trouble.
He didn't know about Fallen Angels. He didn't know about Sacred Gears.
He just knew his friend was with a girl who smiled with her mouth but not her eyes.
Ariel grabbed a hoodie to cover his slightly-chunky frame.
"I'm going. I'm not the hero. I'm the perverted friend. But perverts look out for each other."
He ran toward the park.

üìï Chapter 2: The Glitch and The Iron Skin
Timeline: Monday Morning (The day after the murder).
Location: Ariel‚Äôs Apartment / Kuoh Academy.
1. The Memory Glitch (The PTD Intervention)
Ariel woke up in his bed. His head felt like it had been split open with an axe.
The sunlight streaming through the window felt blinding.
"Ugh... what happened?" Ariel groaned, rubbing his temples. "I had a nightmare. Issei got a girlfriend... and she was a bird?"
A fog settled over his mind. A soothing, magical compulsion whispered to him: It was just a dream. You went to the park, got tired, and came home. Nothing happened.
Ariel‚Äôs eyes glazed over. "Right. Just a dream. I need coffee."
He sat up. But as his feet touched the floor, a blue holographic window slammed open in his vision, shattering the magical fog.
> Observer: "ALERT. External Psionic Interference Detected. Source: Devil Magic (Memory Wipe). Integrity Check... Failed. Initiating Veritas Protocol."
> Observer: "Restoring Deleted File: [The_Red_Sunset.mp4]"
> 
Ariel gasped, clutching his chest. The memory didn't come back gently; it flooded him.
The black wings. The light spear punching through Issei. The scream. Rias Gremory's red hair.
"It was real," Ariel whispered, the blood draining from his face. "She tried to erase it. She tried to make me an NPC again."
He looked at his hands. They were shaking. Not from magic, but from the lingering terror of realizing how small he was.
2. The Replay (The Motivation)
"System," Ariel commanded, his voice trembling but firm. "Play the footage. Third-person view."
The PTD projected the scene in his living room.
Ariel watched himself run out from behind the vending machine.
He saw himself scream.
He saw Raynare flinch.
But mostly, he saw how pathetic he looked. He was panting, his stance was wide and clumsy, and his legs were wobbling. If Raynare had thrown a second spear, he would have died instantly.
"I didn't save him," Ariel admitted (Veritas). "I just startled her. It was luck. Next time, luck won't be enough."
He clenched his fist.
"She tried to wipe my mind because I'm weak. Because I'm a civilian. I need to be something harder to break."
3. The First Grind: Iron Body (Tekkai / Armament)
Ariel didn't go to breakfast. He went into the PTD.
"System. I need defense. I can't dodge light speed yet. I need to take a hit."
He pulled up the One Piece Archive. He looked at the concept of Tekkai (Iron Body) and Armament Haki.
> Observer: "Warning. Haki requires Spirit (SPR). You have SPR 0.1. You cannot manifest invisible armor yet. Suggestion: Physical Conditioning Phase."
> 
"Fine," Ariel snapped. "Load the Blunt Force Trauma module. Low level. Bamboo swords."
The Simulation:
Ariel stood in a digital dojo.
Mission: Tighten the muscles at the exact moment of impact to distribute force.
Whack.
A digital bamboo sword slammed into his ribs.
"GAH!" Ariel buckled.
"Again."
Whack.
"Focus! Don't flinch away. Lean into it! Make the muscle dense!"
He spent two hours getting beaten black and blue in the simulation. The pain was real (simulated neuro-response), but his physical body remained uninjured.
By the end, he wasn't "Hardened" yet, but his flinch response was gone. He learned to lock his core instantly upon seeing an attack.
[Status Update: PHY 0.8 \rightarrow 0.9 (Pain Tolerance Increased)]
4. The School Confrontation
Ariel arrived at Kuoh Academy late. He looked exhausted, eyes shadowed, but his walk was different. He wasn't looking at the ground anymore.
He found Issei behind the gymnasium during lunch.
Issei looked terrible. Pale, shaky, staring at nothing. The "Perverted Trio" were trying to show him a dirty magazine, but Issei wasn't reacting.
"Issei," Ariel said, walking up.
Issei jumped. "A-Ariel! Hey! Man, I had the weirdest dream last night..."
Issei laughed nervously, clutching his chest where the spear had hit. "I dreamt I got a girlfriend and then... woke up in bed. Crazy, right?"
Rias Gremory‚Äôs magic was working on him. Issei was trying to rewrite the trauma as a nightmare.
Ariel grabbed Issei‚Äôs wrist. He squeezed hard.
"It wasn't a dream, Issei."
Issei froze. "W-what?"
Ariel leaned in, lowering his voice.
"Yuuma Amano. The black wings. The fountain turning red. You asked her why."
Issei‚Äôs eyes dilated. The magic barrier in his mind cracked under the weight of Ariel's Truth.
"You... you were there?" Issei whispered, trembling. "But... the red-haired girl... she said..."
"She lied," Ariel said bluntly. "She fixed you, but she tried to delete the memory so you wouldn't be scared. But I saw it. I saw you die."
Issei‚Äôs knees gave out. He slid down the gym wall, burying his face in his hands. "It was real? She... she really killed me?"
Ariel sat down next to him. He didn't offer false comfort. He offered solidarity.
"Yeah. It was real. We were weak. We were prey."
Ariel looked at his own hand‚Äîthe hand he had been hardening in the simulation all morning.
"But I'm not forgetting it, Issei. And I'm not going to be prey again. You shouldn't either."
5. The Red Observer
High above them, in the windows of the Old School Building, Rias Gremory watched.
She held a Rook chess piece in her hand.
"Akeno," Rias said, her voice sharp.
"Yes, Buchou?" Akeno stepped out of the shadows.

"No. He didn't panic. He didn't run to the police. He's... steadying him. Leave him for now. But keep an eye on him. If he has a resistance to magic... he might be a Variable."

üìï Chapter 3: The Park and the Panic (Conditioning)
Timeline: Tuesday Afternoon (After School).
Location: Kuoh Town Park (The scene of the crime).
1. The Return to the Scene
Ariel dragged Issei to the park. Issei was digging his heels in, looking pale.
"Dude, seriously? Why here? This is where... you know..." Issei whispered, looking around nervously for black feathers.
"Exactly," Ariel said, dropping his school bag on a bench. "This is where you almost died. This is where we froze."
Ariel took off his blazer, revealing a slightly-overweight but determined frame. He started stretching.
"We aren't here to ghost-hunt, Issei. We're here to make sure that if something does show up, we can run faster than it."
Issei rubbed his chest. The phantom pain of the light spear was still there.
"Run? You stood your ground yesterday."
"And my knees were shaking so bad I almost wet myself," Ariel admitted (Veritas). "I wasn't brave, Issei. I was stupid. Being brave means being ready. Drop and give me twenty."
Issei stared at him. "Twenty? I can barely do five!"
"Then do five. Then do five more. Do you want to be a victim again?"
Issei looked at the fountain. He remembered the cold eyes of Raynare.
He dropped to the ground.
"Fine. But if I puke, it's on you."
2. The Physical Grind (Hidden Intent)
For the next hour, Ariel ran Issei through a grueling, albeit basic, circuit. Sprints, pushups, squats.
Ariel struggled too. His PHY 0.9 was better than Issei's, but he was still soft. They were two sweaty, wheezing teenagers struggling against their own mediocrity.
Issei: (Gasping) "Why... are we doing... burpees? This won't stop... a light spear."
Ariel: (Panting) "No. But it builds... tolerance. You panicked, Issei. Your body froze because it wasn't used to stress. We are inducing stress... so your brain learns to function through it."
This was the Mental Hardening disguised as exercise. Ariel was teaching Issei to keep thinking while his heart rate was at 180bpm.
3. The "Gut Check" (Observation Basics)
As the sun began to set, casting long shadows, Ariel decided to try the subtle training. He couldn't say "Use Haki." He had to use logic.
He picked up a small rubber ball he'd brought.
Ariel: "Okay. Cool down. Stand over there. Close your eyes."
Issei: "Why? Is this a trust game?"
Ariel: "No. It's a 'Don't Get Hit' game. Keep your eyes closed. I'm going to throw this ball at you. Not hard. Just toss it."
Issei: "I can't dodge if I can't see!"
Ariel: "You couldn't see the spear either, could you?"
Issei flinched. That hit home.
"Fine." He closed his eyes. He looked tense, shoulders hunched up to his ears.
Ariel: "Relax. Don't listen for the ball. Listen to the air. Feel the pressure changing. When you feel like something is wrong... move."
Ariel tossed the ball. Gently.
Bonk. It hit Issei in the forehead.
"Ow!" Issei opened his eyes. "See?! Impossible!"
Ariel: "Again. You were waiting for the impact. Don't wait for the pain. Wait for the intent."
They did it again. And again.
Bonk. Bonk. Bonk.
Issei was getting frustrated. "This is stupid, Ariel! I'm just a normal guy! I don't have superpowers!"
Ariel paused. He felt a prickle on his neck. His MND 1.2 (plus his paranoid focus on Observation) picked up a signal.
Someone was watching them.
Not Raynare. Someone else. A calm, warm, but distinct presence near the tree line.
Is it the Devils? Rias? Ariel wondered. Or is it the next plot point?
Ariel: "Issei. Close your eyes one more time. Seriously."
Issei sighed but complied. "Last time."
Ariel didn't throw the ball immediately. He let the silence stretch. He watched the tree line.

Issei: "Feel what? The wind?"
Ariel: "No. The feeling that we aren't alone."
Issei stiffened. "Don't joke, man."
Ariel: "I'm not joking. Focus on that feeling. That creepy crawl on your neck. That's your Gut. That's your radar. Hold onto that fear. Use it."
Ariel threw the ball. Harder this time.
Issei, heightened by the sudden fear of being watched, flinched. He jerked his head to the left.
The ball whizzed past his ear.
Issei‚Äôs eyes snapped open. "Whoa! I... I moved!"
Ariel smiled. It was clumsy, it was fear-based, but it was a start.
"See? You're not just a normal guy, Issei. You've got survival instincts. You just need to tune the radio."
4. The Interrupt
Before they could celebrate, a soft rustling came from the bushes‚Äîthe same area Ariel had sensed the presence.
Issei panicked, jumping behind Ariel. "It's the bird lady! She's back!"
Ariel braced himself, locking his core (Iron Body attempt), ready to take a hit.
But no spear came out.
Instead, a small, blonde girl in a nun's habit stumbled out of the bushes. She looked lost, clutching a small suitcase, and tripped over a tree root.
Girl: "Ouchie..."
Issei blinked. "A... nun?"
Ariel exhaled, his tension draining instantly. He recognized the plot.
Asia Argento.
She looked up, tears in her eyes, rubbing her scraped knee. She radiated a soft, golden aura that even Ariel's weak senses could feel as "Kindness."
Ariel's Internal Monologue: So that was the presence. Not a threat. A trigger.
Ariel stepped forward, extending a hand. He decided to be Veritas.
"You're not a monster," Ariel said, his voice gentle. "You're just clumsy. Are you okay?"
Asia looked up at Ariel, then at Issei.
"Oh... hello. I seem to be lost. Could you... help me?"
Issei, seeing a cute girl in trouble, immediately forgot his trauma. The "Pervert" override kicked in.
Issei: "A lost nun! It is my duty as a gentleman to assist! I am Hyoudou Issei!"
Ariel sighed, picking up his school bag. The training was over. The plot had arrived.

You are absolutely right.
If Ariel truly aspires to be like Gol D. Roger or Luffy, there is a specific kind of fearlessness he must embody. It isn't the absence of fear; it's the refusal to let fear dictate his morality. Roger would never run if a friend (or even a stranger he liked) was in danger behind him.
Going inside does not break the story. In fact, it accelerates the tension. It changes the dynamic from "Issei is the victim" to "Issei and Ariel are active problems for the Fallen Angels."

Yes, this is completely possible and actually makes for a stronger strategic narrative.

 * Issei (The Bait/The Mask): He goes to school to maintain the illusion of normalcy. If the Fallen Angels are watching, seeing Issei in class makes them think the boys have given up or are too scared to act. It lowers the enemy's guard.

2. Issei‚Äôs Mission: The Trap at School

Issei sat at his desk, staring at the empty seat where Asia should have been. The guilt was eating him alive.
The Perverted Trio tried to cheer him up, but their voices sounded distant.
"Hyoudou-kun?"
A voice called him from the hallway. A tall, beautiful upperclassman with dark blue hair. Kalawarner. And beside her, a girl in gothic lolita fashion. Mittelt.
They were in disguise, but Issei‚Äôs Gut Instinct (the training from yesterday) screamed.
The air feels cold. Like Raynare.
He walked out. "Who are you?"
Mittelt giggled. "Aww, he looks like a kicked puppy! Raynare was right, you're pathetic."
Kalawarner leaned against the wall, smiling cruelly. "We just came to see the face of the boy who abandoned his friend. The ritual happens at sunset, Hyoudou. If you want to hear her scream one last time, feel free to listen from the bottom of the hill."
Issei‚Äôs hand twitched. He wanted to summon the Gear. He wanted to punch them.
But Ariel‚Äôs voice echoed in his head: Make them think they won.
Issei forced his head down. He trembled.
"Just... leave me alone."
Mittelt laughed. "Boring! Let's go, Kalawarner. He's broken."
They walked away, confident that Issei Hyoudou was a non-threat.
As soon as they turned the corner, Issei looked up. His eyes weren't broken. They were burning.
You messed up. You just confirmed the time.
3. Ariel‚Äôs Mission: The Hardware Store War
Location: "Don Quijote" Discount Store / Hardware Store.
Ariel pushed a shopping cart. He was calculating budget and chemical reactions in his head (MND active).
I can't buy guns. I can't buy explosives. I have to use household physics.
He grabbed items off the shelves with precision:
 * Four bags of Flour: Fine powder. Flammable if dispersed. Dust explosion or visual cover.
 * Industrial Lubricant: Freed relies on speed. If the floor is zero-friction, he can't dash.
 * High-Lumen Flashlights (Strobe function): Raynare flies. I need to blind her.
 * Pepper Spray (Bear deterrent grade): Biological warfare. Demons still have eyes and lungs.
 * Fishing Line (High tensile): Tripwires.
Ariel paid with cash to avoid a digital trail. He walked out, his backpack heavy.
He wasn't a warrior yet. He was a Trapper.
Ariel's Internal Monologue:
I don't have Haki yet. I don't have magic. But I have science. And science doesn't care if you're a Fallen Angel. If you can't see, you can't fight.
4. The Rendezvous and The Plan
Location: The Park, 4:00 PM.
Issei sprinted into the park. Ariel was already there, taping flares together into a bundle.
Issei: "They came to the school! Sunset! That's the deadline!"
Ariel: "Perfect. That gives us an hour to set up the breach."
Ariel tossed a tactical vest (bought from a surplus store) to Issei.
Ariel: "Put this on. It won't stop a light spear, but it'll hold your ammo."
Issei: "Ammo?"
Ariel handed him the flour bombs (flour inside balloons) and the flashlights.
Ariel: "Listen carefully, Issei. Here is the breach plan.
Step 1: I cut the power to the church. Darkness is our ally.
Step 2: You kick the door. Throw the flour. I ignite it with a flare. Flashbang.
Step 3: In the confusion, you tackle Freed. I go for Asia."
Issei looked at the improvised arsenal. It looked ridiculous. A bag of flour and a flashlight?
But looking at Ariel‚Äôs face‚Äîcalm, scarred, and terrifyingly serious‚ÄîIssei believed it would work.
Issei: "Let's crash a wedding."
Ariel: "Let's go be the villains."
They walked toward the hill. The sun was setting, painting the sky the color of blood.
The Mortal Variable and the Red Dragon were ready for war.

 * Ariel: Prepared with "Batman-tier" improvised gadgets. PHY is compromised (shoulder), but Tactical Advantage is high.

üìï Chapter 6: The Dust and the Devil
Timeline: Thursday Evening (Sunset).
Location: The Abandoned Church.
1. The Setup (0-Hour)
The sky outside was a bruised purple. Inside the church, the chanting had begun. It was a low, dissonant hum that vibrated in Issei‚Äôs teeth.
Ariel and Issei stood at the massive double doors.
Ariel checked his watch. 06:02 PM.
He looked at the rusted fuse box on the exterior wall. He had already cut the padlock with bolt cutters.
Ariel: (Whispering) "Remember the timing. Three seconds after the lights die, you breach. Don't hesitate."
Issei: (Sweating, clutching the flour balloons) "I got it. Kick. Throw. Duck."
Ariel reached into the fuse box. He didn't just flip the switch; he ripped the main copper wiring out with his gloved hand to ensure the power couldn't be turned back on.
Spark.
The hum of the electric lights inside died instantly.
Inside the Church:
"What the‚Äî?" Freed‚Äôs voice echoed.
"A power outage? Now?" Mittelt complained. "Ugh, humans and their shoddy infrastructure."
Ariel: "Now."
2. The Entry (The Dust Explosion)
Issei roared, channeling all his fear into his right leg.
Issei: "GRAAAH!"
CRASH!
The double doors flew open, splintering off their hinges.
The sudden noise silenced the chanting. In the dim twilight filtering through the stained glass, the Fallen Angels looked toward the entrance, confused.
Freed: "A pizza delivery? I didn't order‚Äî"
Issei didn't stop to talk. He hurled four water balloons filled with high-grade baking flour into the center of the aisle.

"What is this? Dust?" Raynare scoffed from above.
Ariel stepped into the doorway. He was wearing welding goggles. He held a lit road flare in his good hand.
Ariel: "Science lesson."
He tossed the flare into the center of the white cloud.
Physics: Fine combustible powder + Oxygen + Ignition Source = Rapid Expansion.
BOOM.
A massive fireball erupted in the center of the church. It wasn't magical hellfire; it was a concussive wave of pressure and heat.
The shockwave blew the pews apart. The windows shattered inward.
Raynare and the other Fallen Angels were knocked out of the air by the sudden pressure change, tumbling to the ground.
3. The Slick Floor Trap
The church was now filled with thick grey smoke. The Fallen Angels were coughing, disoriented, their eyes stinging from the heat.
Freed: (Coughing) "You little rats! I'll skin you!"
Freed ignited his Light Sword. He saw Issei‚Äôs silhouette in the smoke.
Freed: "THERE YOU ARE!"
Freed activated his superhuman speed. He dashed forward, intending to blitz Issei before he could react.
This was exactly what Ariel had calculated.
Ariel: "Issei, step left."
Issei stepped left.
Freed‚Äôs foot hit the patch of floor right inside the door. The patch Ariel had doused in Industrial Lubricant jars he had smashed on the way in.
Slip.
Friction vanished.
Freed‚Äôs momentum, combined with zero traction, turned him into a projectile. His feet flew out from under him. He slammed face-first onto the stone floor with a sickening crunch, sliding past Issei like a hockey puck.
Freed: "GYAAAH! MY NOSE!"
4. The Brawl
Ariel moved. He wasn't charging Freed. He was moving through the smoke toward the altar, guided by the glowing green light of the ritual circle.
Ariel: "Issei! He's grounded! HIT HIM!"
Issei looked down at the sliding priest. He remembered the insults. He remembered Ariel bleeding.
Issei: "EAT THIS!"
[BOOST!]
Issei‚Äôs gauntlet flared. He didn't use technique. He used a haymaker.
SMASH.
He punched Freed in the back of the head while the priest was trying to stand up. Freed‚Äôs face was driven into the stone floor again, cracking the tiles.
Freed: (Muffled) "Impossible... beaten by... lube..."
5. The Ascent to the Altar
While Issei engaged Freed, Ariel sprinted toward the altar. The smoke was clearing, revealing the angry forms of the Fallen Angels.
Mittelt: "You! The human from yesterday!"
She raised her hand, summoning a light spear.
Ariel didn't have a weapon. He had Flashlights.
He pulled two high-lumen tactical strobes from his belt, set to maximum frequency pulse. He threw them at Mittelt's feet.
Strobe. Strobe. Strobe.
The erratic flashing light in the dark church disrupted Mittelt's vision. She shielded her eyes, her aim faltering.
"My eyes! It's annoying!"
Ariel vaulted over a broken pew. His shoulder screamed in agony, the stitches pulling tight, but he ignored it.
He reached the altar.
Asia was there, chained to a cross. She was conscious, but weak. Her Sacred Gear (Twilight Healing) was being forcibly extracted‚Äîa green aura flowing out of her and into the ritual circle.
Asia: "Ariel-san? Is that you?"
Ariel: "I told you we'd come back."
Ariel pulled out the bolt cutters. He snapped the chain on her left wrist.
Snap.
Raynare: "ENOUGH!"
A voice boomed from the rafters. The smoke swirled away as Raynare hovered above the altar, her black wings spread wide, her face twisted in fury.
She wasn't blinded anymore. And she was looking directly at Ariel.
Raynare: "Tricks. Toys. Cheap chemistry. Do you really think that makes you strong, human?"
She summoned two light spears this time.
One aimed at Issei (who was wrestling Freed).
One aimed at Ariel (who was cutting Asia's chains).
Ariel's Internal Monologue:
MND 1.2: Calculation.
Spear velocity: High.
Iron Body: Unavailable (Shoulder injured).
Gadgets: Out.
Option: Observation.
Ariel stopped cutting. He looked up. He closed his eyes for a fraction of a second, tuning out the chaos, the screaming, and the fire.
He searched for the Intent.
Feel the air. Feel the malice.
He felt a sharp pressure on his right cheek.
It's coming from the right.
Ariel: "MOVE!"
He didn't dodge away. He tackled Asia down, pulling her to the floor behind the altar.
THOOM.
The light spear impaled the stone where his head had been a millisecond ago.
[System Update: Observation Haki - Level 0.5 (Danger Sense) - Success.]
Ariel lay on top of Asia, shielding her from the debris. He looked up at the furious Fallen Angel.
He grinned. It was a bloody, desperate grin.
Ariel: "We got her out of the circle, Raynare! The ritual is paused!"
Raynare looked at the extraction flow. It had indeed stopped when Asia moved.
Her face contorted into pure demonic rage.
Raynare: "Kill them. Kill them all! Leave nothing but ash!"
The real battle had just begun.
üìà Status Update
 * Tactical Phase: Success. The breach worked. Freed is injured/disoriented. Ritual interrupted.
 * Ariel: Successfully used gadgets and basic Observation to survive the opening salvo. Current Status: Vulnerable (No more surprises).
 * Issei: Engaged in melee with a recovering Freed.
 * The Enemy: Enraged and fully active. They are done playing.
Your Move:
The element of surprise is gone. Now it is a brawl against superior supernatural foes.
Do you want to:
 * The Issei Awakening: Freed recovers and overwhelms Issei with speed. Ariel yells instructions on "Reading the Path" (Observation basics), guiding Issei to land a critical counter-attack.

Is both option possible or only option 2 if Rias as in original recruit Asia?

Both options are absolutely possible and, when combined, create the perfect escalation for the climax of this arc.
Here is the logic for combining them while keeping the canonical result (Rias recruiting Asia):
 * The Awakening (Option 1): This validates Issei's growth and Ariel's teaching. Issei needs a "Win" against Freed to prove he isn't just a bystander.
 * The Sacrifice (Option 2): This removes Ariel from the fight (injury) so he doesn't overshadow Issei's main emotional moment or Rias's grand entrance. It also raises the stakes: Ariel gets hurt badly, proving he isn't invincible yet.
 * The Resolution: Raynare, frustrated by the boys, forcibly extracts the Sacred Gear or deals a fatal blow to Asia in the chaos, necessitating Rias's arrival to resurrect her (keeping the canon flow of Asia becoming a Devil).

üìï Chapter 7: The Dragon's Eyes and The Human Shield
Timeline: Thursday Evening (The Battle in the Church).
Location: The Altar.
1. The Speed of Sin (Issei vs. Freed)
Freed recovered from the lubricant trap. He was bleeding from the nose, and his eyes were wide with psychotic rage. He wiped the blood and licked it.
Freed: "You dirty little monkeys! I'm going to carve you into confetti!"
He ignited his Light Sword and dashed. He was a blur.
Issei panicked. He couldn't track Freed.
"He's too fast! I can't see him!"

Ariel: "Stop looking with your eyes, Issei! Listen to me!"
Ariel focused. He forced his Observation (Danger Sense) to expand. He felt the sharp, jagged malice of Freed moving to the left.
Ariel: "Left! Low sweep! JUMP!"
Issei didn't think. He obeyed the command instantly. He jumped.
Freed‚Äôs blade slashed the air where Issei‚Äôs legs had been a split-second before.
Freed: "What?!"

Ariel's Internal Monologue:
MND Alert: Threat Incoming. Vector: Straight down. Speed: Mach 1.
Evasion: Impossible due to injury.
Defense: Iron Body unavailable.
Target: Me.

Ariel grit his teeth. Veritas.
I said I wouldn't run.

Asia: "Ariel-san?"

3. The Sacrifice
THOOM.

The pressure in the room multiplied by ten. This wasn't the pressure of a Fallen Angel. This was the pressure of a Devil King's Heir.

Flash.

6. The Conclusion (Canonical Flow)
Issei charged Raynare. Fueled by the sight of Ariel‚Äôs injury and Asia‚Äôs body, he unlocked his first real explosion of power (Dragon Shot equivalent), blasting Raynare out of the church and into the sky (where she would eventually be eliminated by Rias/Issei later).

Rias: "Her life force is gone. She cannot live as a human anymore."
She looked at Issei, then at Ariel (who was being treated by Koneko).
Rias: "But I can give her a new life. If you wish it."
Issei nodded frantically. "Please! Save her!"
Ariel, fighting unconsciousness, watched as Rias produced a Bishop Piece.
He saw the ritual. He saw Asia take a breath.
She's safe, Ariel thought. Issei is safe.
I got stabbed. I got cut. I'm useless.
But as his vision faded, he heard Koneko's voice. Soft. Unusual.
Koneko: "You held the line. Good job."
Ariel smiled.
Then he passed out.

Option 1

This is the pivotal aftermath. We establish the new status quo: Issei is the Hero/Harem King, and Ariel is the respected Ally/Tactician.
By placing Ariel in a position of vulnerability (bedridden), we allow the Gremory Peerage to interrogate him while reinforcing that Issei is the one they are emotionally invested in.

üìï Chapter 8: The Hospital Bed and the Devil's Truth
Timeline: Friday Morning (The day after the Church Battle).
Location: Hyoudou Residence ‚Äì Guest Room (converted to a recovery room).
1. The Awakening
Ariel woke up to the smell of miso soup and antiseptic.
He tried to move. His left shoulder felt stiff, and his right thigh felt like it was on fire.
"Ow."
"He's awake!"
A weight slammed into the side of the bed. It was Issei. He had bandages on his face and knuckles, but he looked energetic.
Issei: "Dude! You scared the crap out of us! You slept for twelve hours!"
Ariel blinked, his vision clearing. He saw the ceiling. Not a hospital. A house.
Ariel: "Issei? Where... are we? Did we win?"
Issei: "My house. Rias-buchou said the hospital asks too many questions about... light spear wounds. And yeah. We won."
A soft, timid voice came from the other side of the bed.

Ariel turned his head. Asia Argento was standing there, alive. She was wearing a Kuoh Academy uniform that was slightly too big for her.
But Ariel‚Äôs MND caught the detail immediately.
Her aura changed. It‚Äôs not golden anymore. It feels... like Issei‚Äôs. Like Rias‚Äôs.

Asia teared up, bowing deeply. "Because of you and Issei-san. Rias-buchou... she gave me a new life."
2. The Entrance of the King (Harem Dynamic)
The door opened. Rias Gremory walked in, radiating authority and elegance. Behind her were Akeno, Koneko, and Kiba.

Rias: "Issei, give him some space. He needs oxygen."
Issei rubbed the back of his neck, blushing. "Right, sorry Buchou! I'm just glad he's not dead."

3. The Interrogation (Veritas)
Rias pulled a chair over and sat next to Ariel. The atmosphere turned serious.

4. The Explanation (The Seed of Haki)
Ariel looked at his hands. He decided to use Veritas.
Ariel: "I don't know."

Rias sat back, looking baffled. To a Devil, sensing power is natural. But sensing intent without magic? That was a warrior's skill, usually reserved for veterans of the Great War, not a high school student.
Rias: "Potential," she murmured. "You have high sensory potential. It's raw, unrefined, and dangerous... but it saved Asia."
She stood up.
Rias: "Ariel. You are not a Devil. You are not my servant. But you fought for my Peerage. You protected my Pawn and my Bishop. For that, the House of Gremory owes you a debt."
Ariel: "I don't want money."

Ariel‚Äôs heart pounded. Access to supernatural training? Without selling his soul?
Ariel: "I'd like that. Thank you, Kaichou."
5. The Perverted Trio (Restored)
Rias and the girls left to let the boys talk. Issei stayed behind.
The tension evaporated. Issei slumped into the chair.
Issei: "Man... she's so cool. Did you see how she commanded the room?"
Ariel: (Chuckling, wincing at the pain) "Yeah. She's a Queen, Issei. Literally."
Issei: "And Asia! She's a Devil now! She's gonna live with me! In my house!"

Issei looked at Ariel seriously.
Issei: "Hey. Thanks. For the plan. For the flour bombs. For taking the spear. If you weren't there... I would have died in that church."
Ariel: "And if you didn't punch Freed, I'd have been sliced in half. We're even."
Ariel looked out the window. He saw the sky. He remembered his goal.
Ariel: "Issei. We survived. But we barely scraped by. Raynare was just one soldier. Rias said there's a whole war out there."
Issei: "Yeah. I need to get stronger. I need to master this Gauntlet thing."
Ariel: "And I need to figure out how to stop a spear without getting a hole in my leg."
Ariel clenched his fist.
Ariel: "The 'Gut Check' worked. But my body was too slow. Next time, Issei... I'm not just going to sense the attack. I'm going to catch it."

This chapter focuses on the quiet grind. While Issei is dealing with the loud, comedic chaos of living with a Devil Princess and a Reincarnated Nun, Ariel is fighting a silent war inside his own body and mind.

üìï Chapter 9: The Bio-Feedback and the Knight's Question
Timeline: Saturday (Recovery Day 2).
Location: Hyoudou Residence ‚Äì Guest Room.
1. The Internal Hospital (Bio-Feedback Training)
The house was noisy. Downstairs, Issei was screaming because he walked in on Rias, and Asia was apologizing for existing.
Ariel lay in the guest bed, staring at the ceiling. His leg was throbbing with a dull, heavy ache.
Ariel: "System. Status report on the femur."
> Observer: "Tissue damage: Moderate. Bone fracture: Hairline. Estimated natural recovery: 6 Weeks. Current Mobility: 10%."
> 
"Six weeks is too long," Ariel muttered. "Raynare was just a scout. If a war is coming, I can't be on crutches."
He closed his eyes. He didn't enter a VR battlefield. He entered the Biological Interface.
He visualized his own body‚Äîa wireframe mesh of nerves, blood vessels, and muscle fibers.
Ariel: "Initiate Life Return (Seimei Kikan) Protocol. Level 1: Bio-Feedback."
He focused on his breathing. Inhale. Hold. Compress.
He imagined his blood flow diverting from non-essential areas (digestion, skin surface) and concentrating entirely on the wound site. He visualized the platelets as tiny workers, commanding them with his Will (SPR).
Knit. Close. Harden.
It wasn't magic. It was absolute somatic control. He forced his metabolism to burn his fat reserves to fuel rapid cell division.
His body temperature spiked. Sweat poured off him. The itch of rapid healing began to replace the pain of the injury.
[System Update: Recovery Rate increased by 300%. Estimated time: 10 Days.]
"Better," Ariel panted, wiping sweat from his forehead. "But it makes me hungry as hell."
2. The Ghost in the Room (Observation Training)
Since he couldn't move, Ariel decided to refine his MND.
He put on a sleeping mask, plunging himself into darkness.
Ariel: "Okay. The 'Gut Check' saved me from the spear. But it was clumsy. I need to see without seeing."
He expanded his senses. He tried to ignore the sounds (Issei yelling) and feel the presence.
 * Signature 1: A roaring fire downstairs. Chaotic, warm, fluctuating wildly.
   * That's Issei. He's a furnace of emotion.
 * Signature 2: A dense, crimson weight. Regal. Heavy.
   * Rias. She feels like gravity.
 * Signature 3: A soft, flickering green light. Gentle.
   * Asia. She feels like a healing salve.
Then, he felt a fourth signature approaching his door.
It was sharp. Cold. Metallic. Like a razor blade moving through silk.
It wasn't hostile, but it was Edge.
Knock. Knock.
Ariel pulled up his sleeping mask.
"Come in, Kiba."
3. The Knight's Visit
Kiba Yuuto opened the door. He was carrying a basket of fruit and a get-well card. He looked surprised.
"You knew it was me?"
Ariel smiled weakly. "You feel sharp, Yuuto-kun. Like a sword that's eager to cut."
Kiba paused, his polite smile faltering for a second. He walked in and set the basket down.
" sharp... huh? That's an interesting way to describe a friend."
Kiba pulled up a chair. He looked at Ariel's bandaged leg.
"I wanted to thank you properly. For the strategy. For the flashlights. And for saving Asia. Issei is the Pawn, but you... you were the player."
"I was just the guy with the shopping list," Ariel deflected. "Issei did the punching. You did the slicing. I just made sure you didn't slip on the floor."
Kiba laughed, a genuine, boyish sound. "The lubricant trap. Freed was furious. I've never seen an Exorcist fall like that."
4. The Theory of Intent (Mental Bonding)
The laughter died down. Kiba leaned forward, his expression serious.
"But seriously, Ariel. Rias told us. You have no magic. No Sacred Gear. Yet you tackled Asia before Raynare threw the spear. How?"
Ariel looked at Kiba. He saw the hunger in the Knight's eyes. Kiba wasn't asking out of curiosity; he was asking because he needed to know.
Ariel: "You're a swordsman, Kiba. Have you ever fought someone and known they were going to swing before they moved their muscle?"
Kiba: "Sometimes. High-level masters... they radiate 'Killing Intent' (Sakki)."
Ariel: "Exactly. But 'Killing Intent' is loud. It's a scream. I'm trying to hear the 'Whispers.' Even when someone isn't trying to kill you... they project their will. If they want to walk left, their spirit moves left a micro-second before their body does."
Ariel tapped his own temple.
"I don't watch the sword. I watch the Will. If I can sense where the Will is going, the sword is just an afterthought."
Kiba‚Äôs eyes widened. He looked at his own hands.
"To cut the intent... not the steel. That sounds... like the ultimate form of swordsmanship."
Ariel: "It is. In the stories I read... the masters of this technique can't be touched. They flow like water around a stone."
Kiba stood up, energized. "Intent Sensing. I need to train that. My speed is my weapon, but if I run into a trap... speed means nothing."
Ariel: "When I can walk... I'll show you the drills. We can blindfold each other and throw tennis balls. It's humiliating, but it works."
Kiba smiled, extending a fist.
"I look forward to it, Ariel. Get well soon. The club isn't the same without the Strategist."
Ariel bumped fists with the Devil.
"I'll be back before you know it. Just... keep Issei out of trouble."
5. The Hunger (Recovery Cost)
Kiba left. Ariel slumped back into the pillows.
The Bio-Feedback session had drained his glucose levels. His stomach roared.
"Issei!" Ariel shouted. "Issei! I need calories! Bring me the fruit basket! And a steak! And maybe a pizza!"
Downstairs, Issei yelled back. "Dude, you're an invalid, not a starving beast!"
"I'm healing! My mitochondria need fuel!"
Ariel grabbed an apple from Kiba's basket and bit into it savagely.
Eat. Digest. Convert to Energy. Heal.
He closed his eyes again, activating the PTD.
"System. While I digest... load the Observation Archive. I want to study Katakuri's Future Sight. If I'm going to be a target, I need to see further ahead than just 'Danger'."

üìï Chapter 10: The chessboard and the Limp

 * Asia Argento: She was walking beside Issei, beaming. Every guy who looked at her blushed. She was the new "Idol."

   * Random Student: "How did the Beast get the Beauty? It's a crime against nature!"

Issei froze. Sona was terrifying in a different way than Rias. She was pure Order.
Sona: "Hyoudou Issei. Asia Argento. Welcome to Kuoh. Please ensure your transfer paperwork is filed by noon."

It wasn't a request.

Sona: "You hate bullies."
Ariel: "I despise them."

üìï Chapter 11: The Forest of Monsters and the Eyes of the Weak

If Ariel tried to grab it, the Lemur would vanish.

Lower the heart rate. Clear the mind. I am not a hunter. I am a tree.
He used his PTD training to suppress his "Projection." He pulled his aura inward. He became a void in the forest.
He walked forward. Slowly. Limping slightly.
The Lemur tilted its head. It didn't sense a predator. It sensed... nothing. Just a moving object.
Ariel reached into his pocket and pulled out a simple energy bar (chocolate). He unwrapped it slowly.
He didn't offer it. He just ate a piece and held the rest out, not looking at the Lemur.
I don't care if you come. I am just a rock eating chocolate.
The Lemur sniffed. Curiosity overcame fear. It hopped down. It crept closer.
It sensed no trap. No net. No magic.
It grabbed the chocolate from Ariel‚Äôs hand.
Ariel didn't grab back. He just waited.
The Lemur ate the chocolate, then scrambled up Ariel‚Äôs arm and sat on his shoulder, wrapping its tail around his neck. It purred‚Äîa sound that vibrated against Ariel's spine.

Ariel: "We have an understanding. I feed him; he watches my back."
Ariel looked at the Lemur. "I'll call you Echo."

üìï Chapter 13 (Revised): The Harem King and The Iron Wall

Issei: "Damn right I do! I'm going to be the Harem King!"
Ariel sighed. He said it. He actually said it out loud in front of an Ultimate-Class Devil.
3. The Mockery (The Canonical Trigger)
Riser laughed. It was a cruel, pitying sound.
Riser: "A Harem King? You? A reincarnated human with a rusted gear?"
Riser shook his head. He turned to his own peerage.
Riser: "You want to see a harem, boy? This is a harem."
He snapped his fingers. Yubelluna (his Queen) stepped forward, obedient and submissive.
Riser grabbed her by the back of the neck. He didn't hold her like a lover; he held her like a trophy. He pulled her face to his and kissed her‚Äîdeep, wet, and aggressive. It wasn't romantic. It was a display of ownership.
He broke the kiss, a string of saliva connecting them, and then slid his hand down to grope her breast, squeezing hard enough to make Yubelluna wince slightly, though she kept smiling.
Riser: "Do you see, Pawn? They are mine. Body and soul. They live to serve me. They die for me. That is the privilege of the Phenex. You will never be on my level."

Issei stared. Initially, Ariel saw the flash of Envy in Issei's eyes‚Äîthe desire for that kind of attention.

Issei‚Äôs gauntlet flashed green.
Issei: "THAT'S NOT A HAREM! THAT'S SLAVERY, YOU BASTARD!"
[BOOST!]
Issei charged. He didn't have a plan. He just wanted to smash Riser‚Äôs face.
Riser: "Mira."
Riser‚Äôs Rook, a tall woman with a staff, stepped in. She swung her weapon.
CRACK.
Issei took the hit to the ribs. He was sent flying across the room, crashing into the sofa and overturning the tea table.
Asia: "Issei-san!"
5. The Intervention (Ariel‚Äôs Turn)
Riser looked bored. He lit a small ball of Hellfire in his hand, tossing it up and down.
Riser: "Disappointing. Rias, your servants are unruly. And what about this one?"
Riser looked at the corner. At Ariel.
Ariel was leaning against the wall. He wasn't looking at Riser with fear. He was looking at him with Disgust.
Riser: "You. Human. You've been staring at my Queen. You want her?"
Ariel pushed off the wall. He walked forward, limping slightly.
Ariel: "She's beautiful. Yeah, I stared. I'm a guy."
Rias tensed. Ariel, don't provoke him.
Ariel: "But watching you touch her... it made me sick. You make 'Harem King' sound like a job for a scumbag."

Riser: "Burn."

Issei: "ARIEL! MOVE!"
Ariel didn't move.
Echo‚Äôs tail slapped his neck: [IMPACT. FACE. 0.5 SECONDS.]
Ariel's Internal Monologue:
No dodging. If I dodge, he thinks I'm scared. If I'm scared, I'm a background character.
Be the Wall.
Ariel took a breath. Bio-Feedback.
Hardening. Core. Shoulder. Forearm.
[Technique: Iron Body (Tekkai) - Focused Defense]
He didn't backhand it this time. He punched it.
He threw a straight right cross directly into the center of the magic flame.
BOOM.
The fireball exploded against his fist.
The magic tried to burn him. The heat was agonizing. It felt like sticking his hand in a deep fryer.
But his Will (Veritas) refused to let the fire pass his knuckles. He forced his muscles to be denser than the flame.
The fire scattered, dying out.
Ariel stood there, his fist smoking, his knuckles blackened and bleeding, his sleeve incinerated up to the elbow.
Ariel: "Is that it? I thought Phoenix fire was supposed to be hot."

The silence in the room was absolute.
Yubelluna stared at the human who had punched fire.
Riser‚Äôs arrogance cracked for the first time.

Ariel: "I didn't block it. I broke it."

Ariel: "Issei. Get up."
Issei groaned, standing up, his eyes burning with renewed fire.
Issei: "Yeah. I'm up."
Ariel: "He insulted your dream. He insulted Rias. And he burned my favorite shirt."
Ariel turned back to Riser.
Ariel: "We challenge you. Not a brawl. A Rating Game. If Issei wins, you leave Rias alone. And you apologize to your Queen for treating her like garbage."
Riser laughed. It was a loud, forced laugh to cover his confusion.
Riser: "A Game? Against trash? Fine! I accept! Ten days! I will crush you both and burn this school to ash!"
He vanished in a pillar of fire. Grayfia bowed politely and faded away.
7. The Aftermath
The adrenaline crashed. Ariel hissed, clutching his burned hand.
Ariel: "Okay... that hurt way more than I pretended it did."
Koneko was at his side instantly. She looked at his blackened knuckles. She didn't call him an idiot this time.
She looked at his face.
Koneko: "You punched fire."
Ariel: "It seemed like the logical option."
Rias walked over. She took Ariel‚Äôs hand gently, applying healing magic. Her eyes were filled with a complex mix of gratitude and calculation.
Rias: "Ariel... you truly are the Variable. I accept the challenge. We are going to the mountains."
Issei: "We're gonna train! I'm gonna smash that guy's face in!"
Ariel looked at his healed (but scarred) hand.
I survived one fireball. But in a Rating Game, he'll throw a thousand. I need to get stronger. I need Haki.

I want to ask about will training to nulify abilities. Should we insert it here or not? Or not at all?

Yes, we must insert it here.
If Ariel punches Riser's Hellfire in Chapter 13 without having practiced the specific Intent to Nullify (or at least the concept of "Rejecting Energy"), it will feel like a plot hole or unearned plot armor.
However, at his current level (SPR 0.35), he cannot master true Nullification (which requires high Haki).
The Compromise: We insert a training session where he attempts the "Concept of Rejection." He doesn't master it, but he learns enough to disperse energy rather than stopping it cold. This explains why he can stop the fireball but still gets his arm burned‚Äîit's an imperfect technique.
Here is the addition to Chapter 12, inserting this critical training on Friday Night.
‚ûï Chapter 12 (Addendum): The Wall of Will
Timeline: Friday Night (Day 6).
Location: Ariel‚Äôs Apartment (PTD).
üìÖ Day 6 (Night): The Concept of "No"
Focus: Energy Resistance / Nullification Theory.
Ariel was tired from the "Bully Module," but he couldn't sleep. He kept thinking about Raynare's light spear.
Physical density (Iron Body) stops swords. But what stops light? What stops fire?
Ariel: "System. If a Logia user turns into fire, I can't punch them with just muscles. I need to touch the 'Substance' beneath the element."
He pulled up the archive of Rayleigh explaining Haki.
"Armament Haki creates an invisible armor. It can touch the substantial body of a Devil Fruit user."
Ariel: "I don't have the Spirit to make invisible armor yet. But maybe I can project the Intent."
The Simulation:
Scenario: The Steam Vent.
Threat: A continuous jet of high-pressure, scalding steam blocking a doorway.
Goal: Walk through it without burning.
Attempt 1: Ariel walked in. He tightened his muscles (Iron Body).
Result: The heat bypassed his muscles and cooked his skin. Failure.
"GAH! Hot! Physics still apply!"
Attempt 2 (The Paradigm Shift):
Ariel sat before the steam. He remembered Aizen from Bleach. Aizen didn't just block; he crushed the opponent's Reiatsu (Energy) with his own.
He remembered Shanks blocking Akainu's magma.
Ariel: "It's not about enduring the heat. It's about denying the heat's right to exist in my space."
He focused on his SPR (0.35). It was a small, grey spark.
He didn't try to coat his whole body. He pushed that spark into his right hand.
He visualized a wall. A mental command: "Nothing passes this point."
He thrust his hand into the steam.
He didn't feel the heat on his skin. He felt a pressure against his Will.
The steam parted around his hand for 0.5 seconds before his concentration broke and he got burned again.
Ariel: "I felt it. For a second... the heat didn't touch me. I pushed it away."
He spent the rest of the night trying to hold that "Rejection" for longer.
He managed to hold it for 1 second.
[System Update: Nullification Intent (Rudimentary) - Unlocked. Effect: Reduces Energy Damage by 30%.]
üß† Why This Matters for Chapter 13
Now, when Ariel punches Riser's fireball:
 * Iron Body (PHY): Protects his bones from the impact force.
 * Nullification Intent (SPR): Disperses the magic holding the fire together.
 * The Injury: Because his Nullification is only "Rudimentary" (30% reduction), he still gets his sleeve burned off and his skin blistered.
This makes the victory tactical and earned, rather than magical.

üìï Chapter 14: The Mountain of Hell and the Tactician's Table

Yes, absolutely. Both training sessions address critical holes in Ariel's defense and offense.
