This is the critical juncture where Ren's divergence solidifies. He doesn't abandon his heroes; he just realizes he has to translate their language into one his broken spirit can speak.
Here is Chapter 3: The False Dream and The Rotting Fist.
üåë Chapter 3: The False Dream and The Rotting Fist
Timeline: Monday (The Day After the Park Incident).
Location: Kuoh Academy / The Abandoned Park.
1. The Morning After (The Wall of Silence)
Ren walked into class 2-B. His arms were stiff, phantom pains radiating from where the bones had snapped the night before. Rias's magic was flawless physically, but the memory of the crack remained.
He saw Issei. The protagonist looked... fine. Better than fine. He was glowing with a nervous, excited energy. He was staring at Rias Gremory (who was sitting in her usual seat) with a blush on his face.
Ren's Internal Monologue:
He died yesterday. I watched the light leave his eyes. And now he's blushing at the girl who treated me like a stray dog.
The Perverted Trio Reunion:
Matsuda and Motohama rushed Issei.
Matsuda: "Issei! You traitor! You got a girlfriend and ditched us!"
Issei: (Laughing nervously) "Ah, no! She... uh... moved away! It didn't work out!"
Issei looked at Ren. His eyes darted away. Guilt. Rias had ordered him to keep the Devil world secret.
Issei: "Hey, Ren. Crazy weekend, huh?"
Ren: "Yeah. Crazy."
2. The Roof (Veritas)
Lunchtime. Ren dragged Issei to the roof. He didn't beat around the bush.
Ren: "Drop the act, Issei. You're terrible at lying."
Issei flinched. "What act? Yuuma just‚Äî"
Ren: "Yuuma was a Fallen Angel. She put a light spear through your stomach. I tackled you. She broke my arms. Then the Crimson-Haired Princess showed up and resurrected you."
Issei stared, his mouth gaping. "You... you remember? Buchou said she wiped your memory!"
Ren: "She tried. I guess I'm too stubborn to forget." (Ren tapped his temple). "Veritas, remember? I don't do lies."
Issei slumped against the railing, sliding down to sit on the concrete.
Issei: "It's true. I'm a Devil now, Ren. Rias-senpai... she saved me. I'm her Pawn."
Issei looked at his hand.
Issei: "It's kinda terrifying. But... she's giving me a chance. To be strong. To be the Harem King for real."
Ren looked at his friend. He saw the hope. He felt the pang of Envy‚Äîsharp and hot.
He got a reset button. He got a new game plus.
But Ren forced a smile. It was a genuine smile, strained by pain.
Ren: "That's awesome, man. Seriously. You're living the anime life."
Issei: "I can't tell anyone else. But... I'm glad you know. I was scared I'd have to lie to you forever."
Ren: "We're the Perverted Trio. We don't lie about the important stuff."
Ren offered a fist bump. Issei bumped it.
Ren felt the difference immediately. Issei's fist felt heavy. Solid. Even without the Gauntlet, the Devil physiology was already making him denser.
Ren‚Äôs hand felt frail in comparison.
3. The Dark Grind (After School)
Ren skipped the peeping mission that afternoon.
Ren: "I have to study math."
Issei: "Since when do you study?"
Ren: "Since I realized I'm falling behind."
He went to the park. The sun was setting. The same park where they almost died.
Goal: Armament Hardening (Busoshoku Haki).
Inspiration: Monkey D. Garp. The Fist of Love. Pure physical density + Spiritual armor.
Ren stood before the large oak tree. He wrapped his hands in bandages to hide the bruising.
Ren: "Okay. The theory is sound. Visualizing the armor. Push the Spirit out. Make it solid."
He closed his eyes. He visualized Garp punching a mountain. He visualized the shiny black sheen of Haki.
He threw a punch.
THUD.
Pain shot up his wrist. The bark didn't crack. His skin split.
Ren: "Again."
THUD.
"Focus! Don't just hit it! Will it to break!"
THUD.
Blood soaked the bandages.
Ren panted, leaning his forehead against the rough bark.
Ren: "Why? Ariel (in his imagination/dreams) could do this. The legends can do this. I'm putting in the effort. I'm not afraid of the pain. Why is the output zero?"
4. The Discovery of the "Void Shift"
Ren sat at the base of the tree, exhausted. The sun vanished. The shadows lengthened.
He felt the Envy again.
Issei is probably learning magic right now. He's probably with Rias. He's getting stronger by existing.
Ren: "It's not fair."
He didn't suppress the thought. He let it sit in his chest. It felt cold. Heavy.
He looked at his hand in the dark.
Instead of trying to visualize "Garp's Light" or "Burning Spirit," he visualized the Cold.
Ren: "If I can't be hard like a diamond... maybe I can be heavy like lead."
He channeled the Despair.
I am nothing. I am the guy who got left behind.
The shadows around his hand seemed to deepen. It wasn't the shiny black of Haki. It was a matte, light-absorbing grey. A faint wisp of smoke curled off his knuckles.
Ren: "Dark... Armament?"
He stood up. He approached the tree again.
He didn't try to break the tree. He tried to infect it with his heaviness.
He punched.
He didn't shout. He exhaled.
Thump.
The sound was different. It wasn't a sharp crack. It was a muffled, dead sound. Like hitting a bag of wet sand.
Ren pulled his hand back.
There was no crater. The bark wasn't shattered.
But where his fist had connected, the wood had turned grey and brittle. A circle of rot. He touched it, and the wood crumbled into dust under his finger.
Ren: "I didn't break it with force. I... dampened its structure."
5. The Verdict
Ren looked at his hand. The "Darkness" faded.
It wasn't the heroic destruction of Garp. Garp breaks things with power.
Ren had broken it by entropy. By introducing a void that the wood couldn't survive.
Ren: "It's ugly. It's not what Garp does."
He clenched his fist.
Ren: "But it worked."
He resumed his stance.
Ren: "I don't care if it's ugly. I don't care if it's dark. If it lets me stand next to them... I'll use it."
He punched the tree again. And again.
Not training to be a "Hero of Light," but training to perfect the Rotting Fist.
üìà Status Update
 * Ren:
   * Friendship: Maintained with Issei, but a "Secret Wall" exists.
   * Ability Unlocked: Void Armament (Prototype). It doesn't harden his skin (he still takes damage); it erodes the target's durability/kinetic energy upon contact.
   * Mental State: Determined but darkening. He accepts the negative emotion as a necessary tool.
Your Move:
The timeline moves to the Asia Arc (The Church).
Do you want to:
 * The Encounter: Ren is with Issei when they meet Asia. Ren uses his Observation (Sense of Void) to realize Asia is "hollow" or "doomed" before anyone else, spotting the Fallen Angel watchers instantly because he is attuned to their wavelength.
 * The Training Session (Part 2): Ren tries to spar with a human (maybe the Kendo club or a thug) to test his new "Rotting Fist" on a person, realizing it hurts him just as much as them (recoil damage).

Do what you think is best.

This is the pivotal moment where Ren realizes the cost of his new path. Unlike Ariel, whose power is clean and heroic, Ren‚Äôs power is ugly and parasitic. It hurts the user as much as the target.
We will combine the Live Combat Test and the Asia Encounter to show the stark contrast between Ren's grim reality and Issei's harem-protagonist optimism.
Here is Chapter 4: The Sickening Fist and The Empty Girl.
üåë Chapter 4: The Sickening Fist and The Empty Girl
Timeline: Tuesday Afternoon (After School).
Location: Back Alley near Kuoh Academy / The Park.
1. The Live Test (The Ugly Truth)
Ren didn't go straight to the park. He needed to know if his "Void Armament" worked on flesh. A tree doesn't fight back; a person does.
He found a group of thugs from a neighboring technical high school harassing a Kendo club junior.
Ren: "Hey. Leave him alone."
Thug Leader: "Hah? You want to play hero, Kuoh-boy?"
The leader swung a baseball bat.
Ren didn't dodge. He stepped in.
Ren's Thought: Focus on the Cold. Reject the kinetic energy. Accept the Void.
He caught the bat with his left hand.
[Technique: Void Dampening]
The bat didn't stop abruptly; it felt like it hit a pool of tar. The momentum just... died.
The thug blinked. "What the‚Äî?"
Ren clenched his right fist. He didn't harden it. He filled it with Entropy.
Punch.
He struck the thug in the solar plexus.
It wasn't a satisfying smack. It was a wet thud.
The thug‚Äôs eyes rolled back. He collapsed instantly, retching. Where Ren had hit him, the skin wasn't just bruised; it was grey and cold to the touch, as if the life force had been sucked out of the tissue.
The Backlash:
Ren stumbled back, clutching his own stomach. He fell to his knees and dry-heaved.
His right hand felt numb, like he had slept on it for hours. The cold was spreading up his arm.
Ren: "It... it eats me too."
He looked at the unconscious thug. It wasn't a heroic victory. It looked like he had poisoned the guy.
Ren: "Issei gets a cool dragon claw. I get... frostbite and nausea. Figures."
2. The Meeting (The Park)
Ren washed his face in a public fountain to hide the paleness. He wrapped his "rotting" hand in a bandage. He met Issei at the park bench.
Issei: "Ren! There you are! You look terrible, man."
Ren: "Bad lunch. So, the Fallen Angels are active?"
Issei: "Yeah. I can feel... something. My Gauntlet keeps twitching."
Then, she appeared.
Asia Argento tripped out of the bushes, landing face-first.
"Ouchie..."
Issei blushed. "A nun? She's cute!"
Ren looked at her. He activated his Observation (Void Sense).
To Ariel, she looked like a beacon of Kindness.
To Ren, she looked like a Hollow Shell.
Ren's Perspective:
He didn't see a golden aura. He saw a girl who had no tether to the world. She felt like she was already dead, just waiting for gravity to realize it.
She‚Äôs just like me, Ren realized with a jolt of sympathy. She doesn't belong here.
3. The Interaction (Veritas)
Issei helped her up. "Are you okay? I'm Hyoudou Issei!"
Asia smiled, but Ren saw the cracks in it. "I am Asia Argento. I am lost."
Ren stepped forward. He didn't try to be cool. He spoke softly.
Ren: "You're not just lost on the map, are you?"
Asia looked at him, startled. She saw Ren‚Äôs eyes‚Äîdark, tired, and honest.
Asia: "I... pardon?"
Ren: "You have the eyes of someone who is waiting to be punished."
Issei elbowed Ren. "Dude! Don't be creepy!"
Ren: "I'm being honest, Issei. Look at her. No luggage. No phone. Walking into a Devil-controlled territory alone. Asia, who sent you here?"
Asia shrank back. "I... I follow the Lord's guidance."
Ren: "The Lord doesn't send sheep into a wolf den without a shepherd. Someone is using you as bait."
Asia began to tremble. Ren sighed. He hated being right.
He reached out with his uninjured hand (the left one) and gently patted her head.
Ren: "It's okay. I'm used to being bait too."
Asia looked up at him. For the first time, her smile reached her eyes. It wasn't a "Saintly" smile; it was a lonely girl finding another lonely soul.
Asia: "You are very kind, mister..."
Ren: "Ren. Just Ren. The guy in the background."
4. The Shadow on the Hill
They walked her to the church. Ren walked behind them, his bandaged hand throbbing with a dull, cold ache.
He scanned the tree line.
Ren's Observation:
He didn't sense "Killing Intent." He sensed Empty Spaces in the foliage where birds weren't singing.
There. And there.
Two watchers. He felt the pressure of their gaze. It felt heavy, arrogant.
Issei: "This place gives me the creeps."
Ren: "It should. It smells like a trap."
They reached the gate. Asia turned to them.
Asia: "Thank you. Please... don't come closer. It is dangerous."
Ren: "We know."
Issei: "We can't just leave you!"
Ren: "Issei." Ren grabbed Issei's shoulder. His grip was weak, but firm. "We leave. Now."
Issei: "But‚Äî!"
Ren: "Look at my hand, Issei." Ren held up the bandaged, trembling fist. "I fought a thug earlier. Just a human. And I almost passed out. If we fight a Fallen Angel tonight, we die. And she dies in the crossfire."
Issei looked at Ren's pale face. He realized his friend wasn't being cowardly; he was being Real.
Issei: "Okay. We retreat."
They watched Asia walk into the dark church.
As the doors closed, Ren looked up at the steeple. He saw the black-winged silhouette (Raynare).
He didn't glare with "Killing Intent" like Ariel.
He stared with Dead Calm.
I see you. You think I'm nothing. You're right. But even nothing can choke you.
5. The Vow
They walked back to the city in silence.
Issei: "She's gonna die in there, isn't she?"
Ren: "Probably. Unless we change the script."
Issei: "How? You're hurt. I'm... I'm just a Pawn."
Ren stopped. He looked at a streetlamp flickering in the dark.
Ren: "Light attracts monsters, Issei. You be the Light. You be the Hero. Charge in the front door. Scream. Glow. Be the distraction."
Issei: "And you?"
Ren looked at his "Rotting Hand." He clenched it, ignoring the nausea.
Ren: "I'll be the Shadow. I won't fight fair. I won't fight honorably. I'm going to sneak in the back and stab them in the kidneys while they're looking at you."
Ren: "You save the girl. I'll bury the trash."

   * Power: Void Fist (Touch of Decay) confirmed effective but causes self-harm (Stamina Drain/Nausea).

   * Relationship: Connected with Asia through shared loneliness.
 * Issei: Realizes Ren is hurting himself to keep up. Feels guilty but motivated.

üåë Chapter 5: The Sewer Rat and The Stray Dog
Timeline: Thursday (The Day of the Ritual).
Location: Kuoh Hardware District / The Abandoned Church.
1. The Preparation (The Weapons of the Weak)
Ren skipped school. He stood in the hardware store aisle, staring at the shelves. His bandaged hand throbbed‚Äîa constant reminder that he was fragile.
Ren's Internal Monologue:
I don't know what we're walking into. Magic? Lasers? Monsters? I can't fight those.
I need to bring the fight down to the gutter.
He didn't buy high-tech gadgets. He bought street weapons.
 * Bear Mace (Capsicum Spray): If they have eyes, they can be blinded.
 * Bag of Fine Sand: For throwing. Oldest trick in the book.
 * Steel Pipe (threaded end): A sword breaks. A pipe just bends.
 * Duct Tape: To strap his broken hand tight so he can still punch.
He walked out of the store. He felt ridiculous.
Ren: "Issei gets a magic dragon gauntlet. I get a pipe and sand. This really is a Kusoge (Trash Game)."
2. The Scouting (The Path of the Rat)
Time: 5:00 PM (One hour before sunset).
Ren met Issei at the park. Issei was vibrating with anxiety.
Issei: "I'm ready! I practiced the Boost! I can hold it for... like, twelve seconds!"
Ren: "Good. Because you're the distraction."
Ren laid out a rough map he drew on a napkin.
Ren: "I scouted the perimeter. The front door is thick oak. You kick that down. Make noise. Scream about being the Harem King. Draw every eye in the room."
Issei: "And you?"
Ren pointed to a squiggly line on the back of the church.
Ren: "There's a storm drain. It leads into the crypts beneath the altar. The grate is rusted through."
Issei: "Dude... you're going in through the sewer? That's gross."
Ren: "Heroes use the front door, Issei. Rats use the walls. I'm going to pop up behind them while they're laughing at you."
Ren looked Issei in the eye. Veritas.
Ren: "I'm not strong enough to fight them fair, Issei. If I stand next to you, I'm just a hostage. I have to be the knife they don't see."
Issei nodded, solemn. "Okay. I'll be loud. I'll be the loudest decoy ever."
3. The Assault (The Light and The Shadow)
Time: Sunset.
The Front Door:
Issei: "HEY! BIRD-LADY! GIVE BACK MY FRIEND!"
CRASH.
Issei kicked the doors open. He was glowing green. He screamed his heart out. The Fallen Angels inside laughed, mocking the "Pawn" who came to die.
The Sewer:
Ren was crawling through muck. It smelled of rot and old water. He held his breath, forcing his Observation (Void Sense) to expand.
Above me. Three signatures. One big (Freed?), two floating (Angels).
He reached the grate under the altar. He pushed it up silently.
He emerged in the shadows behind the pulpit. He was covered in filth, but his eyes were cold and focused.
He saw Asia tied to the cross.
He saw Freed Sellzen, the white-haired priest, laughing at Issei.
He saw Raynare hovering above.
Ren: Target identified. The Priest is the threat on the ground.
4. The Ambush (Ren vs. Freed)
Freed drew his Light Sword and Light Gun.
Freed: "A devil? No, a stray human! I'll gut you like a fish!"
Freed dashed at Issei. Issei braced himself.
Ren: Now.
Ren didn't shout. He burst from the shadows behind the altar.
He didn't punch. He threw the Sand.
POOF.
A cloud of grit hit Freed in the face mid-dash.
Freed: "GAH! MY EYES!"
Freed stumbled, slashing blindly.
Ren stepped in. He swung the Steel Pipe.
CLANG.
He hit Freed in the wrist holding the gun. The gun clattered away.
Freed: "You dirty little‚Äî!"
Ren didn't stop. He used a Low Kick (Mori Dan style), aiming for the knee.
Freed buckled.
Ren tackled him. It wasn't a martial arts move; it was a street brawl. They rolled on the floor.
Issei: "Ren!"
Ren: "Get Asia! I'll hold the psycho!"
5. The Void Glitch (The Awakening)
Ren was on top of Freed, trying to pin him.
But Freed was an enhanced human. He was stronger.
Freed: "Get off me, sewer rat!"
Freed headbutted Ren. Blood sprayed from Ren's nose. Ren fell back.
Freed scrambled up, wiping the sand from his eyes. He grabbed his Light Sword.
Freed: "I'm going to carve your heart out and eat it!"
He swung the sword down at Ren‚Äôs neck.
Ren looked at the blade.
I can't dodge. I can't block with a pipe (it will slice through).
I'm going to die.
Fear hit him. Then, Acceptance.
If I die... at least I wasn't useless.
He raised his hand instinctively.
Ren's Thought: Be empty. Be nothing. If there's nothing there, he can't cut it.
He channeled the Void.
The shadows in the corner of the church seemed to lurch toward him.
His hand didn't turn black or hard. It turned Blurry.
SWISH.
The Light Sword hit Ren‚Äôs forearm.
It didn't clang. It didn't slice.
It Flickered.
For a micro-second, the light of the sword touched Ren‚Äôs "Void" and was swallowed. The blade passed through his arm as if he were a ghost, reforming on the other side.
Freed: "What?!"
Ren: "Huh?"
Ren looked at his arm. No blood. Just a lingering sensation of extreme cold.
[Ability Unlocked: Phase Shift (Glitch). Duration: 0.1 Seconds.]
6. The Reality Check
The surprise didn't last.
Raynare: "Enough playing."
Raynare threw a Light Spear from above.
Ren‚Äôs "Glitch" was on cooldown. He couldn't phase again.
He tried to roll.
THUNK.
The spear slammed into his thigh, pinning him to the floor.
"AAAAHHH!"
Ren screamed. The pain was absolute. It felt like burning acid.
Issei: "REN!"
Issei charged, punching Freed away with the Boosted Gear. He stood over Ren.
Issei: "Hold on! I got you!"
Ren looked up. He saw Issei‚Äôs back. The Red Dragon Gauntlet was glowing, pulsing with power. Issei was holding off Freed and Raynare with sheer force of will.
Ren's Perspective:
Look at him. He's shining. He's the hero.
I threw sand. I got stabbed. I'm lying in the dirt.
Ren reached out, grabbing the handle of the light spear in his leg. His hand smoked.
Ren: "Don't... worry about me. Get... the girl."
7. The Conclusion
The rest happened in a blur.
The doors exploded. Rias Gremory arrived with her peerage.
The "Light" of the rescue was blinding. Kiba moved like lightning. Koneko threw pews. Akeno called thunder.
Ren lay on the floor, bleeding out.
He watched Rias hold Asia's body. He watched Issei cry. He watched the resurrection.
Nobody was looking at Ren. He was part of the scenery.
Eventually, Koneko walked over. She looked at the spear in his leg.
She knelt down.
Koneko: "You smell like sewage."
Ren: (Weak laugh) "Tactical... perfume."
She grabbed the spear. "This will hurt."
She pulled it out. Ren passed out from the pain.

This chapter cements the divergence. While Ariel was offered a seat at the table, Ren is offered a ticket to the exit. It highlights the cruel meritocracy of the DxD world: Power gets you recruited. Bravery just gets you healed.
Here is Chapter 6.
üåë Chapter 6: The Glitch in the Hand and The Pity of the King
Timeline: Friday Morning (The Day After the Church Raid).
Location: Kuoh General Hospital ‚Äì Room 304.
1. The White Room (Solitude)
Ren woke up.
There was no miso soup. No yelling. No harem antics.
Just the hum of the AC and the sterile smell of bleach. The room was white, empty, and silent.
He tried to move his right leg. It was heavy, wrapped in a cast. His nose was taped up. His chest felt like it had been trampled by a horse.
Ren: "I'm alive."
He looked at the bedside table. There was a cheap vase with store-bought flowers. The card read: ‚ÄúGet well soon! - Issei & Asia.‚Äù
They weren't here. They were probably registering Asia for school. They were living the "Slice of Life" episode. Ren was living the "Medical Drama."
2. The Experiment (The Coin)
Ren looked at his left hand‚Äîthe one that had phased through Freed's sword. It looked normal, but it felt... cold. Numb. Like he had fallen asleep on it and the blood hadn't come back.
Ren: "What was that? It wasn't speed. It wasn't armor."
He reached for a 100-yen coin on the table. He held it in his palm.
Ren: "I wanted to be empty. I wanted to be nothing."
He closed his eyes. He focused on the Envy. The feeling of being left behind in this hospital room while his best friend became a main character.
I am a ghost. I am not here.
He focused on the space between the atoms of his hand.
[Technique: Phase Shift (Glitch)]
Ching.
Ren opened his eyes.
The coin wasn't in his palm. It was on the bedsheet under his hand.
It had fallen straight through his flesh and bone. There was no blood. Just a lingering sensation of absolute freezing cold in the center of his palm.
Ren: "Intangibility. Through... rejection of mass?"
He shuddered. It didn't feel like a superpower. It felt like his body was forgetting how to exist.
Ren: "Issei gets a dragon. I get... a glitch."
3. The Visitor (The Cruel Kindness)
The door opened. Rias Gremory walked in.
She was alone. She carried a basket of high-quality fruit. She looked perfect, regal, and out of place in the sterile room.
Rias: "Ren-kun. I'm glad you're awake."
Ren: "Gremory-senpai. Where's Issei?"
Rias: "He is helping Asia settle in. He wanted to come, but I told him to wait. We need to speak privately."
She sat down. Her expression was gentle. Too gentle. It was the look one gives to a child who tried to fly and broke their leg.
Rias: "You were brave last night. Foolish, but brave. You saved my Bishop and bought time for my Pawn. The House of Gremory thanks you."
Ren: "I didn't do it for your House. I did it for my friends."
Rias: "I know. That loyalty is rare."
She leaned forward.
Rias: "But Ren... look at you. You are broken. Freed is a stray priest. He is the bottom of the barrel in our world. And he almost killed you."
Ren: "I know. I'm weak." (Veritas).
Rias: "You are Human. It is not a fault; it is biology. Issei has a Sacred Gear‚Äîa Longinus. He belongs in this world. You... do not."
4. The Participation Award (The Insult)
Rias placed her hand on his cast. A soft red light glowed, easing the pain.
Rias: "I cannot let you continue this. Next time, you won't just break a leg. You will die."
She looked him in the eyes.
Rias: "I can help you. I can use my magic to remove the memories of the last week. You can forget the Fallen Angels, the Devils, the blood. You can go back to being a normal student. You can be happy."
Ren stared at her.
For a second, he thought she was going to offer him an Evil Piece. He thought she was going to say, "Join us."
But she wasn't.
She was offering him a lobotomy.
Ren: "Happy? You mean ignorant."
Rias: "Ignorance is safety. Issei has a burden to carry. You don't have to."
Ren: "Because I'm not useful?"
Rias flinched. She hadn't meant it that way, but her silence confirmed it. She didn't see "Potential" in Ren. She saw a "Liability."
Ren: (Laughing softly) "That's funny. Issei gets a promotion. I get a eraser."
He pulled his hand away from hers.
Ren: "No."
Rias: "Ren, please be reasonable."
Ren: "I am being reasonable. I am Veritas. I don't lie to myself. If you erase my memory, you erase the only time in my life I actually mattered."
He pointed to the door.
Ren: "Keep your magic, President. I'm keeping my scars."
Rias stood up. She looked sad. She respected his choice, but she also wrote him off.
Rias: "Very well. But you are not to engage in Devil affairs again. If you do, I cannot protect you."
Ren: "I never asked you to protect me. You were the one who showed up late."
Rias stiffened. She nodded once, formally, and walked out.
Ren was alone again.
5. The Divergence
Ren stared at the fruit basket. It looked expensive. It looked like a consolation prize.
He grabbed an apple.
He tried to activate his Void again.
He squeezed.
The apple didn't phase. It bruised.
Ren: "It only works when I'm scared. Or empty."
He looked out the window. He saw Issei and Asia walking on the street below, laughing. Issei was carrying her bags. They looked like a couple. They looked like the main characters.
Ren felt the Envy curl in his gut. It wasn't hot anger anymore. It was a cold, heavy stone.
Ren: "She didn't invite me. She invited Ariel (in the other timeline), but she didn't invite me. Because Ariel punched fire. I just threw sand."
He lay back on the bed.
Ren: "Okay. Message received. The Light doesn't want me."
He held up his hand toward the ceiling light. He focused on the shadow his hand cast on the bedsheets.
Ren: "If the Light burns me... then I'll learn to live in the Shadow."

 * Ren:
   * Status: Rejected by the Devil Faction (Socially).
   * Ability: Phase Shift confirmed (Requires "Empty Mindset").

Your Move:
The timeline moves toward the Riser Phenex Arc.
Do you want to:
 * The Invisible Training Camp: Ren is not invited to the mountain training (because he's human/injured). He is left behind in Kuoh. He trains alone in the sewers or abandoned buildings, developing his Darkness in isolation while the heroes bond.

Beautiful, it touches my heart, and probably many others as the spotlights are limited (personal praise to you). The next options are both great, so it is hard for me to choose. What would you choose or integrate both? Ren did not witness Riser humiliate Issei?

This is a heavy, emotional path, but it is the most honest one for this character.
The Integration Strategy:
We will combine the Pity Invite with the Invisible Training.
Ren missed the Riser encounter (because he wasn't in the clubroom; he was in the hospital/recovering). This means he has no personal beef with Riser yet. He only knows that his best friend is fighting a war, and he is currently peeling potatoes on the sidelines.
This creates the perfect "Oikawa" Dynamic: He is physically present with the heroes, but spiritually miles away.
Here is Chapter 7: The Cook, The Camp, and The Gap.
üåë Chapter 7: The Cook, The Camp, and The Gap
Timeline: The Start of the 10-Day Training Camp.
Location: Kuoh Academy / Gremory Mountain Villa.
1. The News from the Sidelines
Ren returned to school on Monday. His leg was in a brace, his hand taped up.
The school was buzzing. Rumors of "Issei Hyoudou challenging a senior" were everywhere.
Ren found Issei at lunch. Issei looked stressed, tired, but... important.
Issei: "Ren! Man, you missed it! This guy, Riser Phenex, came in with fire wings! He toasted the clubroom! I punched him in the face!"
Ren sat down, opening his bento.
Ren: "You punched a High-Class Devil?"
Issei: "Yeah! I have to fight him in a Rating Game in ten days. If I win, Rias is free. If I lose... well, I won't lose!"
Ren's Internal Monologue:
While I was staring at the hospital ceiling, Issei started a war. I wasn't even an extra in the scene. I was off-screen.
Ren: "That's huge, Issei. You're really doing it. You're the protagonist."
Issei: "We're going to the mountains to train. It's gonna be hell." Issei paused. He looked at Ren‚Äôs leg brace. "I... I wish you could come, man. We need the 'Strategist'."
Ren smiled. It was a sad, honest smile.
Ren: "I can't run, Issei. And I don't have magic. I'd just be baggage."
2. The Pity Invite
That afternoon, outside the Old School Building. The Peerage was loading the car.
Issei was arguing with Rias.
Issei: "Please, Buchou! He saved Asia! He's part of the team!"
Rias: "Issei, be reasonable. He is a human with a fractured leg. The training we are doing involves high-level demolition magic. It is not safe for him."
Issei: "He can... he can cook! Yeah! He makes amazing curry! If he cooks, we don't have to waste time making food! We can train more!"
Ren stood by the gate, listening.
I'm being hired as the chef. Not the tactician. The help.
He wanted to say no. His pride screamed at him to walk away.
But he looked at Asia. She looked terrified of the upcoming battle.
He looked at Issei. His friend was desperate for support.
Ren: (Walking up) "I make good stew, too. And I can clean weapons."
Rias looked at him. She sighed, relenting.
Rias: "Very well. If you are willing to work as support staff, you may come. But you stay in the Safe Zone. No wandering off."
Ren: "Understood. Safe Zone."
3. The View from the Kitchen Window
Location: The Mountain Villa. Day 3.
The training was intense.
Through the kitchen window, Ren watched.
 * Issei was running up the mountain carrying tires, screaming his lungs out.
 * Kiba was moving so fast he was invisible, cutting leaves into confetti.
 * Koneko was lifting boulders.
 * Akeno was blasting the sky with lightning.
Ren looked down at his hands. He was peeling potatoes.
Peel. Chop. Drop in water.
Ren: "Garp destroyed mountains with his fist. I'm destroying root vegetables."
He felt the Envy. It was a cold, suffocating pressure in his chest.
Why couldn't I have a Gear? Just a small one. A sword. A shield. Anything.
Asia ran into the kitchen to get water bottles. She was sweating, exhausted from magic training.
Asia: "Ren-san! The stew smells wonderful!"
Ren: "Thanks, Asia. How's Issei?"
Asia: "He... he unlocked a new move! He can boost for 10 seconds now! He's amazing!"
Ren: "Yeah. Amazing."
He smiled at her. As soon as she left, the smile dropped like a stone.
He looked at the potato in his hand.
He channeled his Void.
Absorb. Decay.
The potato turned grey and withered in seconds.
Ren: "I can kill a potato. Tremble before me."
4. The Night Grind (The Shadow in the Woods)
Time: 2:00 AM.
The Devils were asleep. Magic drained stamina.
Ren was awake. His leg hurt, but his heart hurt more.
He sneaked out the back door, limping into the woods away from the Safe Zone.
Ren: "I can't lift boulders. I can't run fast. But I have this... coldness."
He stood before a tree.
Goal: Replicate Observation Haki.
Reality: He couldn't sense "Life." He couldn't sense the birds or the bugs.
Ren: "Stop trying to be Ariel (The Ideal). Be Ren (The Reality)."
He closed his eyes. He stopped looking for Presence. He looked for Absence.
He felt the gaps between the trees. He felt the silence between the owl hoots.
He felt a "Hole" in the air to his left.
Duck.
A bat flew through the space where his head was.
Ren: "Passive Void. I can sense... empty paths."
He looked at his hand.
Goal: Replicate Armament Hardening.
Reality: He couldn't make his skin hard.
Ren: "If I can't block the force... maybe I can catch it."
He gathered the shadows around his feet. He poured his Inferiority into them.
The shadows didn't become armor. They became Sticky.
He punched the tree.
Thump.
He didn't pull his hand back. He let the shadow "stick" to the bark.
He pulled.
A chunk of bark ripped off, dissolved into grey dust.
Ren: "It's not a punch. It's a bite. My darkness... eats."
It was weak. It was slow. But it was his.
5. The Spar (The Reality Check)
Time: Day 7. Afternoon.
The peerage was taking a break. Issei was high on adrenaline.
Issei: "I feel great! I feel like I could punch a hole in the moon!"
Ren walked out with a tray of lemonade.
Ren: "Hey, Issei. Spar with me."
The group went silent.
Rias: "Ren-kun, your leg."
Ren: "I'm not moving much. Just... hand-to-hand. No magic. No Boosted Gear. Just technique."
Issei looked at Rias. She nodded slowly. "Be careful, Issei. He is fragile."
Fragile. The word burned Ren like acid.
They squared up.
Ren: "Don't hold back."
Issei: "I won't!" (He was lying).
Issei threw a punch. It was slow. Telegraphed. He was treating Ren like glass.
Ren saw the pity in the punch.
Ren: (Veritas) "Don't you dare pity me!"
Ren stepped in. He used his Void Sense to slip past the slow punch.
He used his Rotting Fist (Void Dampening) on Issei‚Äôs stomach.
Thud.
Issei gasped. It felt like the air had been sucked out of his lungs. The cold shock startled him.
Instinctively‚Äîdefensively‚ÄîIssei‚Äôs body reacted.
[BOOST!]
The Gauntlet manifested for a split second. A shockwave of Dragon Power blasted out.
BOOM.
Ren was blown back. He flew ten feet, crashing into the dirt. His bad leg twisted.
He lay there, staring at the sky.
Issei: "REN! Oh god, I'm sorry! It just‚Äîit reacted!"
Issei ran over, helping him up. "Are you okay?!"
Ren looked at Issei‚Äôs panicked face. He looked at the Gauntlet.
A normal punch from Ren made Issei‚Äôs automatic defense nearly kill Ren.
Ren: "I'm fine."
He pushed Issei‚Äôs hand away and stood up, dusting himself off.
Ren: "I'm going to start dinner. Curry tonight."
He walked back to the house. He didn't look back.
His back was straight. He didn't cry.
But inside, the last piece of "Hope" had just cracked.
No matter how hard I train... I am just a trigger for his power.

üåë Chapter 11: The Shadow Library and The Meditation of the Void
Timeline: Three Days before the Wedding.
Location: Ren‚Äôs Apartment / The Night Park.
1. The Acceptance of the Stain
Ren stood in his apartment. It was dark. He hadn't paid the electricity bill‚Äînot because he was broke, but because he preferred the dark.
On his wall, he still had the posters of Luffy, Goku, and Naruto.
He didn't tear them down. He looked at them with a deep, aching respect.

He looked at his hand. The black necrosis from the Riser fight had faded, but the skin remained greyish and cold. The Darkness wasn't a temporary buff anymore; it was his biology.
Ren: "Ariel (the ideal) climbs the mountain in the sun. I have to climb it from the inside, through the caves. But we are climbing the same mountain."
2. The Dark Syllabus (Reviewing the Legends)
Ren went to the park at midnight. It was raining.
He needed to codify his power. He needed to translate the "Library of Legends" into a language his broken body could speak.
Ren: "Okay. Let's review the curriculum. Adaptation Strategy: Void Shift."
A. One Piece: The Haki of the Abyss
Ren punched the air.
Goal: Armament Haki (Busoshoku).
Original Concept: Invisible armor. Hardening the spirit.
Ren‚Äôs Reality: He couldn't harden. He lacked the "burning spirit."
The Adaptation:
Ren pulled the shadows around his fist. They didn't harden; they swirled like a black hole.
Ren: "I can't bounce the attack back. So I'll catch it."
He punched a stone pillar. Instead of cracking the stone, his fist sank into it slightly, the stone turning to dust where he touched it.
[Technique: Void Armament (Blackbeard Style)]
Function: Absorbs kinetic energy and rot matter. It‚Äôs not a shield; it‚Äôs a hungry mouth.
B. Naruto: The Chidori of Sorrow
Ren held his hand open.
Goal: Lightning Release / Rasengan.
Original Concept: Focusing vital energy into a visible form.
Ren‚Äôs Reality: He had no Chakra. He had Envy.
The Adaptation:
He focused his self-loathing into his palm. It didn't spark with electricity. It hissed with Entropy. A ball of violet, unstable gravity formed. It sounded like a thousand whispering voices.
[Technique: Dark Impulse (Sasuke/Xehanort Style)]
Function: A close-range blast of rejection force. It doesn't shock; it pushes the world away.
C. Bleach: The Cero of Nothingness
Ren pointed a finger.
Goal: Cero / Kido.
Original Concept: Spiritual Pressure firing a beam.
Ren‚Äôs Reality: He felt empty.
The Adaptation:
He remembered Ulquiorra Cifer. The aspect of Emptiness.
He compressed the air in front of his finger using his Void. He couldn't fire a beam yet, but he could fire a "Bullet" of vacuum.
Pop.
A small hole appeared in the tree trunk. Not burned, just deleted.
[Technique: Void Bullet.]
D. Kingdom Hearts: The Key to the Heart
This was the core. The glue holding his shattered style together.
Goal: A Weapon.
Original Concept: The Keyblade. A weapon of light/heart.
The Adaptation:
Ren reached into his chest. He pulled out the feeling of being the "Third Wheel." The feeling of watching Issei get the girl.
The shadows coalesced. A jagged, reverse-blade sword formed in his grip. It looked like a stained-glass window made of obsidian.
[Weapon: Soul Eater (Prototype).]
Ren: "It's ugly. It's jagged. It fits me."
3. The Final Practice (Mastering the Toolkit)
For the next two nights, Ren didn't sleep. He drilled these corrupted techniques until his body screamed.
He fought imaginary Devils.
 * Parry with Soul Eater.
 * Absorb the counter-attack with Void Armament.
 * Blast them back with Dark Impulse.
He was clumsy. He tripped. He hurt himself.
But every time he fell, the Darkness caught him. It was getting easier to move. The "Lag" between his thought and the Shadow was vanishing.
Ren: "I'm not a master. I'm still a novice. But I have a toolbox now. I'm not just throwing sand anymore."
4. The Final Day: The Goku Meditation
Timeline: The Day of the Wedding (Morning).
Location: Ren‚Äôs Apartment.
The sun was rising. The birds were singing.
Ren sat in the center of his room, legs crossed. He was dressed in the cheap black suit he would wear to the wedding. The Black Coat was folded neatly beside him.
He remembered the start of the Buu Saga. Goku in the Other World. Meditating. Visualizing.
He remembered Hunter x Hunter. Netero‚Äôs gratitude.
Ren: "I don't have gratitude. I have clarity."
He closed his eyes.
He didn't "Charge Up." He Cooled Down.
He visualized the upcoming battle.
 * Issei will be the fire.
 * Riser will be the wind.
 * I will be the vacuum that eats them both.
He regulated his breathing.
Inhale the Light.
Exhale the Dark.
He sat there for six hours. He didn't move. He didn't eat. He let his mind settle into a state of Absolute Zero.
The envy didn't vanish, but it stopped vibrating. It became a cold, still lake.
Ren's Internal Monologue:
I am ready. I know what I have to do.
I'm going to save my friends one last time.
And then... I'm going to break their hearts so they let me go.
5. The Awakening
The clock struck 4:00 PM.
Ren opened his eyes. They were clear. The whites of his eyes seemed slightly darker, the shadows under them profound.
He stood up. He picked up the Black Coat and draped it over his arm.
He looked at the posters on his wall one last time.
He saluted Goku.
Ren: "Watch me. I'm going to go Super Saiyan... my way."
He walked out the door. He didn't lock it. He knew he wasn't coming back.

Here is the revised Chapter 11, incorporating the four pillars of power (Martial Arts, Energy, Sense, Will), the lore of the Legends, and the introduction of Ren‚Äôs ultimate training ground: the Corridor of Darkness.
Chapter 11: The Corridor of Darkness
The realization hit Ren not like a physical blow, but like a cold dousing of water. He was strong, yes. But compared to the Legends of the old era, he was an infant trying to topple a mountain.
Ren sat in the silence of his quarters, running the ancient texts through his mind. The Legends didn't just possess raw strength. They had mastered the four pillars that upheld the heavens:
 * Martial Arts: The perfection of physical form and technique.
 * Energy: The ocean of Qi that fueled the body.
 * Sense: The ability to perceive the universe beyond sight and sound.
 * Will: The sheer, tangible pressure of one's intent that could crush a weaker mind.
"If I stop here," Ren whispered, clenching his fist until the knuckles turned white, "I will be nothing but a stepping stone for the true monsters."
He closed his eyes, reaching deep into the dormant part of his soul‚Äîthe part that felt like a black hole. He pulled.
The air in the room warped. The light bent and shattered. A rift tore open in the fabric of reality right before him. This was his secret. His burden. His kingdom.
The Corridor of Darkness.
Into the Abyss
Ren stepped through the rift. Instantly, the temperature plummeted to absolute zero. There was no light here, no sound, no gravity unless he willed it. This was a dimension of pure void, a place that devoured existence.
"Perfect," Ren muttered.
In the Corridor, time moved differently. Hours here were mere seconds outside. But the cost was high; the darkness constantly tried to erode his sanity and drain his life force.
He assumed a stance, the darkness swirling around his ankles like hungry smoke.
The Four Pillars
First, the Will.
The darkness pressed against his mind, a million whispering voices telling him to give up, to sleep, to die. Ren‚Äôs eyes snapped open, glowing with a faint, defiant light. He didn't just resist the pressure; he pushed back. He projected his Will outward, turning his killing intent into a physical heavy gravity that forced the swirling shadows to recede. He had to make his mind a fortress that no god nor demon could breach.
Second, the Sense.
Ren closed his eyes again. In this absolute void, eyes were useless. He had to see without looking. He visualized the flow of the chaotic energy around him. At first, it was nothing. Then, a spark. He felt the shift in the air currents, the vibration of the void. He dodged to the left‚Äîa fraction of a second later, a construct of shadow slashed through the space his head had just occupied. His Sense was sharpening, evolving from simple observation to precognition.
Third, the Energy.
He began to cycle his breath. The atmosphere in the Corridor was dense, filled with a violent, corrupted mana. Ordinary cultivators would explode if they tried to absorb it. Ren didn't just absorb it; he devoured it. He forced the chaotic energy into his meridians, purifying it through the sheer heat of his core, turning the hostile environment into fuel. His internal reservoir expanded, cracking and rebuilding stronger with every breath.
Fourth, the Martial Arts.
Ren began to move. He didn't use flashy techniques. He returned to the basics‚Äîthe strike, the block, the step. But in the Corridor, every movement required ten times the effort. He drilled the forms of the Legends, repeating a single punch ten thousand times until the air cracked with a sonic boom before his fist even fully extended.
The Monster Emerges
Hours turned into days within the void, though only minutes passed in the real world.
Ren stood amidst the swirling blackness, sweat evaporating off his skin as steam. He wasn't just surviving the Corridor anymore; he was commanding it. The shadows that once tried to eat him now curled around his arms like loyal pets, coating his limbs in armor made of the void itself.
He threw a punch. It wasn't just a physical strike.
 * It carried the perfection of Martial Arts.
 * It was propelled by boundless Energy.
 * It was guided by omniscient Sense.
 * It was hardened by an unbreakable Will.
The shockwave tore through the infinite darkness, shaking the dimension itself.
Ren exhaled, the sound echoing like a thunderclap in the silence. He stepped back toward the rift, his eyes burning with a terrifying promise.
"Let them come," he said, his voice layering with the echo of the void. "I will overpower them all."

 * Specific Training: Broke down the training scene to show him leveling up each of the four specific attributes.
 * The Goal: The ending emphasizes that this training is specifically designed to ensure he overpowers everyone in the future.

Here is the revised Chapter 11, focusing on the integration of the Legends' teachings, the unlocking of the Corridor of Darkness, and the final meditative preparation.
Chapter 11: The Synthesis of Shadows
Three days remained before the departure.
Ren stood at the precipice of his own soul, a metaphysical space he had carved out through sheer willpower. This was no longer the training hall of his youth, nor the battlefields of his past. He stood before a swirling, obsidian gate that hummed with a terrifying, abyssal resonance.
The Corridor of Darkness.
Until now, he had only dipped his toes into the shadows. Today, he would submerge.
Ren stepped forward. The darkness didn't attack him; it welcomed him. It recognized a predator, not prey. As he entered the Corridor, the laws of physics bent. Here, time moved differently, and gravity was a suggestion rather than a rule. This was the space where he would ensure that when the time came, he would not just win‚Äîhe would overpower everyone.
The Legacy of the Legends
The darkness swirled around his hands, coating his skin like liquid armor. It was seductive, promising easy power. But Ren remembered the core of his strength. He closed his eyes, and the voices of the Legends echoed in the void.
> ‚ÄúDarkness is fuel. The engine is what you have built with us.‚Äù
> 
Ren snapped his eyes open. He began to move, not as a creature of shadow, but as the heir to the Legends. He would not abandon a single lesson.
1. Martial Arts (The Vessel)
Ren shifted into a stance, the darkness trailing his movements like ink in water. He executed the Void-Step Kata. His fists tore through the air with sonic precision. He didn't rely on the darkness to strike; he used his physical mastery to deliver the darkness. Every punch was perfect mechanics; every kick was a lifetime of discipline.
 * The Drill: 10,000 strikes in the heavy gravity of the Corridor. He pushed his muscles until they tore and healed instantly under the dark influence.
2. Energy (The Flow)
He paused, bringing his hands together. He summoned his internal energy‚Äîthe pure, radiant ki he had cultivated for years. The darkness tried to snuff it out, but Ren forced them to coexist. He cycled his energy through his meridians, expanding his capacity.
 * The Result: He created a dual-core resonance. Bright energy flowing through a conduit of absolute darkness. A volatile, catastrophic mixture that only he could control.
3. Sense (The Awareness)
Ren blindfolded himself within the pitch-black Corridor. He shut down his five basic senses and expanded his Sense. He felt the microscopic shifts in the atmosphere. He sensed the intent of the chaotic energy around him before it even moved.
 * The Mastery: He reached a state of "Spherical Awareness." Nothing could enter a hundred-meter radius without him knowing its mass, velocity, and intent.
4. Will (The King‚Äôs Mind)
This was the hardest. The darkness in the Corridor whispered doubts and fears. It tried to break his sanity. Ren countered with the Will of the Legends. He projected a mental aura so dense it physically pushed the shadows back. He imposed his order upon the chaos.
 * The Decree: "I do not serve the shadow. The shadow serves me."
Embracing the Abyss
With the foundation of the Legends solidified, Ren finally allowed the darkness to fully integrate. He didn't fight it anymore; he wore it.
He extended his hand, and the Shadow Spike manifested‚Äîno longer a jagged, unstable mess, but a refined, sleek lance of compressed gravity. He practiced his new dark arts, fusing them with his martial prowess. He teleported through shadows, struck with energy-infused dark blasts, and used his amplified will to crush the space around him.
He had completed the initial dark powers. He was no longer a martial artist with a dark trick. He was a complete anomaly.
The Final Silence
The day before departure.
Ren stepped out of the Corridor of Darkness. He returned to the physical world, to a quiet cliffside overlooking the ocean. The storm of training was over. The violence of the Corridor was gone.
Now, there was only Stillness.
He sat cross-legged on the grass, mimicking the final state of the greatest warriors before a cataclysm. Just as Goku had found peace before the tournament, Ren entered a deep, restorative meditation.
He wasn't charging energy. He wasn't visualizing combat. He was completely emptying his cup.
 * Breath in: The roar of the ocean.
 * Breath out: The silence of the void.
His aura vanished. To an outsider, he would look like a normal human, completely defenseless. But beneath that tranquility lay a compressed star. He had condensed the Martial Arts, the Energy, the Sense, the Will, and the infinite potential of the Darkness into a singular point of calm.
He sat there for twenty-four hours, unmoving, unworried.
When the sun rose on the day of departure, Ren opened his eyes. They were clear, devoid of anxiety, and terrifyingly sharp.
"It's time."

Here is Chapter 12.
Chapter 12: The Path of the Lone Wolf
The sky was a bruised purple, hanging low over the town of Kuoh. It was that fragile hour between night and dawn, where the world holds its breath.
Ren stood at the gates of the Hyoudou residence. He wore a high-collared dark coat, the hem brushing his ankles, and a single bag slung over one shoulder. He didn't look back at the house. He didn't need to. He had memorized every laugh, every perverted joke, and every moment of warmth shared within those walls.
He was leaving. Not as a traitor, and not as an exile. He was leaving as a seeker.
The Silent Departure
He took a step forward, his boots crunching softly on the asphalt.
"You were really just going to leave without saying a word?"
The voice cut through the morning mist. Ren stopped, but he didn't turn around immediately. He knew that voice. It was the erratic, passionate heartbeat of the group.
Issei Hyoudou.
Ren turned his head slightly, looking over his shoulder. Issei was standing at the front door, messy hair, still in his pajamas, but his eyes were wide awake. Behind him, leaning against the doorframe with crossed arms and a somber expression, was Rias Gremory.
"It‚Äôs not a goodbye, Issei," Ren said, his voice calm, carrying the weight of the meditation he had just completed. "Goodbyes imply the end. This is just... a change in trajectory."
Issei clenched his fists. "But why? We're a team! The Rating Games, the Fallen Angels‚Äîwe can fight them together! You don't have to do this alone."
The Calling
Ren fully turned to face them. The wind picked up, blowing dust across the street, but Ren stood immovable, like a statue rooted in the earth.
"That is exactly why I have to go," Ren replied. He looked at his own hand, clenching it into a fist. The air around it shimmered, a subtle distortion of space caused by the sheer density of his energy. "I‚Äôve reached a ceiling here, Issei. The peace of this town... it softens me. The Legends I follow, the Will I carry‚Äîthey demand a storm."
He looked Issei in the eye, a small, genuine smile touching his lips‚Äîa rare expression that softened his sharp features.
"You have your path, the path of the Red Dragon Emperor. You draw strength from your friends, from your desires. That is your power." Ren tapped his own chest. "My path is solitary. To master the Darkness, to truly honor the Martial Arts and the Sense... I need to walk the wasteland. I need to go where there is no safety net."
Rias stepped forward, her crimson hair flowing in the wind. She didn't look angry. She looked proud.
"You‚Äôve outgrown the board, haven't you?" Rias asked softly.
"I'm not a piece to be played anymore, Rias," Ren said respectfully. "I'm the player."
The Bonds That Remain
"What about the guys?" Issei asked, his voice cracking slightly. "Matsuda and Motohama? They're gonna cry like babies when they find out their 'Master' is gone."
Ren chuckled, a low sound. "Tell the Trio not to slack off. If I come back and they haven't improved their... research... I'll be disappointed. They are my friends. That doesn't change just because I'm not sitting in a classroom."
He walked over to Issei. The distance closed in an instant‚Äînot a teleport, but a step of pure efficiency. Ren raised his hand.
Issei hesitated, then raised his own. They bumped fists.
A shockwave of pressure rattled the windows nearby. It wasn't an attack; it was the silent clash of two massive potentials acknowledging each other.
"Don't die," Issei said.
"I don't plan to," Ren answered. He looked at Rias and nodded. "Take care of him, President."
"Take care of yourself, Ren," Rias replied, bowing her head slightly‚Äîa gesture of respect from a King to an equal.
Into the Horizon
Ren turned his back to them. He adjusted the strap of his bag. The sun was just beginning to crack the horizon, casting a long, stretching shadow in front of him.
"Ren!" Issei shouted one last time. "When will you come back?"
Ren didn't stop walking. He raised his left hand, waving casually without looking back‚Äîthe universal sign of a wanderer who knows exactly where he is going.
"When the storm settles," Ren called back, his voice fading into the distance. "Or when you need me to save the world. Whichever comes first."
He walked down the empty road, the silhouette of a warrior fading into the morning light. He had the Corridor of Darkness waiting in the palm of his hand, and the teachings of the Legends in his soul.
The school life was over. The Legend had begun.

Here is the alternative Chapter 12. This version leans heavily into the tragedy of Ren's character arc‚Äîthe realization that his burden of knowledge and his necessary embrace of darkness make him incompatible with the peaceful days he fought to protect.
Chapter 12: The Shadow That Doesn't Belong
The Gremory household was alive with the sound of glass clinking and laughter. The rescue mission was a success. Rias was smiling, Akeno was teasing Issei, and the Perverted Trio‚ÄîMatsuda and Motohama having crashed the party‚Äîwere crying tears of joy over the high-class food.
It was a picture-perfect "Happy Ending."
Ren stood on the balcony, the sliding glass door shut behind him, muffling the warmth of the party inside. He held a glass of water in his hand, but he wasn't drinking. He was watching the reflection in the glass.
His eyes. They looked older than they should.
From Chapter 1, he had known this world was dangerous. He had trained until his bones cracked. He had adopted the Legends. But with every chapter, with every victory, the weight got heavier. The "Tragedy" wasn't that he lost fights; it was that he was losing his ability to relate to the peace he was fighting for.
Inside, Issei was doing a ridiculous dance with Asia. They looked so innocent.
Ren looked at his hand. The faint, black residue of the Corridor of Darkness (from Chapter 11) still clung to his fingertips. It was cold. It was violent. It was necessary.
"I don't fit in that frame anymore," Ren whispered to the night air.
The Decision
He didn't pack a bag. He didn't need clothes where he was going. He only needed his Will.
He slid the door open just an inch. He could hear Issei shouting, "Ren! Get in here! President Rias is opening the expensive vintage!"
Ren smiled, a genuine, painful smile. "Enjoy it, Issei. You earned it."
He closed the door. He didn't go back inside. He vaulted over the balcony railing, landing silently in the garden two stories below.
The Interception
He made it to the edge of the town, walking the same path Sasuke once walked when leaving Konoha. The moon was full, casting long, judgmental shadows.
"So, this is it?"
Ren stopped. He didn't need to use his Sense to know who it was. Rias Gremory stood under a streetlamp, her arms crossed. Issei was beside her, panting slightly, looking confused and hurt.
"You're leaving in the middle of your own victory party?" Issei asked, his voice trembling. "Ren, stop messing around. Come back inside."
Ren turned slowly. He didn't put on a mask of indifference. He let them see the exhaustion in his eyes.
"It wasn't my victory, Issei. It was yours," Ren said quietly. "I was just the mechanism that ensured it."
"Don't give me that crap!" Issei stepped forward, angry tears in his eyes. "We're friends! We're the Perverted Trio plus one! We're the ORC! You‚Äôre one of us!"
"I am," Ren admitted, and the admission hurt more than a denial. "And that is why I have to go."
The Tragedy of the Strong
Ren looked up at the moon. "Do you remember when we started? I told myself I‚Äôd just get strong enough to survive. But look at me now."
He raised his hand, and for a split second, the atmosphere crushed down on them‚Äîa glimpse of the murderous intent and darkness he had cultivated in Chapter 11. Issei flinched instinctively. Rias‚Äôs eyes widened.
"My path... it's getting darker, Issei," Ren said, lowering his hand. "To protect you, to protect this town, I had to become something that doesn't belong at a dinner table. I had to embrace the Corridor of Darkness. If I stay, that darkness will bleed into your lives. I‚Äôll become a danger to the very peace I‚Äôm trying to uphold."
"We don't care!" Issei yelled. "We can take it!"
"I know you can," Ren said softy. "But I can't watch you try."
He looked at Rias. "President. You need a Pawn who can stand in the light and inspire hope. That‚Äôs Issei. But you also need a monster who can walk into the abyss and kill the threats before they ever reach you. That‚Äôs me."
The Departure
Ren turned his back on them. The wind picked up, blowing his coat around him like a shroud.
"Ren!" Issei moved to grab him.
Ren didn't attack. He didn't dodge. He simply flared his Will‚Äînot to hurt, but to push. An invisible wall of sheer pressure gently but firmly stopped Issei in his tracks. It was the gap in their power, laid bare.
"Don't follow me," Ren said. His voice cracked, just for a second. "Let me keep the memory of you guys smiling. If you follow me where I'm going... you won't be smiling anymore."
"Ren..." Issei whispered, realizing for the first time the sheer magnitude of the burden his friend had been carrying alone since the beginning.
Ren looked over his shoulder one last time. He memorized their faces. The sadness, the confusion, the love.
"Thank you," Ren said.
He stepped forward, and the shadows on the ground surged up, swallowing him whole. He didn't walk away; he sank into the darkness he had mastered, vanishing from the street, from the town, and from their lives.
The streetlamp flickered. He was gone.

Chapter 12: The Ceiling of Effort
The victory party at the Hyoudou residence was loud.
"Cheers to the Red Dragon Emperor!" Matsuda roared, raising a soda.
"Cheers!" the club shouted back.
Ren sat on the sofa, a bandage wrapped around his left forearm‚Äîa souvenir from the rescue mission. He held his cup, but he didn't drink. He watched Issei.
Issei was laughing, scratching the back of his head while Rias and Akeno fussed over him. Just hours ago, Ren had watched Issei trigger the Boosted Gear. He had felt that power. It was raw, unrefined, and clumsy... but it was infinite.
Ren looked down at his own hand. It was calloused from thousands of strikes. It was scarred from the Corridor of Darkness.
I calculated every move, Ren thought, the bitterness rising like bile in his throat. I utilized the Legends. I planned the tactics. I risked my soul dipping into the darkness just to secure an opening.
And yet, the MVP was Issei. Not because of skill. Not because of Will. But because he was chosen.
Effort was losing to Destiny.
The Suffocating Light
Ren stood up. The noise of the party suddenly felt deafening. It wasn't jealousy‚Äînot exactly. It was a terrifying realization of his own irrelevance. If he stayed here, standing next to a Dragon, he would become nothing more than a spectator. A footnote. "The guy who tries hard."
"Ren? Where are you going?" Issei asked, noticing movement. "The pizza is getting here soon!"
"I need air," Ren said. His voice was too flat. Too controlled.
He walked out the front door, the cool night air hitting his face. He didn't stop at the porch. He kept walking. He went to the small park nearby, the one where they used to spy on girls. He sat on the swing, clutching the chains until the metal groaned.
"Dammit," he whispered.
He punched the sand.
Martial Arts.
He punched again.
Energy.
Again.
Sense.
"It's not enough," he hissed, his eyes burning. "The Legends... they are perfect. But I am not. My container is too small."
The Confrontation
"I knew I'd find you here."
Ren froze. Issei walked into the park, looking unusually serious. He wasn't the pervert right now; he was a friend who sensed something was wrong.
"You've been weird all night," Issei said, stopping a few feet away. "We won, Ren. We saved them. Why do you look like you lost?"
Ren stared at the ground. "You doubled your power in an instant today, Issei. How did you do it?"
Issei blinked, taken aback. "I dunno. I just... I wanted to protect everyone. I got mad, and the gauntlet just responded! It went BOOM, you know?"
Ren let out a hollow, dry laugh. He stood up slowly.
"You just got mad," Ren repeated. "I have meditated for three years. I have broken my bones to harden them. I have studied the flow of ki until my eyes bled. And you... you just got mad."
Issei stepped back, sensing the volatility in Ren's aura. "Ren, what's your point? We're on the same side. My power is your power!"
"NO!"
Ren snapped. His aura flared‚Äînot the golden light of a hero, but the erratic, violet-tinged blackness of the Corridor.
"That is the problem, Issei! I don't want to be carried by you! I don't want to be the 'smart friend' who hides behind the Dragon when the real monsters show up!"
Ren pointed a trembling finger at Issei. "I love you, brother. But looking at you... it kills me. It makes me feel like everything I've done‚Äîevery drop of sweat, every sacrifice‚Äîis a joke compared to your destiny."
The Hard Truth
Silence stretched between them. Issei looked hurt, but for the first time, he seemed to understand the massive chip on Ren's shoulder.
"So you're leaving," Issei said quietly.
"I have to," Ren replied, his voice steadying, the outburst fading into cold resolve. "If I stay in your light, I will never grow. I will just be your shadow. And eventually, I will resent you."
Ren turned away, looking toward the treeline where the shadows were deepest.
"I found a way, Issei. A place where 'Destiny' doesn't matter. A place where only Will survives." He was talking about the Corridor of Darkness. "It‚Äôs dangerous. It might kill me. But it‚Äôs the only way I can bridge the gap between a Human and a Dragon."
"You're my best friend," Issei said, his voice cracking. "You don't have to be the strongest. Just be here."
Ren closed his eyes. That was the temptation. To settle. To be safe.
"The Legends didn't settle," Ren whispered.
He turned back one last time. He didn't offer a fist bump. He didn't smile. He looked at Issei with the eyes of a rival.
"Next time we meet, Issei... I won't be the tactician. And I won't be the support."
Ren‚Äôs figure began to distort. He wasn't using a magic circle; he was forcefully tearing a hole in space using the darkness he had practiced in Chapter 11. The Corridor was hungry, and it pulled him in.
"Next time," Ren‚Äôs voice echoed as he vanished into the void, "I will be the one who stands in front."
The Void
The park was empty. Issei stood alone under the swings.
He looked at his hand‚Äîthe hand that held the Boosted Gear. For the first time, he didn't feel cool. He felt the weight of what his "gift" had cost him.
He clenched his fist. "I won't lose either, Ren."
Ren plummeted through the darkness. No sensory input. No light. Just the crushing pressure of the Corridor.
He didn't panic. He smiled.
Here, there were no chosen ones. Here, there were no Dragons. There was only the darkness, and the man crazy enough to try and tame it.
"Let's begin."

Chapter 11: The Weight of a Human Soul
The adrenaline of the rescue had faded. Now, there was only the ache in his bones.
Ren sat on the edge of his bed in the Hyoudou household guest room. His torso was wrapped in gauze. His knuckles were bruised violet. While Asia had healed the worst of the cuts, his internal energy‚Äîhis Ki‚Äîwas dangerously low.
Downstairs, he could hear laughter. Issei, Matsuda, and Motohama were celebrating. They were loud, vibrant, and alive.
Ren looked at his hands. They were shaking.
During the fight, he had executed a perfect tactical feint. He had read the Fallen Angel's movements using his Sense. He had applied maximum Will to force his body past its limits. He had struck with perfect Martial Arts form.
And the result? He had barely scratched the enemy.
Then Issei, with zero training, zero discipline, and zero tactical awareness, had simply gotten angry. The Boosted Gear responded, and raw power obliterated the threat.
0 x Infinity is still 0.
1 x Infinity is Infinity.
Ren realized he was the zero. No matter how much he multiplied his effort, he was fighting a mathematical impossibility.
The Stagnation of the Legends
Ren stood up, ignoring the protest of his bruised ribs. He needed to move. He couldn't sit still while the gap widened.
He slipped out of the house and went to the backyard. The moon was high.
He began his forms.
 * Martial Arts: He moved through the Void-Step kata. His form was flawless. A master would weep at the perfection. But Ren scowled. Too slow. Against a devil's speed, "perfect" was slow.
 * Energy: He gathered his Ki. It was a warm, golden light. It was pure. But it was a candle flame compared to the roaring bonfire of Issei's Dragon energy. Too weak.
 * Sense: He expanded his awareness. He could hear the heartbeat of a cat two blocks away. But during the fight, knowing the attack was coming didn't matter if he was too slow to dodge it effectively.
He sped up. He pushed his body harder. Sweat stung his eyes.
Faster. Stronger. More.
He visualized the legends.
Ryu‚Äôs discipline.
Goku‚Äôs drive.
Batman‚Äôs preparation.
He channeled them all. He threw a punch with everything he had‚Äîa strike meant to shatter stone.
CRACK.
It wasn't the stone that broke. It was his wrist.
Ren fell to his knees, clutching his arm. He didn't scream. He just stared at the limb, hanging limp. The vibration of his own power was too much for his human frame.
"The vessel is too weak," he whispered to the grass.
The Realization
He sat there for a long time, the pain in his wrist a dull throb.
He remembered the DxD world's reality. It wasn't fair. Devils lived for thousands of years. Dragons were born with world-ending power. Humans? Humans were fragile. They were designed to be protected, not to fight.
Ren had hit the Human Ceiling.
If he stayed here, doing the same push-ups, the same meditation, the same sparring, he would peak. In a year, Issei would be fighting gods. Ren would be fighting to stay relevant against foot soldiers.
He would become a liability. A mascot. "Issei's human friend who tries hard."
The thought made him nauseous.
The Forbidden Door
Ren closed his eyes and looked inward. Deep in the recesses of his mind, past the bright lights of his Ki, there was a shadow he had always ignored.
The Dark Hado. The Satsui no Hado. The Abyssal energy.
The Legends warned against it. It corrupted the mind. It destroyed the body. It was the path of the Ashura.
But it was also the only thing that could shatter the ceiling.
He needed a catalyst. He couldn't train this in a backyard. If he lost control here, he would kill Issei. He would kill the Trio. He would destroy the town.
He needed a place where the darkness was absolute. A place where he could tear his humanity apart and rebuild it into something that could hold the power of a Legend.
He recalled an obscure occult text he had read in the ORC clubroom‚Äîa mention of a dimensional rift, a "Corridor of Darkness," located in a cursed zone far from civilization. It was a graveyard for lost souls, a place of high gravity and mental torture.
Devils avoided it. Humans died instantly in it.
"Perfect," Ren muttered.
He stood up. He used his remaining Ki to stabilize his broken wrist. The pain was sharp, grounding him.
He looked back at the house. The lights were warm. Issei‚Äôs laughter floated out the window. It was a beautiful sound. A sound Ren wanted to protect.
But he couldn't protect it with these hands.
He had to leave. He had to throw away his safety, his comfort, and his sanity. He had to go to the Corridor. And he couldn't tell them why, because they would stop him. They would tell him "it's okay to be weak."
Ren clenched his good fist.
"It is not okay."
Chapter 11 ends with Ren‚Äôs resolve hardening, fueled by his inferiority complex and the crushing reality of his limitations.

Chapter 11: The Death of the Butler

1. The Embrace of the Shadow

The air imploded. A perfect circle of vacuum formed, twisting the wallpaper without touching it.
Ren: "Good. Kinetic force amplified by negative pressure."
The Sense (The Haki/Ki):
He closed his eyes. The Darkness was loud, screaming at him to destroy.
He used the discipline of the Turtle School. He breathed.
Inhale. Accept the Envy.
Exhale. Control the Void.
He expanded his senses. He could feel the rats in the walls. He could feel Issei sleeping three blocks away.
Ren: "I don't need to see. The Darkness touches everything."
3. The Final Meditation (Goku Style)
Sweating, exhausted, but mentally clear, Ren sat back down in the lotus position.
This was the Buu Saga Meditation. The moment of absolute stillness before the final tournament.
He wasn't gathering energy. He was "Image Training" in his mind.
Inside his mind:
He fought Issei. He fought Kiba. He fought Rias.
He visualized every counter. Every parry.
He visualized the Corridor of Darkness.
Ren (Internal): I am ready. I have the technique of the masters and the power of the villain. I am no longer an NPC.
He opened his eyes. They were pitch black for a second, then returned to normal.
Ren: "Time to go."

üåë Chapter 12: The Valley of the End (The Departure)
Timeline: The Next Day (After the Victory Party).
Location: The Old School Building (Clubroom).
1. The Celebration
The clubroom was loud. Issei was the center of the universe, swathed in bandages but beaming.
Ren stood by the window. He had changed out of his school uniform. He was wearing the Black Coat (Organization XIII style) he had sewn himself, reinforcing the fabric with shadow threads during his meditation.
Issei: "Ren! Dude! Did you see me punch him?! And you! You took out the rook! We're unstoppable!"
Issei ran over, arm extended for a high-five.
Ren didn't raise his hand.
He looked at Issei. The training from last night kept his face calm, his posture rooted.
Ren: "You're unstoppable, Issei. I'm just... stuck."
2. The Veritas (Truth)
The room quieted down. Rias sensed the shift in the air‚Äîthe distinct chill of the Void.
Rias: "Ren-kun? Is something wrong?"
Ren turned to them. His eyes were clear. Brutally honest.
Ren: "I'm leaving, Rias. I'm dropping out of school. I'm quitting the club."
Issei: "What? Why? We just won!"
Ren: "You won. I survived."
Ren pulled up his sleeve. His arm was black‚Äînecrosis mixed with solidified shadow.
Ren: "This world... this 'Light' you fight for... it's killing me. I can't save anyone without destroying myself."
He raised his hand to the empty air.
Ren: "I'm done being the side character in your harem anime, Issei. I want to be the Protagonist of my own story. Even if it's a tragedy."
He clawed the air.
RIIIIIIP.
Reality tore open. A swirling vortex of purple and black energy appeared. The Corridor of Darkness.
3. The Confrontation (Sasuke Style)
Issei: "Stop! That thing looks dangerous! You'll die in there!"
Rias: "Ren! I order you to stand down! That is forbidden magic!"
Ren stepped toward the portal.
Issei: "Don't make me do this, Ren!"
Issei activated his Gauntlet. [BOOST!]
Kiba drew a sword. Koneko took a stance.
They charged. Not to kill, but to restrain.
Ren didn't panic. He remembered his meditation.
Ren: "Too slow. Too bright."
[Technique: Eclipsing Zone]
Ren stomped. The room plunged into absolute darkness. No light. No sound.
Issei: "I can't see! Ren!"
Ren moved through the dark using Void Steps. He appeared behind Koneko.
He placed a hand on her back. [Gravity Well].
She slammed into the floor, pinned by 10x gravity.
Ren: "Stay down, Rook. Your strength means nothing if you can't stand."
Kiba slashed blindly. Ren caught the blade‚Äînot with magic, but with a precision pinch catch he had visualized a thousand times.
Ren: "Sloppy."
Ren kicked Kiba in the chest using the Garp Style impact. Kiba flew back.
Issei: "REN!"
Issei flared his Dragon Aura, burning away the darkness.
He saw Ren standing at the portal's edge.
Issei: "Why?! We're friends!"
Ren: "That's why I have to leave. Because if I stay... I'll start hating you. And I don't want to hate you, Issei."
4. The Clash of Ideals
Issei charged. He threw a punch.
Ren summoned a weapon for the first time. He pulled the darkness from the air. It crystallized into a jagged, reverse-blade sword.
[Weapon: Soul Eater (Prototype)]
CLANG.
Ren parried the Dragon Fist. The impact shook the building.
Ren slid back, his feet dragging on the floor. He was physically weaker, but his Technique bridged the gap.
Ren: "You have the Red Dragon. I have the Void. Let's see which one goes deeper."
He blasted Issei with a wave of pure Repulsion. Issei was thrown back, skidding across the floor.
5. The Exit
Ren stood in the portal. The winds of the Void whipped his coat.
He looked back one last time. He looked at Rias, Asia, and Issei. He didn't look like a monster. He looked like a martial artist who had just finished his final spar.
Ren: "Goodbye, Issei. Become the Harem King."
Issei: (Reaching out, tears in his eyes) "REN!"
Ren: "I'm going to find the Kingdom... where the Heart is True."
He stepped back. The darkness swallowed him.
The rift snapped shut.
The room was silent. The party decorations fluttered in the wind.
Ren Nocturnus Veritas was gone.
[Route B - The Dark Seeker: Demo Complete]

Finally, add in chapter 11 what happen if Ren access the corridor of darkness for training to make sure he can defeat everyone during the chapter 12 departure including Rias and Akeno? Should Asia also fight? If not, that's logical but if you have other ideas.

This is a crucial addition. To make it believable that a human (even a darkness-enhanced one) can hold off the entire Gremory Peerage‚Äîincluding two High-Class Devils (Rias and Akeno)‚ÄîRen needs a "Hyperbolic Time Chamber" moment.

Regarding **Asia**: You are correct. It is **illogical** for Asia to fight physically. She has no offensive magic and her nature is pacifistic.
* **However:** She is Ren's greatest weakness. Her "attack" should be emotional. While everyone else attacks his body, Asia attacks his *resolve* by trying to heal him or begging him to stay. Ren has to "defeat" her by rejecting her kindness, which hurts him more than any punch.

Here is the revised **Chapter 11 (The Void Training)** and the expanded **Chapter 12 (The Grand Exit)**.
